day, January 30), 1992 with an amendment and an amendment to the title
HR 4210 RS

102d CONGRESS

H.R. 4210

IN THE SENATE OF THE UNITED STATES

Received; read twice and referred to the Committee on Finance

Reported under the authority of the order of the Senate of March 5 (legislative
day, January 30), 1992 by Mr. BENTSEN, with an amendment and an amendment
to the title
[Strike out all after the enacting clause and insert the part printed
in italic]
AN ACT
To amend the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 to provide incentives for increased
economic growth and to provide tax relief for families.
  Be it enacted by the Senate and House of Representatives of the United
  States of America in Congress assembled,
 [Struck out->] SECTION 1. SHORT TITLE, ETC. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) SHORT TITLE- This Act may be cited as the `Tax Fairness
 and Economic Growth Act of 1992'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) AMENDMENT OF 1986 CODE- Except as otherwise expressly
 provided, whenever in this Act an amendment or repeal is expressed in
 terms of an amendment to, or repeal of, a section or other provision, the
 reference shall be considered to be made to a section or other provision
 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) SECTION 15 NOT TO APPLY- No amendment made by this Act
 shall be treated as a change in a rate of tax for purposes of section 15
 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (d) UNDERPAYMENT OF ESTIMATED TAX- No addition to tax
 shall be made under section 6654 or 6655 of the Internal Revenue Code of
 1986 for any period before April 16, 1993 (March 16, 1993, in the case of
 a taxpayer subject to such section 6655) with respect to any underpayment
 to the extent such underpayment was created or increased by any amendment
 made by this Act. The preceding sentence shall not apply to the amendments
 made by section 3101. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] TITLE I--MIDDLE CLASS TAX RELIEF [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 1001. CREDIT FOR PORTION OF SOCIAL SECURITY
 TAXES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Subpart C of part IV of subchapter A
 of chapter 1 (relating to refundable credits) is amended by redesignating
 section 35 as section 36 and by inserting after section 34 the following
 new section: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 35. CREDIT FOR PORTION OF SOCIAL SECURITY
 TAXES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) ALLOWANCE OF CREDIT- In the case of an individual,
 there shall be allowed as a credit against the tax imposed by this subtitle
 for the taxable year an amount equal to 20 percent of the taxpayer's social
 security taxes for the taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) LIMITATION- The amount of the credit allowable under
 subsection (a) to any taxpayer for any taxable year shall not exceed $200
 ($400 in the case of a joint return). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) SOCIAL SECURITY TAXES- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The term `social security taxes' means,
 with respect to any taxpayer for any taxable year-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the amount of the taxes imposed by subsections (a)
 and (b) of section 3101 on amounts received by the taxpayer during the
 calendar year in which the taxable year begins, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the amount of the taxes imposed by section 3201(a)
 on amounts received by the taxpayer during the calendar year in which the
 taxable year begins, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) 50 percent of the taxes imposed by subsections (a)
 and (b) of section 1401 on the self-employment income of the taxpayer for
 the taxable year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) 50 percent of the taxes imposed by section 3211(a)(1)
 on amounts received by the taxpayer during the calendar year in which the
 taxable year begins. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) COORDINATION WITH SPECIAL REFUND OF SOCIAL SECURITY
 TAXES- The term `social security taxes' shall not include any taxes to the
 extent the taxpayer is entitled to a special refund of such taxes under
 section 6413(c). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) SPECIAL RULE- Any amounts paid pursuant to an agreement
 under section 3121(l) (relating to agreements entered into by American
 employers with respect to foreign affiliates) which are equivalent to the
 taxes referred to in paragraph (1)(A) shall be treated as taxes referred
 to in such paragraph. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) YEARS TO WHICH SECTION APPLIES- This section shall
 only apply to taxable years beginning after December 31, 1991, and before
 January 1, 1994.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CLERICAL AMENDMENT- The table of sections for subpart
 C of part IV of subchapter A of chapter 1 is amended by striking the item
 relating to section 35 and inserting the following: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 35. Credit for portion of social security
 taxes. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 36. Overpayments of tax.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to taxable years beginning after December 31, 1991. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 1002. CREDIT FOR INTEREST ON EDUCATION LOANS. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Subpart A of part IV of subchapter A
 of chapter 1 (relating to nonrefundable personal credits) is amended by
 inserting after section 22 the following new section: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 23. INTEREST ON EDUCATION LOANS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) ALLOWANCE OF CREDIT- In the case of an individual,
 there shall be allowed as a credit against the tax imposed by this chapter for
 the taxable year an amount equal to 15 percent of the interest paid by the
 taxpayer during the taxable year on any qualified education loan. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) MAXIMUM CREDIT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The credit allowed by subsection (a)
 for the taxable year shall not exceed $300 with respect to each individual
 whose qualified higher education expenses were financed by any qualified
 education loan to which such interest relates. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) HIGHER LIMIT FOR TAXPAYERS WITH LARGE AMOUNTS OF
 EDUCATION LOAN INTEREST-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If the taxpayer's education loan interest
 percentage for the taxable year is at least 10 percent, paragraph (1)
 shall be applied by substituting the higher limit for `$300', determined
 in accordance with the following table: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   If the education loan [<-Struck out]
-- [Struck out->] The higher [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]    interest percentage is: [<-Struck out]
-- [Struck out->] limit is: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]  At least 10 but less than 11 [<-Struck out]
-- [Struck out->] $350   [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]  At least 11 but less than 12 [<-Struck out]
-- [Struck out->] 400   [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]  At least 12 but less than 13 [<-Struck out]
-- [Struck out->] 450   [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]  At least 13 [<-Struck out]
-- [Struck out->] 500.   [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) EDUCATION LOAN INTEREST PERCENTAGE- For purposes of
 subparagraph (A), the taxpayer's education loan interest percentage is the
 percentage which the amount of interest paid by the taxpayer during the
 taxable year on qualified education loans bears to the taxpayer's modified
 adjusted gross income for such year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) PHASEOUT OF BENEFIT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If the modified adjusted gross income of
 the taxpayer for the taxable year exceeds the applicable limit, the dollar
 limitation otherwise applicable under this subsection for the taxable year
 shall be reduced (but not below zero) by the amount which bears the same
 ratio to such limit as such excess bears to $25,000 ($12,500 in the case
 of a married individual filing a separate return). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) APPLICABLE DOLLAR AMOUNT WHERE PARENT OF STUDENT
 CLAIMING CREDIT- For purposes of subparagraph (A), if the qualified education
 loan was used to pay the qualified higher education expenses of an individual
 other than the taxpayer or his spouse, the applicable dollar amount is--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) $45,000, in the case of a return of an unmarried
 individual, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) $75,000, in the case of a joint return, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) $37,500 in the case of a married individual filing
 a separate return. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) APPLICABLE DOLLAR AMOUNT WHERE STUDENT OR FORMER
 STUDENT CLAIMING CREDIT- For purposes of subparagraph (A), if the qualified
 education loan was used to pay the qualified higher education expenses of
 the taxpayer or his spouse, the applicable dollar amount is-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) $30,000, in the case of a return of an unmarried
 individual, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) $50,000, in the case of a joint return, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) $25,000 in the case of a married individual filing
 a separate return. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) CREDIT NOT TO EXCEED TAX ON EARNED INCOME FOR TAXPAYERS
 UNDER AGE 23- If the taxpayer has not attained age 23 (or, in the case of a
 joint return, if neither the husband or wife have attained age 23) before
 the close of the calendar year ending with or within the taxable year,
 the credit allowed by subsection (a) for such taxable year shall not exceed
 the amount equal to the percentage of the taxpayer's regular tax liability
 for such taxable year which is the same as the percentage of the taxpayer's
 modified adjusted gross income for such taxable year which is attributable
 to earned income (as defined in section 911(d)(2)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) LIMITATIONS ON TAXPAYERS ELIGIBLE FOR CREDIT-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) CREDIT ALLOWED TO TAXPAYER ONLY IF NOT CLAIMED AS
 PERSONAL EXEMPTION BY ANOTHER TAXPAYER- No credit shall be allowed by this
 section to an individual for the taxable year if a deduction under section
 151 with respect to such individual is allowed to another taxpayer for
 the taxable year beginning in the calendar year in which such individual's
 taxable year begins. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CREDIT ALLOWED TO PARENT, ETC. ONLY IF DEPENDENT
 IS STUDENT AND PERSONAL EXEMPTION CLAIMED FOR DEPENDENT- If the qualified
 education loan was used to pay the qualified higher education expenses of
 an individual other than the taxpayer or his spouse, no credit shall be
 allowed by this section for the taxable year with respect to interest on
 such loan unless-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) a deduction under section 151 with respect to
 such individual is allowed to the taxpayer for such taxable year, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such individual is at least a half-time student with
 respect to such taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) LIMIT ON PERIOD CREDIT ALLOWED-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- In the case of a qualified education loan
 used to pay the qualified higher education expenses of the taxpayer or his
 spouse, no credit shall be allowed by this section for any taxable year
 after the first 5 taxable years (whether or not consecutive) with respect
 to which the taxpayer or his spouse (as the case may be) is not at least
 a half-time student. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) PERIODS OF INTEREST DEFERRAL NOT COUNTED- For purposes
 of paragraph (1), an individual shall be treated as a half-time student during
 any period during which payment of interest on any qualified education loan
 is deferred under Federal or State law. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) DEFINITIONS- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) QUALIFIED EDUCATION LOAN- The term `qualified education
 loan' means any indebtedness incurred to pay qualified higher education
 expenses-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) which are paid or incurred within a reasonable period
 of time before or after the indebtedness is incurred, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) which are attributable to education furnished during a
 period during which the recipient was at least a half-time student. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->] Such term includes indebtedness used to refinance
 indebtedness which qualifies as a qualified education loan. The term
 `qualified education loan' shall not include any indebtedness owed to a
 person who is related (within the meaning of section 267(b) or 707(b)(1))
 to the taxpayer. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) QUALIFIED HIGHER EDUCATION EXPENSES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The term `qualified higher education
 expenses' means qualified tuition and related expenses of the taxpayer, his
 spouse, or a dependent for attendance at an eligible educational institution
 (as defined in section 135(c)(3)), reduced by the amount excluded from
 gross income under section 135 by reason of such expenses. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) QUALIFIED TUITION AND RELATED EXPENSES- The term
 `qualified tuition and related expenses' has the meaning given such term by
 section 117(b), except that such term shall include any reasonable living
 expenses while away from home. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) MODIFIED ADJUSTED GROSS INCOME- The term `modified
 adjusted gross income' has the meaning given to such term by section
 86(b)(2). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) HALF-TIME STUDENT- The term `half-time student' means
 any individual who would be a student as defined in section 151(c)(4) if
 `half-time' were substituted for `full-time' each place it appears in such
 section. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) DEPENDENT- The term `dependent' has the meaning given
 such term by section 152. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) SPECIAL RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) CARRYOVER- If the amount of interest which may be
 taken into account by the taxpayer under subsection (a) for the taxable
 year exceeds the amount necessary to produce the maximum credit under this
 section for such year, such excess shall be treated as interest paid by
 the taxpayer during the succeeding taxable year on a qualified education
 loan. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) DENIAL OF DOUBLE BENEFIT- No credit shall be allowed
 under this section for any amount for which a deduction is allowable under
 any other provision of this chapter. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) MARITAL STATUS- Marital status shall be determined
 in accordance with section 7703. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(g) CARRYOVER OF UNUSED CREDIT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the credit allowable under subsection (a) for any
 taxable year after the application of subsections (b), (c), and (d) exceeds
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the limitation imposed by section 26(a) for such
 taxable year reduced by the sum of the credits allowable under sections 21,
 22, and 25, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] such excess shall be carried to the succeeding taxable year
 and shall be allowable under subsection (a) for such succeeding taxable
 year. The limitations of subsections (b), (c), and (d) shall not apply
 to the amount allowable in any succeeding taxable year by reason of the
 preceding sentence. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) 5-YEAR LIMIT ON CARRYFORWARD- No amount may be carried
 under paragraph (1) to any taxable year after the 5th taxable year for
 which the credit was originally determined.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CLERICAL AMENDMENT- The table of sections for such
 subpart A is amended by inserting after the item relating to section 22
 the following new item: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 23. Interest on education loans.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to taxable years beginning after December 31, 1991. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 1003. PENALTY-FREE WITHDRAWALS FOR FIRST HOME PURCHASE,
 HIGHER EDUCATION EXPENSES, AND MEDICAL EXPENSES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) FIRST HOME PURCHASE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Paragraph (2) of section 72(t) (relating
 to exceptions to 10-percent additional tax on early distributions from
 qualified retirement plans) is amended by adding after subparagraph (C)
 the following new subparagraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) DISTRIBUTION FROM INDIVIDUAL RETIREMENT PLAN FOR
 FIRST HOME PURCHASE- A distribution to an individual from an individual
 retirement plan with respect to which the requirements of paragraph (6)
 are met.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) DEFINITIONS- Subsection (t) of section 72 is amended
 by adding after paragraph (5) the following new paragraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(6) REQUIREMENTS APPLICABLE TO FIRST HOME PURCHASE
 DISTRIBUTION- For purposes of paragraph (2)(D)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The requirements of this paragraph are met
 with respect to a distribution if the distribution meets the requirements
 of clauses (i), (ii), and (iii). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) DOLLAR LIMIT- A distribution meets the requirements
 of this clause to the extent that the amount of the distribution does not
 exceed the excess (if any) of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) $10,000, over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the sum of the distributions to which paragraph
 (2)(D) previously applied with respect to the residence (whether or
 not such distributions were from the individual retirement plan of the
 owner). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) USE OF DISTRIBUTION- A distribution meets the
 requirements of this clause if the distribution-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) is made to or on behalf of a qualified first home
 purchaser, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) is applied within 60 days of the date of
 distribution to the purchase or construction of a principal residence of
 such purchaser. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) ELIGIBLE PLANS- A distribution meets the requirements
 of this clause if the distribution is not made from an individual retirement
 plan-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) which is an inherited individual retirement plan
 (within the meaning of section 408(d)(3)(C)(ii)), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) any part of the contributions to which were
 excludable from income under section 402(a)(5), 402(a)(7), 403(a)(4),
 or 403(b)(8). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) QUALIFIED FIRST HOME PURCHASER- For purposes of this
 paragraph, the term `qualified first home purchaser' means the individual
 who is the owner of the individual retirement plan or who is a child (as
 defined in section 151(c)(3)) of such owner, but only if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) such individual (and, if married, such individual's
 spouse) had no present ownership interest in a residence at any time within
 the 36-month period ending on the date on which the distribution is applied
 pursuant to subparagraph (A)(ii), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) subsection (h) or (k) of section 1034 did not suspend
 the running of any period of time specified in section 1034 with respect
 to such individual on the day before the date the distribution is applied
 pursuant to subparagraph (A)(ii). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SPECIAL RULE WHERE DELAY IN ACQUISITION- If any
 distribution from an individual retirement plan fails to meet the requirements
 of subparagraph (A) solely by reason of a delay or cancellation of the
 purchase or construction of the residence, the amount of the distribution
 may be contributed to an individual retirement plan as provided in section
 408(d)(3)(A)(i) (determined by substituting `120 days' for `60 days' in
 such section), except that-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) section 408(d)(3)(B) shall not be applied to such
 contribution, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) such amount shall not be taken into account--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) in determining whether section 408(d)(3)(A)(i)
 applies to any other amount, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) for purposes of subclause (II) of subparagraph
 (A)(i). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) PRINCIPAL RESIDENCE- For purposes of this paragraph,
 the term `principal residence' has the meaning given such term by section
 1034. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) OWNER- For purposes of this paragraph, the term `owner'
 means, with respect to any individual retirement plan, the individual with
 respect to whom such plan was established.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) EDUCATIONAL EXPENSES- Paragraph (2) of section 72(t)

 [Struck out->] SEC. 1004. MODIFICATIONS OF ONE-TIME EXCLUSION OF GAIN FROM

 [Struck out->] SEC. 1005. TREATMENT OF EMPLOYER-PROVIDED TRANSPORTATION
 BENEFITS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) EXCLUSION- Subsection (a) of section 132 (relating to

 [Struck out->]   (b) QUALIFIED TRANSPORTATION FRINGE- Section 132 is amended
 by redesignating subsections (f), (g), (h), (i), (j), and (k) as subsections
 (g), (h), (i), (j), (k), and (l), respectively, and by inserting after
 subsection (e) the following new subsection: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) QUALIFIED TRANSPORTATION FRINGE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this section, the term
 `qualified transportation fringe' means any of the following provided by
 an employer to an employee: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) Transportation in a commuter highway vehicle if such
 transportation is in connection with travel between the employee's residence
 and place of employment. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) Any transit pass. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) Qualified parking. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) LIMITATION ON EXCLUSION- The amount of the fringe
 benefits which are provided by an employer to any employee and which may
 be excluded from gross income under subsection (a)(5) shall not exceed--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) $60 per month in the case of the aggregate of the
 benefits described in subparagraphs (A) and (B) of paragraph (1), and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) $160 per month in the case of qualified
 parking. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) BENEFIT NOT IN LIEU OF COMPENSATION- Subsection (a)(5)
 shall not apply to any qualified transportation fringe unless such benefit
 is provided in addition to (and not in lieu of) any compensation otherwise
 payable to the employee. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) DEFINITIONS- For purposes of this subsection--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) TRANSIT PASS- The term `transit pass' means any
 pass, token, farecard, voucher, or similar item entitling a person to
 transportation (or transportation at a reduced price) if such transportation
 is-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) on mass transit facilities (whether or not publicly
 owned), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) provided by any person in the business of transporting
 persons for compensation or hire if such transportation is provided in a
 vehicle meeting the requirements of subparagraph (B)(i). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) COMMUTER HIGHWAY VEHICLE- The term `commuter highway
 vehicle' means any highway vehicle-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the seating capacity of which is at least 6 adults
 (not including the driver), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) at least 80 percent of the mileage use of which can
 reasonably be expected to be-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) for purposes of transporting employees in connection
 with travel between their residences and their place of employment, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) on trips during which the number of employees
 transported for such purposes is at least 1/2 of the adult seating capacity
 of such vehicle (not including the driver). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) QUALIFIED PARKING- The term `qualified parking'
 means parking provided to an employee on or near the business premises of
 the employer or on or near a location from which the employee commutes to
 work by transportation described in subparagraph (A), in a commuter highway
 vehicle, or by carpool. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) TRANSPORTATION PROVIDED BY EMPLOYER- Transportation
 referred to in paragraph (1)(A) shall be considered to be provided by an
 employer if such transportation is furnished in a commuter highway vehicle
 operated by or for the employer. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) EMPLOYEE- For purposes of this subsection, the term
 `employee' does not include an individual who is an employee within the
 meaning of section 401(c)(1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) COORDINATION WITH OTHER PROVISIONS- For purposes of
 this section, the terms `working condition fringe' and `de minimis fringe'
 shall not include any qualified transportation fringe (determined without
 regard to paragraph (2)).' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) CONFORMING AMENDMENT- Subsection (i) of section 132
 (as redesignated by subsection (b)) is amended by striking paragraph (4)
 and redesignating the following paragraphs accordingly. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (d) EFFECTIVE DATE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- The amendments made by this section shall
 apply to benefits provided after December 31, 1991. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) PARKING LIMIT- The limitation of subparagraph (B)
 of section 132(f)(2) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 (as amended by
 this section) shall only apply to benefits provided for months beginning
 after the date of the enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 1006. EXTENSION OF DEDUCTION FOR HEALTH INSURANCE COSTS
 OF SELF-EMPLOYED INDIVIDUALS. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] SEC. 2002. SPECIAL DEPRECIATION ALLOWANCE FOR CERTAIN
 EQUIPMENT ACQUIRED IN 1992. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Section 168 (relating to accelerated cost
 recovery system) is amended by adding at the end the following new subsection:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(j) SPECIAL ALLOWANCE FOR CERTAIN EQUIPMENT ACQUIRED IN
 1992-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) ADDITIONAL ALLOWANCE- In the case of any qualified
 equipment-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the depreciation deduction provided by section 167(a)
 for the taxable year in which such equipment is placed in service shall
 include an allowance equal to 15 percent of the adjusted basis of the
 qualified equipment, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the adjusted basis of the qualified equipment shall
 be reduced by the amount of such deduction before computing the amount
 otherwise allowable as a depreciation deduction under this chapter for such
 taxable year and any subsequent taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) QUALIFIED EQUIPMENT- For purposes of this subsection--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The term `qualified equipment' means
 property to which this section applies-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) which is section 1245 property (within the meaning
 of section 1245(a)(3)), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the original use of which commences with the taxpayer
 on or after February 1, 1992, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) which is-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) acquired by the taxpayer on or after February 1,
 1992, and before January 1, 1993, but only if no written binding contract
 for the acquisition was in effect before February 1, 1992, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) acquired by the taxpayer pursuant to a written
 binding contract which was entered into on or after February 1, 1992,
 and before January 1, 1993, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) which is placed in service by the taxpayer before
 July 1, 1993. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) EXCEPTIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) ALTERNATIVE DEPRECIATION PROPERTY- The term `qualified
 equipment' shall not include any property to which the alternative

 [Struck out->]   `(I) without regard to paragraph (7) of subsection (g)
 (relating to election to have system apply), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) after application of section 280F(b) (relating to
 listed property with limited business use). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) ELECTION OUT- If a taxpayer makes an election under
 this clause with respect to any class of property for any taxable year,
 this subsection shall not apply to all property in such class placed in
 service during such taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SPECIAL RULES RELATING TO ORIGINAL USE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) SELF-CONSTRUCTED PROPERTY- In the case of a taxpayer
 manufacturing, constructing, or producing property for the taxpayer's own use,
 the requirements of clause (iii) of subparagraph (A) shall be treated as met
 if the taxpayer begins manufacturing, constructing, or producing the property
 on and after February 1, 1992, and before January 1, 1993. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) SALE-LEASEBACKS- For purposes of subparagraph (A)(ii),
 if property-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) is originally placed in service on or after February 1,
 1992, by a person, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) is sold and leased back by such person within 3 months
 after the date such property was originally placed in service, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] such property shall be treated as originally placed in
 service not  earlier than the date on which such property is used under
 the leaseback referred to in subclause (II). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 280F- For purposes of
 section 280F-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) AUTOMOBILES- In the case of a passenger automobile (as
 defined in section 280F(d)(5)) which is qualified equipment, the Secretary
 shall increase the limitation under section 280F(a)(1)(A)(i), and decrease
 each other limitation under subparagraphs (A) and (B) of section 280F(a)(1),
 to appropriately reflect the amount of the deduction allowable under paragraph
 (1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) LISTED PROPERTY- The deduction allowable under
 paragraph (1) shall be taken into account in computing any recapture amount
 under section 280F(b)(2).' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) ALLOWANCE AGAINST ALTERNATIVE MINIMUM TAX-  [<-Struck
 out]

 [Struck out->] Subtitle B--Capital Gain Provisions [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 2101. INDEXING OF CERTAIN ASSETS ACQUIRED ON OR AFTER
 FEBRUARY 1, 1992, FOR PURPOSES OF DETERMINING GAIN. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Part II of subchapter O of chapter 1
 (relating to basis rules of general application) is amended by inserting
 after section 1021 the following new section: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1022. INDEXING OF CERTAIN ASSETS ACQUIRED ON OR AFTER
 FEBRUARY 1, 1992, FOR PURPOSES OF DETERMINING GAIN. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) GENERAL RULE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) INDEXED BASIS SUBSTITUTED FOR ADJUSTED BASIS- Solely for
 purposes of determining gain on the sale or other disposition by a taxpayer
 (other than a corporation) of an indexed asset which has been held for more
 than 1 year, the indexed basis of the asset shall be substituted for its
 adjusted basis. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULE FOR RECAPTURE GAIN-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- Paragraph (1) shall not apply for
 purposes of determining the amount of recapture gain on the sale or other
 disposition of an indexed asset, but the amount of any such recapture gain
 shall increase the adjusted basis of the asset for purposes of applying
 paragraph (1) to determine the amount of other gain on such sale or other
 disposition. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) RECAPTURE GAIN- For purposes of subparagraph (A),
 the term `recapture gain' means any gain treated as ordinary income under
 section 1245, 1250, or 1254. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) INDEXED ASSET-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this section, the term
 `indexed asset' means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any stock in a corporation, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any tangible property (or any interest therein),
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] which is a capital asset or property used in the trade or
 business (as defined in section 1231(b)) and the holding period of which
 begins on or after February 1, 1992. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CERTAIN PROPERTY EXCLUDED- For purposes of this section,
 the term `indexed asset' does not include-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) CREDITOR'S INTEREST- Any interest in property which
 is in the nature of a creditor's interest. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) COLLECTIBLES- Any collectible (as defined in section
 408(m)(2) without regard to section 408(m)(3)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) OPTIONS- Any option or other right to acquire an
 interest in property. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) NET LEASE PROPERTY- In the case of a lessor, net
 lease property (within the meaning of subsection (i)(3)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) STOCK IN FOREIGN CORPORATIONS- Stock in a foreign
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(F) STOCK IN S CORPORATIONS- Stock in an S
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) EXCEPTION FOR STOCK IN FOREIGN CORPORATION WHICH
 IS REGULARLY TRADED ON NATIONAL OR REGIONAL EXCHANGE- Paragraph (2)(E)
 shall not apply to stock in a foreign corporation the stock of which is
 listed on the New York Stock Exchange, the American Stock Exchange, or any
 domestic regional exchange for which quotations are published on a regular
 basis or is authorized for trading on the national market system operated
 by the National Association of Securities Dealers other than-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) a passive foreign corporation (as defined in section
 1296), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) stock in a foreign corporation held by a United States
 person who meets the requirements of section 1248(a)(2). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) INDEXED BASIS- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) INDEXED BASIS- The indexed basis for any asset is--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the adjusted basis of the asset, multiplied by
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the applicable inflation ratio. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) APPLICABLE INFLATION RATIO- The applicable inflation
 ratio for any asset shall be determined by dividing-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the CPI for the calendar year preceding the calendar
 year in which the disposition takes place, by [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the CPI for the calendar year preceding the calendar
 year in which the taxpayer's holding period for such asset began. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->] The applicable inflation ratio shall not be taken into
 account unless it is greater than 1. The applicable inflation ratio for
 any asset shall be rounded to the nearest one-thousandth. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) CONVENTIONS- For purposes of paragraph (2), if any
 asset is disposed of during any calendar year-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such disposition shall be treated as occurring on
 the last day of such calendar year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the taxpayer's holding period for such asset shall be
 treated as beginning in the same calendar year as would be determined for
 an asset actually disposed of on such last day with a holding period of the
 same length as the actual holding period of the asset involved. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) CPI- For purposes of this subsection, the CPI for
 any calendar year shall be determined under section 1(f)(4). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) SHORT SALES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- In the case of a short sale of an indexed
 asset with a short sale period in excess of 1 year, for purposes of this
 title, the amount realized shall be an amount equal to the amount realized
 (determined without regard to this paragraph) multiplied by the applicable
 inflation ratio. In applying subsection (c)(2) for purposes of the preceding
 sentence, the date on which the property is sold short shall be treated as
 the date on which the holding period for the asset begins and the closing
 date for the sale shall be treated as the date of disposition. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SHORT SALE OF SUBSTANTIALLY IDENTICAL PROPERTY- If
 the taxpayer or the taxpayer's spouse sells short property substantially
 identical to an asset held by the taxpayer, the asset held by the taxpayer
 and the substantially identical property shall not be treated as indexed
 assets for the short sale period. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) SHORT SALE PERIOD- For purposes of this subsection,
 the short sale period begins on the day after property is sold and ends on
 the closing date for the sale. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) TREATMENT OF REGULATED INVESTMENT COMPANIES AND REAL
 ESTATE INVESTMENT TRUSTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) ADJUSTMENTS AT ENTITY LEVEL-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 paragraph, the adjustment under subsection (a) shall be allowed to any
 qualified investment entity (including for purposes of determining the
 earnings and profits of such entity). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) EXCEPTION FOR CORPORATE SHAREHOLDERS- Under
 regulations-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) in the case of a distribution by a qualified investment
 entity (directly or indirectly) to a corporation-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) the determination of whether such distribution is a
 dividend shall be made without regard to this section, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the amount treated as gain by reason of the receipt of
 any capital gain dividend shall be increased by the percentage by which the
 entity's net capital gain for the taxable year determined without regard to
 this section exceeds the entity's net capital gain for such year determined
 with regard to this section, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) there shall be other appropriate adjustments (including
 deemed distributions) so as to ensure that the benefits of this section are
 not allowed (directly or indirectly) to corporate shareholders of qualified
 investment entities. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of the preceding sentence, any amount includible
 in gross income under section 852(b)(3)(D) shall be treated as a capital gain
 dividend and an S corporation shall not be treated as a corporation. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) EXCEPTION FOR QUALIFICATION PURPOSES- This section
 shall not apply for purposes of sections 851(b) and 856(c). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) EXCEPTION FOR CERTAIN TAXES IMPOSED AT ENTITY LEVEL-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) TAX ON FAILURE TO DISTRIBUTE ENTIRE GAIN- If any
 amount is subject to tax under section 852(b)(3)(A) for any taxable year,
 the amount on which tax is imposed under such section shall be increased
 by the percentage determined under subparagraph (B)(i)(II). A similar rule
 shall apply in the case of any amount subject to tax under paragraph (2) or
 (3) of section 857(b) to the extent attributable to the excess of the net
 capital gain over the deduction for dividends paid determined with reference
 to capital gain dividends only. The first sentence of this clause shall not
 apply to so much of the amount subject to tax under section 852(b)(3)(A)
 as is designated by the company under section 852(b)(3)(D). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) OTHER TAXES- This section shall not apply for
 purposes of determining the amount of any tax imposed by paragraph (4),
 (5), or (6) of section 857(b). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) ADJUSTMENTS TO INTERESTS HELD IN ENTITY-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- Stock in a qualified investment entity
 shall be an indexed asset for any calendar month in the same ratio as
 the fair market value of the assets held by such entity at the close of
 such month which are indexed assets (determined without regard to the
 requirement that the holding period begin on or after February 1, 1992)
 bears to the fair market value of all assets of such entity at the close
 of such month. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) RATIO OF 90 PERCENT OR MORE- If the ratio for any
 calendar month determined under subparagraph (A) would (but for this
 subparagraph) be 90 percent or more, such ratio for such month shall be
 100 percent. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) RATIO OF 10 PERCENT OR LESS- If the ratio for any
 calendar month determined under subparagraph (A) would (but for this
 subparagraph) be 10 percent or less, such ratio for such month shall be
 zero. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) VALUATION OF ASSETS IN CASE OF REAL ESTATE INVESTMENT
 TRUSTS- Nothing in this paragraph shall require a real estate investment
 trust to value its assets more frequently than once each 36 months (except
 where such trust ceases to exist). The ratio under subparagraph (A) for any
 calendar month for which there is no valuation shall be the trustee's good
 faith judgment as to such valuation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) QUALIFIED INVESTMENT ENTITY- For purposes of this
 subsection, the term `qualified investment entity' means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) a regulated investment company (within the meaning
 of section 851), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) a real estate investment trust (within the meaning
 of section 856). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) OTHER PASS-THRU ENTITIES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) PARTNERSHIPS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- In the case of a partnership, the adjustment
 made under subsection (a) at the partnership level shall be passed through
 to the partners (but only for purposes of determining the income of partners
 who are not corporations). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) SPECIAL RULE IN THE CASE OF SECTION 754 ELECTIONS-
 In the case of a transfer of an interest in a partnership with respect to
 which the election provided in section 754 is in effect-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the adjustment under section 743(b)(1) shall, with
 respect to the transferor partner, be treated as a sale of the partnership
 assets for purposes of applying this section, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) with respect to the transferee partner, the
 partnership's holding period for purposes of this section in such assets
 shall be treated as beginning on the date of such adjustment. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) S CORPORATIONS- In the case of an S corporation,
 the adjustment made under subsection (a) at the corporate level shall
 be passed through to the shareholders. This section shall not apply for
 purposes of determining the amount of any tax imposed by section 1374 or
 1375. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) COMMON TRUST FUNDS- In the case of a common trust
 fund, the adjustment made under subsection (a) at the trust level shall be
 passed through to the participants (but only for purposes of determining
 the income of participants who are not corporations). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(g) DISPOSITIONS BETWEEN RELATED PERSONS- This section
 shall not apply to any sale or other disposition of property between related
 persons (within the meaning of section 465(b)(3)(C)) if such property,
 in the hands of the transferee, is of a character subject to the allowance
 for depreciation provided in section 167. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(h) TRANSFERS TO INCREASE INDEXING ADJUSTMENT- If any
 person transfers cash, debt, or any other property to another person
 and the principal purpose of such transfer is to secure or increase an
 adjustment under subsection (a), the Secretary may disallow part or all of
 such adjustment or increase. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) SPECIAL RULES- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) TREATMENT AS SEPARATE ASSET- In the case of any asset,
 the following shall be treated as a separate asset: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) A substantial improvement to property. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) In the case of stock of a corporation, a substantial
 contribution to capital. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) Any other portion of an asset to the extent that
 separate treatment of such portion is appropriate to carry out the purposes
 of this section. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) ASSETS WHICH ARE NOT INDEXED ASSETS THROUGHOUT HOLDING
 PERIOD- The applicable inflation ratio shall be appropriately reduced for
 periods during which the asset was not an indexed asset. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) NET LEASE PROPERTY DEFINED- The term `net lease
 property' means leased property where-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the term of the lease (taking into account options
 to renew) was 50 percent or more of the useful life of the property, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) for the period of the lease, the sum of the deductions
 with respect to such property which are allowable to the lessor solely by
 reason of section 162 (other than rents and reimbursed amounts with respect
 to such property) is 15 percent or less of the rental income produced by
 such property. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(j) REGULATIONS- The Secretary shall prescribe such
 regulations as may be necessary or appropriate to carry out the purposes
 of this section.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) GAINS AND LOSSES FROM INDEXED ASSETS NOT TAKEN
 INTO ACCOUNT UNDER LIMITATION ON INVESTMENT INTEREST- Subparagraph (B)
 of section 163(d)(4) (defining investment income) is amended by adding at
 the end thereof the following new sentences: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Gain from the sale or other disposition of an indexed asset
 (as defined in section 1022) held for more than 1 year shall not be taken
 into account for purposes of the preceding sentence. The preceding sentence
 shall not apply to gain from the sale or other disposition of any such asset
 if the taxpayer elects to waive the benefits of section 1022 in determining
 the amount of such gain.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) RECAPTURE OF ENTIRE AMOUNT OF DEPRECIATION UNDER SECTION
 1250- Section 1250 (relating to gain from dispositions of certain depreciable
 realty) is amended by adding at the end thereof the following new subsection:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) RECAPTURE OF ENTIRE AMOUNT OF DEPRECIATION IN CASE
 OF PROPERTY TO WHICH SECTION 1022 APPLIES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- In the case of any taxpayer other than
 a corporation-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) subsection (a) shall be applied with respect to any
 disposition of section 1250 property to which section 1022 applies as if
 it read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   ` `(a) GENERAL RULE- Except as otherwise provided in
 this section, if section 1250 property is disposed of, the lesser of--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   ` `(1) the depreciation adjustments in respect of such
 property, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   ` `(2) the excess of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   ` `(A) the amount realized (or, in the case of a disposition
 other than  sale, exchange, or involuntary conversion, the fair market
 value of such property), over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   ` `(B) the adjusted basis of such property, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] shall be treated as gain which is ordinary income. Such gain
 shall be recognized notwithstanding any other provision of this subtitle.',
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) in the case of any disposition described in subparagraph
 (A), subsections (e) and (f) shall not apply and appropriate adjustments
 shall be made in the provisions of subsection (d). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULES FOR CERTAIN ENTITIES- For purposes
 of paragraph (1), the following shall not be treated as a corporation:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) An S corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) A regulated investment company. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) A real estate investment trust. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 453(i)- Subsection (i) of
 section 453 shall be applied without regard to this subsection.' [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   (d) CLERICAL AMENDMENT- The table of sections for part II
 of subchapter O of chapter 1 is amended by inserting after the item relating
 to section 1021 the following new item: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1022. Indexing of certain assets acquired on or after
 February 1, 1992, for purposes of determining gain.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (e) EFFECTIVE DATE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- The amendments made by this section shall
 apply to the disposition of any property the holding period of which begins
 on or after February 1, 1992. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) CERTAIN TRANSACTIONS BETWEEN RELATED PERSONS- The
 amendments made by this section shall not apply to the disposition of any
 property acquired on or after February 1, 1992, from a related person (as
 defined in section 465(b)(3)(C) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986) if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) such property was so acquired for a price less than
 the property's fair market value, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) the amendments made by this section did not apply to
 such property in the hands of such related person. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (f) ELECTION TO RECOGNIZE GAIN ON READILY TRADABLE SECURITIES
 HELD ON FEBRUARY 1, 1992-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- If a taxpayer other than a corporation
 holds any readily tradable security on February 1, 1992, the taxpayer may
 elect to treat such security as having been sold on the last business day
 before such date for an amount equal to its closing market price on such
 last business day (and as having been reacquired on such last business day
 for an amount equal to such closing market price). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) TREATMENT OF GAIN OR LOSS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) Any gain resulting from an election under paragraph (1)
 shall be treated as received or accrued on the last business day referred
 to in paragraph (1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) Any loss resulting from an election under paragraph
 (1) shall not be allowed for any taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (3) ELECTION- An election under paragraph (1) shall
 be made in such manner as the Secretary may prescribe and shall specify
 the readily tradable securities for which such election is made. Such an
 election, once made with respect to any readily tradable security, shall
 be irrevocable. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (4) READILY TRADABLE SECURITY- For purposes of this
 subsection, the term `readily tradable security' means any stock or other
 security which, as of February 1, 1992, is readily tradable on an established
 securities market or otherwise. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 2102. 50-PERCENT EXCLUSION FOR GAIN OF INDIVIDUALS FROM
 CERTAIN SMALL BUSINESS STOCK. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Part I of subchapter P of chapter 1
 (relating to capital gains and losses) is amended by adding at the end
 thereof the following new section: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1202. 50-PERCENT EXCLUSION FOR GAIN OF INDIVIDUALS
 FROM CERTAIN SMALL BUSINESS STOCK. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) GENERAL RULE- In the case of a taxpayer other than
 a corporation, gross income shall not include 50 percent of any gain from
 the sale or exchange of qualified small business stock held for more than
 5 years. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) QUALIFIED SMALL BUSINESS STOCK- For purposes of this
 section-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 section, the term `qualified small business stock' means any stock in a
 corporation which is originally issued on or after February 1, 1992, if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) as of the date of issuance, such corporation is a
 qualified small business, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) except as provided in subsections (d) and (e), such
 stock is acquired by the taxpayer at its original issue (directly or through
 an underwriter)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) in exchange for money or other property (not including
 stock), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) as compensation for services (other than services
 performed as an underwriter of such stock). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) ACTIVE BUSINESS REQUIREMENT- Stock in a corporation
 shall not be treated as qualified small business stock unless, during
 substantially all of the taxpayer's holding period for such stock,
 such corporation meets the active business requirements of subsection
 (d). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) CERTAIN PURCHASES BY CORPORATION OF ITS OWN STOCK-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- Stock issued by a corporation shall
 not be treated as qualified small business stock if such corporation has
 purchased or purchases any of its stock within the 2-year period beginning
 1 year before the date of the issuance of such stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) WAIVER WHERE BUSINESS PURPOSE- Subparagraph (A)
 shall not apply where the issuing corporation establishes that there was
 a business purpose for the purchase of the stock and such purchase is not
 inconsistent with the purposes of this section. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) MEMBERS OF AFFILIATED GROUP- For purposes of this
 paragraph, the purchase by any corporation which is a member of the same
 affiliated group (within the meaning of section 1504) as the issuing
 corporation of any stock in any corporation which is a member of such
 group shall be treated as a purchase by the issuing corporation of its
 stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) QUALIFIED SMALL BUSINESS- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The term `qualified small business'
 means any domestic corporation if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the aggregate capitalization of such corporation
 (or any predecessor thereof) at all times on or after February 1, 1992,
 and before the issuance did not exceed $100,000,000, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the aggregate capitalization of such corporation
 immediately after the issuance (determined by taking into account amounts
 to be received in the issuance) does not exceed $100,000,000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) AGGREGATE CAPITALIZATION- For purposes of paragraph
 (1), the term `aggregate capitalization' means the excess of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the amount of cash and the aggregate adjusted bases
 of other property held by the corporation, over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the aggregate amount of the short-term indebtedness
 of the corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of the preceding sentence, the term `short-term
 indebtedness' means any indebtedness which, when incurred, did not have a
 term in excess of 1 year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) LOOK-THRU IN CASE OF SUBSIDIARIES- In determining
 whether a corporation meets the requirements of this subsection--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) stock and debt of any subsidiary (as defined in
 subsection (d)(4)(C)) held by such corporation shall be disregarded, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) such corporation shall be treated as holding its
 ratable share of the assets of such subsidiary and as being liable for its
 ratable share of the indebtedness of such subsidiary. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) ACTIVE BUSINESS REQUIREMENT- For purposes of this
 section-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of subsection (b)(2), the
 requirements of this subsection are met for any period if during such period--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the corporation is engaged in the active conduct of
 a trade or business, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) substantially all of the assets of such corporation
 are used in the active conduct of a trade or business, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) such corporation is an eligible corporation. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULE FOR CERTAIN ACTIVITIES- For purposes
 of paragraph (1), if, in connection with any future trade or business,
 a corporation is engaged in-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) start-up activities described in section 195(c)(1)(A),
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) activities resulting in the payment or incurring of
 expenditures which may be treated as research and experimental expenditures
 under section 174, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) activities with respect to in-house research expenses
 described in section 41(b)(4), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] such corporation shall be treated with respect to such
 activities as engaged in (and assets used in such activities shall
 be treated as used in) the active conduct of a trade or business. Any
 determination under this paragraph shall be made without regard to whether
 a corporation has any gross income from such activities at the time of the
 determination. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) ELIGIBLE CORPORATION- For purposes of this subsection--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The term `eligible corporation' means any
 domestic corporation; except that such term shall not include-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) any corporation predominantly engaged in a disqualified
 business, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) any corporation the principal activity of which is
 the performance of personal services, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) a DISC, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) a corporation with respect to which an election
 under 936 is in effect, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(v) any regulated investment company, real estate investment
 trust, or REMIC, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(vi) any cooperative. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) DISQUALIFIED BUSINESS- The term `disqualified business'
 means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) any banking, insurance, financing, or similar business,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) any farming business, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) any business involving the production or extraction
 of products of a character with respect to which a deduction is allowable
 under section 613 or 613A, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) any business of operating a hotel, motel, or restaurant
 or similar business. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) STOCK IN OTHER CORPORATIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) LOOK-THRU IN CASE OF SUBSIDIARIES- For purposes of
 this subsection, stock and debt in any subsidiary corporation shall be
 disregarded and the parent corporation shall be deemed to own its ratable
 share of the subsidiary's assets, and to conduct its ratable share of the
 subsidiary's activities. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) PORTFOLIO STOCK OR SECURITIES- A corporation shall
 be treated as failing to meet the requirements of paragraph (1) for any
 period during which more than 10 percent of the value of its assets (in
 excess of liabilities) consist of stock or securities in other corporations
 which are not subsidiaries of such corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SUBSIDIARY- For purposes of this paragraph, a
 corporation shall be considered a subsidiary if the parent owns at least
 50 percent of the combined voting power of all classes of stock entitled
 to vote, or at least 50 percent in value of all outstanding stock, of such
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) WORKING CAPITAL- For purposes of paragraph (1)(B),
 any assets which-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) are held for investment, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) are to be used to finance future research and
 experimentation or working capital needs of the corporation, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] shall be treated as used in the active conduct of a trade
 or business. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(6) MAXIMUM REAL ESTATE HOLDINGS- A corporation shall
 not be treated as meeting the requirements of paragraph (1) for any period
 during which more than 10 percent of the total value of its assets is real
 property which is not used in the active conduct of a trade or business. For
 purposes of the preceding sentence, the ownership of, dealing in, or renting
 of real property shall not be treated as the active conduct of a trade or
 business. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(7) COMPUTER SOFTWARE ROYALTIES- For purposes of paragraph
 (1), rights to computer software which produces income described in section
 543(d) shall be treated as an asset used in the active conduct of a trade
 or business. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) STOCK ACQUIRED ON CONVERSION OF PREFERRED STOCK-
 If any stock is acquired through the conversion of other stock which is
 qualified small business stock in the hands of the taxpayer-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) the stock so acquired shall be treated as qualified
 small business stock in the hands of the taxpayer, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the stock so acquired shall be treated as having been
 held during the period during which the converted stock was held. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) TREATMENT OF PASS-THRU ENTITIES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Any amount included in income by reason of
 holding an interest in a pass-thru entity shall be treated as gain described
 in subsection (a) if such amount meets the requirements of paragraph
 (2). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) REQUIREMENTS- An amount meets the requirements of
 this paragraph if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such amount is attributable to gain on the sale or
 exchange by the pass-thru entity of stock which is qualified small business
 stock in the hands of such entity and which was held by such entity for
 more than 5 years, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such amount is includible in the gross income of the
 taxpayer by reason of the holding of an interest in such entity which was
 held by the taxpayer on the date on which such pass-thru entity acquired
 such stock and at all times thereafter before the disposition of such stock
 by such pass-thru entity. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) PASS-THRU ENTITY- For purposes of this subsection,
 the term `pass-thru entity' means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any partnership, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any S corporation, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) any regulated investment company, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) any common trust fund. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(g) CERTAIN TAX-FREE AND OTHER TRANSFERS- For purposes
 of this section-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- In the case of a transfer of stock to which
 this subsection applies, the transferee shall be treated as-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) having acquired such stock in the same manner as the
 transferor, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) having held such stock during any continuous period
 immediately preceding the transfer during which it was held (or treated as
 held under this subsection) by the transferor. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TRANSFERS TO WHICH SUBSECTION APPLIES- This subsection
 shall apply to any transfer-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) by gift, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) at death. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) CERTAIN RULES MADE APPLICABLE- Rules similar
 to the rules of section 1244(d)(2) shall apply for purposes of this
 section. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) INCORPORATIONS AND REORGANIZATIONS INVOLVING
 NONQUALIFIED STOCK-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- In the case of a transaction described
 in section 351 or a reorganization described in section 368, if a qualified
 small business stock is transferred for other stock, such transfer shall be
 treated as a transfer to which this subsection applies solely with respect
 to the person receiving such other stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) LIMITATION- This section shall apply to the sale or
 exchange of stock treated as qualified small business stock by reason of
 subparagraph (A) only to the extent of the gain (if any) which would have
 been recognized at the time of the transfer described in subparagraph (A)
 if section 351 or 368 had not applied at such time. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SUCCESSIVE APPLICATION- For purposes of this paragraph,
 stock treated as qualified small business stock under subparagraph (A)
 shall be so treated for subsequent transactions or reorganizations, except
 that the limitation of subparagraph (B) shall be applied as of the time of
 the first transfer to which subparagraph (A) applied. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) CONTROL TEST- Except in the case of a transaction
 described in section 368, this paragraph shall apply only if, immediately
 after the transaction, the corporation issuing the stock owns directly or
 indirectly stock representing control (within the meaning of section 368(c))
 of the corporation whose stock was transferred. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(h) BASIS RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) STOCK EXCHANGED FOR PROPERTY- For purposes of this
 section, in the case where the taxpayer transfers property (other than
 money or stock) to a corporation in exchange for stock in such corporation--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such stock shall be treated as having been acquired
 by the taxpayer on the date of such exchange, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the basis of such stock in the hands of the taxpayer
 shall in no event be less than the fair market value of the property
 exchanged. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) BASIS OF S CORPORATION STOCK- For purposes of this
 section, the adjusted basis of stock in an S corporation shall in no event
 be less than its adjusted basis determined without regard to any adjustment
 to the basis of such stock under section 1367. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) REGULATIONS- The Secretary shall prescribe such
 regulations as may be appropriate to carry out the purposes of this section,
 including regulations to prevent the avoidance of the purposes of this
 section through split-ups or otherwise.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) EXCLUSION TREATED AS PREFERENCE FOR MINIMUM TAX-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Subsection (a) of section 57 (relating
 to items of tax preference) is amended by adding at the end thereof the
 following new paragraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(8) EXCLUSION FOR GAINS ON SALE OF CERTAIN SMALL BUSINESS
 STOCK- An amount equal to the amount excluded from gross income for the
 taxable year under section 1202.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) CONFORMING AMENDMENT- Subclause (II) of section
 53(d)(2)(B)(ii) is amended by striking `and (6)' and inserting `(6), and
 (8)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) CONFORMING AMENDMENTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1)(A) Section 172(d)(2) (relating to modifications with
 respect to net operating loss deduction) is amended to read as follows:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CAPITAL GAINS AND LOSSES OF TAXPAYERS OTHER THAN
 CORPORATIONS- In the case of a taxpayer other than a corporation--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the amount deductible on account of losses from sales
 or exchanges of capital assets shall not exceed the amount includable on
 account of gains from sales or exchanges of capital assets; and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the exclusion provided by section 1202 shall not be
 allowed.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) Subparagraph (B) of section 172(d)(4) is amended by
 inserting `, (2)(B),' after `paragraph (1)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) Paragraph (4) of section 642(c) is amended to read as
 follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) ADJUSTMENTS- To the extent that the amount otherwise
 allowable as a deduction under this subsection consists of gain described
 in section 1202(a), proper adjustment shall be made for any exclusion
 allowable to the estate or trust under section 1202. In the case of a trust,
 the deduction allowed by this subsection shall be subject to section 681
 (relating to unrelated business income).' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (3) Paragraph (3) of section 643(a) is amended by adding
 at the end thereof the following new sentence: `The exclusion under section
 1202 shall not be taken into account.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (4) Paragraph (4) of section 691(c) is amended by striking

 [Struck out->]   (5) The second sentence of paragraph (2) of section 871(a)
 is amended by inserting `such gains and losses shall be determined without
 regard to section 1202 and' after `except that'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (e) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to stock issued on or after February 1, 1992. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] Subtitle C--Real Estate Provisions [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] PART I--MODIFICATION OF PASSIVE LOSS RULES [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 2201. MODIFICATION OF PASSIVE LOSS RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Subsection (c) of section 469 (relating
 to passive activity losses and credits limited) is amended by adding at
 the end thereof the following new paragraphs: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(7) TAXPAYERS ENGAGED IN THE REAL PROPERTY BUSINESS-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- In the case of a taxpayer engaged in the
 real property business, the determination of what constitutes an activity
 and whether an activity is a passive activity shall be made by treating the
 taxpayer's rental real property operations, undertakings, and activities
 in the same manner as nonrental trade or business operations, undertakings,
 and activities. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) EXCEPTIONS- Subparagraph (A) shall not apply with
 respect to-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) any interest held as a limited partner, and [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) any rental activity with respect to any real property
 originally placed in service after the date of the enactment of this paragraph
 (whether or not by the taxpayer). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) 20 PERCENT OF ITEMS REMAIN SUBJECT TO LIMITATION-
 Notwithstanding subparagraph (A), 20 percent of the items of income, gain,
 loss, deduction, or credit allocable to any real property rental activity
 shall continue to be treated as items allocable to a passive activity. Any
 amount disallowed by reason of the preceding sentence shall be treated as
 an amount allocable to a former passive activity for purposes of applying
 subsection (f) (as modified by subparagraph (D) of this paragraph). [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) TREATMENT OF SUSPENDED LOSSES- For purposes of applying
 subsection (f) with respect to any rental activity which is treated as
 not being a passive activity by reason of this paragraph, the holding and
 renting of each separate property shall be treated as a separate activity
 which may not be aggregated with rental activities with respect to other
 properties or with other real property operations. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(8) INDIVIDUALS ENGAGED IN THE REAL PROPERTY BUSINESS-
 For purposes of paragraph (7), an individual is engaged in the real property
 business if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such individual spends at least 50 percent of such
 individual's working time in real property operations; and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such individual spends more than 500 hours during
 the taxable year in real property operations. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(9) REAL PROPERTY OPERATIONS- For purposes of paragraph (8),
 the term `real property operations' means any real property development,
 redevelopment, construction, reconstruction, acquisition, conversion,
 rental, operation, management, leasing, brokerage, appraisal, and finance
 operations. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(10) WORKING TIME- For purposes of paragraph (8), the
 term `working time' means any time spent as an employee, sole proprietor,
 S corporation shareholder, partner in a partnership, or beneficiary of a
 trust or estate. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(11) CLOSELY HELD C CORPORATIONS ENGAGED IN THE REAL
 PROPERTY BUSINESS- For purposes of paragraph (7), a closely held C corporation
 is engaged in the real property business if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) 1 or more shareholders owning stock representing more
 than 50 percent (by value) of the outstanding stock of such corporation
 materially participate in the aggregate real property activities of such
 corporation; or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such corporation meets the requirements of section
 465(c)(7)(C) (without regard to clause (iv)) with respect to the aggregate
 real property activities of such corporation.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CONFORMING AMENDMENTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) Paragraph (2) of section 469(c) is amended to read as
 follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) PASSIVE ACTIVITY INCLUDES CERTAIN RENTAL ACTIVITIES-
 Except for rental activities treated in the same manner as nonrental trade
 or business activities pursuant to paragraph (7), each rental activity is
 a passive activity without regard to whether or not the taxpayer materially
 participates in the rental activity.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) Paragraph (4) of such section 469(c) is amended to
 read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) MATERIAL PARTICIPATION NOT REQUIRED FOR PARAGRAPH
 (3)- Paragraph (3) shall be applied without regard to whether or not the
 taxpayer materially participates in the activity.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to taxable years beginning after December 31, 1991. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] PART II--PROVISIONS RELATING TO REAL ESTATE INVESTMENTS BY
 PENSION FUNDS [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 2211. REAL ESTATE PROPERTY ACQUIRED BY A QUALIFIED
 ORGANIZATION. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) MODIFICATIONS OF EXCEPTIONS- Paragraph (9) of section
 514(c) (relating to real property acquired by a qualified organization)
 is amended by adding at the end thereof the following new subparagraphs:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(G) SPECIAL RULES FOR PURPOSES OF THE EXCEPTIONS- Except
 as otherwise provided by regulations-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) SMALL LEASES DISREGARDED- For purposes of clauses
 (iii) and (iv) of subparagraph (B), a lease to a person described in such
 clause (iii) or (iv) shall be disregarded if no more than 10 percent of
 the leasable floor space in a building is covered by the lease and if the
 lease is on commercially reasonable terms. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) COMMERCIALLY REASONABLE FINANCING- Clause (v)
 of subparagraph (B) shall not apply if the financing is on commercially
 reasonable terms. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(H) QUALIFYING SALES OUT OF FORECLOSURE BY FINANCIAL
 INSTITUTIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- In the case of a qualifying sale out of
 foreclosure by a financial institution, except as provided in regulations,
 clauses (i) and (ii) of subparagraph (B) shall not apply with respect to
 financing provided by such institution for such sale. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) QUALIFYING SALE- For purposes of this clause, there
 is a qualifying sale out of foreclosure by a financial institution where--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) a qualified organization acquires foreclosure property
 from a financial institution and the financial institution treats any income
 realized from the sale or exchange of the foreclosure property as ordinary
 income, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the stated principal amount of the financing provided
 by the financial institution does not exceed the amount of the outstanding
 indebtedness (including accrued but unpaid interest) of the financial
 institution with respect to the foreclosure property immediately before
 the acquisition referred to in clause (iv), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(III) the value (determined as of the time of the sale)
 of the amount pursuant to the financing that is determined by reference
 to the revenue, income, or profits derived from the property does not
 exceed 25 percent of the value of the property (determined as of such
 time). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) FINANCIAL INSTITUTION- For purposes of this
 subparagraph, the term `financial institution' means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) any financial institution described in section 581
 or 591(a), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) any other corporation which is a member of an
 affiliated group (as defined in section 1504(a)) which includes an institution
 referred to in subclause (I) but only if such other corporation is subject
 to supervision and examination by the same Federal or State agency as the
 institution referred to in subclause (I), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(III) any person acting as a conservator or receiver of
 an entity referred to in subclause (I) or (II). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) FORECLOSURE PROPERTY- For purposes of this
 subparagraph, the term `foreclosure property' means any real property
 acquired by the financial institution as the result of having bid on such
 property at foreclosure, or by operation of an agreement or process of law,
 after there was a default (or a default was imminent) on indebtedness which
 such property secured.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CONFORMING AMENDMENT- Paragraph (9) of section 514(c)
 is amended-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) by adding the following new sentence at the end of
 subparagraph (A): `For purposes of this paragraph, an interest in a mortgage
 shall in no event be treated as real property.', and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) by striking the last sentence of subparagraph
 (B). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to acquisitions on or after February 1, 1992. [<-Struck out]

 the requirements of subclause (II). [<-Struck out]

 subparagraph, the term `disqualified person' means any person described
