 [Struck out->] SEC. 2215. TREATMENT OF PENSION FUND INVESTMENTS IN REAL
 ESTATE INVESTMENT TRUSTS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Subsection (h) of section 856 (relating
 to closely held determinations) is amended by adding at the end thereof
 the following new paragraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) TREATMENT OF TRUSTS DESCRIBED IN SECTION 401(a)-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) LOOK-THRU TREATMENT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- Except as provided in clause (ii), in
 determining whether the stock ownership requirement of section 542(a)(2)
 is met for purposes of paragraph (1)(A), any stock held by a qualified
 trust shall be treated as held directly by its beneficiaries in proportion
 to their actuarial interests in such trust and shall not be treated as held
 by such trust. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) CERTAIN RELATED TRUSTS NOT ELIGIBLE- Clause (i)
 shall not apply to any qualified trust if one or more disqualified persons
 (as defined in section 4975(e)(2)) with respect to such qualified trust
 hold in the aggregate 5 percent or more in value of the interests in the
 real estate investment trust and such real estate investment trust has
 accumulated earnings and profits attributable to any period for which it
 did not qualify as a real estate investment trust. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) COORDINATION WITH PERSONAL HOLDING COMPANY RULES-
 If any entity qualifies as a real estate investment trust for any taxable
 year by reason of subparagraph (H), such entity shall not be treated as a
 personal holding company for such taxable year for purposes of part II of
 subchapter G of this chapter. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) TREATMENT FOR PURPOSES OF UNRELATED BUSINESS TAX- If
 any qualified trust holds 10 percent or more (by value) of the interests in
 any real estate investment trust described in subparagraph (D), any income
 of such qualified trust attributable to its interests in such real estate
 investment trust shall be taken into account under part III of subchapter
 F of this chapter under rules similar to the rules applicable to income
 attributable to interests in partnerships. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) DESCRIPTION OF REAL ESTATE INVESTMENT TRUSTS-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- A real estate investment trust is described
 in this subparagraph if such trust would not have qualified as a real
 estate investment trust but for the provisions of this paragraph and if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) interests in such trust are not readily tradable on
 an established securities market, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) interests in such trust are so tradable but such
 trust is predominantly held by qualified trusts. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) PREDOMINANTLY HELD- For purposes of clause (i)(II),
 a real estate investment trust is predominantly held by qualified trusts if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) at least 1 qualified trust holds more than 25 percent
 (by value) of the interests in such real estate investment trust, or
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) 1 or more qualified trusts (each of whom own at least
 10 percent by value of the interests in such real estate investment trust)
 hold in the aggregate more than 50 percent (by value) of the interests in
 such real estate investment trust. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) QUALIFIED TRUST- For purposes of this paragraph (D),
 the term `qualified trust' means any trust described in section 401(a)
 and exempt from tax under section 501(a).' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendment made by this section
 shall apply to taxable years beginning after December 31, 1991. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] Subtitle F--Repeal of Certain Luxury Excise Taxes; Imposition
 of Tax on Diesel Fuel Used in Noncommercial Motorboats [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 2501. REPEAL OF LUXURY EXCISE TAXES OTHER THAN ON
 PASSENGER VEHICLES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Subchapter A of chapter 31 (relating to
 retail excise taxes) is amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subchapter A--Luxury Passenger Automobiles [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 4001. Imposition of tax. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 4002. 1st retail sale; uses, etc. treated as sales;
 determination of price. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 4003. Special rules. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 4001. IMPOSITION OF TAX. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) IMPOSITION OF TAX- There is hereby imposed on the 1st
 retail sale of any passenger vehicle a tax equal to 10 percent of the price
 for which so sold to the extent such price exceeds $30,000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) PASSENGER VEHICLE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this subchapter, the term
 `passenger vehicle' means any 4-wheeled vehicle-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) which is manufactured primarily for use on public
 streets, roads, and highways, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) which is rated at 6,000 pounds unloaded gross vehicle
 weight or less. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) TRUCKS AND VANS- In the case of a truck or van,
 paragraph (1)(B) shall be applied by substituting `gross vehicle weight'
 for `unloaded gross vehicle weight'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) LIMOUSINES- In the case of a limousine, paragraph (1)
 shall be applied without regard to subparagraph (B) thereof. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) EXCEPTIONS FOR TAXICABS, ETC- The tax imposed by
 this section shall not apply to the sale of any passenger vehicle for use
 by the purchaser exclusively in the active conduct of a trade or business
 of transporting persons or property for compensation or hire. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) EXEMPTION FOR LAW ENFORCEMENT USES, ETC- No tax shall be
 imposed by this section on the sale of any passenger vehicle-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) to the Federal Government, or a State or local
 government, for use exclusively in police, firefighting, search and rescue,
 or other law enforcement or public safety activities, or in public works
 activities, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) to any person for use exclusively in providing
 emergency medical services. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) INFLATION ADJUSTMENT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- In the case of any calendar year after
 1991, the $30,000 amount in subsection (a) and section 4003(a) shall be
 increased by an amount equal to-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) $30,000, multiplied by [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the cost-of-living adjustment under section 1(f)(3)
 for such calendar year, determined by substituting `calendar year 1990'
 for `calendar year 1991' in subparagraph (B) thereof. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) ROUNDING- If any amount as adjusted under paragraph
 (1) is not a multiple of $100, such amount shall be rounded to the nearest
 multiple of $100 (or, if such amount is a multiple of $50 and not of $100,
 such amount shall be rounded to the next highest multiple of $100). [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) TERMINATION- The tax imposed by this section shall
 not apply to any sale or use after December 31, 1999. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 4002. 1ST RETAIL SALE; USES, ETC. TREATED AS SALES;
 DETERMINATION OF PRICE. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) 1ST RETAIL SALE- For purposes of this subchapter,
 the term `1st retail sale' means the 1st sale, for a purpose other than
 resale, after manufacture, production, or importation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) USE TREATED AS SALE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If any person uses a passenger vehicle
 (including any use after importation) before the 1st retail sale of such
 vehicle, then such person shall be liable for tax under this subchapter in
 the same manner as if such vehicle were sold at retail by him. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) EXEMPTION FOR FURTHER MANUFACTURE- Paragraph (1)
 shall not apply to use of a vehicle as material in the manufacture or
 production of, or as a component part of, another vehicle taxable under
 this subchapter to be manufactured or produced by him. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) EXEMPTION FOR DEMONSTRATION USE- Paragraph (1) shall
 not apply to any use of a passenger vehicle as a demonstrator for a potential
 customer while the potential customer is in the vehicle. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) EXCEPTION FOR USE AFTER IMPORTATION OF CERTAIN
 VEHICLES- Paragraph (1) shall not apply to the use of a vehicle after
 importation if the user or importer establishes to the satisfaction of the
 Secretary that the 1st use of the vehicle occurred before January 1, 1991,
 outside the United States. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) COMPUTATION OF TAX- In the case of any person made
 liable for tax by paragraph (1), the tax shall be computed on the price at
 which similar vehicles are sold at retail in the ordinary course of trade,
 as determined by the Secretary. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) LEASES CONSIDERED AS SALES- For purposes of this
 subchapter-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 subsection, the lease of a vehicle (including any renewal or any extension
 of a lease or any subsequent lease of such vehicle) by any person shall be
 considered a sale of such vehicle at retail. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULES FOR LONG-TERM LEASES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) TAX NOT IMPOSED ON SALE FOR LEASING IN A QUALIFIED
 LEASE- The sale of a passenger vehicle to a person engaged in a passenger
 vehicle leasing or rental trade or business for leasing by such person
 in a long-term lease shall not be treated as the 1st retail sale of such
 vehicle. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) LONG-TERM LEASE- For purposes of subparagraph (A),
 the term `long-term lease' means any long-term lease (as defined in section
 4052). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SPECIAL RULES- In the case of a long-term lease
 of a vehicle which is treated as the 1st retail sale of such vehicle--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) DETERMINATION OF PRICE- The tax under this subchapter
 shall be computed on the lowest price for which the vehicle is sold by
 retailers in the ordinary course of trade. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) PAYMENT OF TAX- Rules similar to the rules of section
 4217(e)(2) shall apply. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) NO TAX WHERE EXEMPT USE BY LESSEE- No tax shall be
 imposed on any lease payment under a long-term lease if the lessee's use
 of the vehicle under such lease is an exempt use (as defined in section
 4003(b)) of such vehicle. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) DETERMINATION OF PRICE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- In determining price for purposes of this
 subchapter-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) there shall be included any charge incident to placing
 the article in condition ready for use, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) there shall be excluded-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the amount of the tax imposed by this subchapter,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) if stated as a separate charge, the amount of any
 retail sales tax imposed by any State or political subdivision thereof or
 the District of Columbia, whether the liability for such tax is imposed on
 the vendor or vendee, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) the value of any component of such article if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) such component is furnished by the 1st user of such
 article, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) such component has been used before such furnishing,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) the price shall be determined without regard to any
 trade-in. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) OTHER RULES- Rules similar to the rules of
 paragraphs (2) and (4) of section 4052(b) shall apply for purposes of this
 subchapter. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 4003. SPECIAL RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) SEPARATE PURCHASE OF VEHICLE AND PARTS AND ACCESSORIES
 THEREFOR- Under regulations prescribed by the Secretary-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as provided in paragraph (2), if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the owner, lessee, or operator of any passenger vehicle
 installs (or causes to be installed) any part or accessory on such vehicle,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such installation is not later than the date 6 months
 after the date the vehicle was 1st placed in service, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] then there is hereby imposed on such installation a
 tax equal to 10 percent of the price of such part or accessory and its
 installation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) LIMITATION- The tax imposed by paragraph (1) on the
 installation of any part or accessory shall not exceed 10 percent of the
 excess (if any) of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the sum of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the price of such part or accessory and its
 installation, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the aggregate price of the parts and accessories
 (and their installation) installed before such part or accessory, plus
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) the price for which the passenger vehicle was sold,
 over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) $30,000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) EXCEPTIONS- Paragraph (1) shall not apply if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the part or accessory installed is a replacement part
 or accessory, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the part or accessory is installed to enable or
 assist an individual with a disability to operate the vehicle, or to enter
 or exit the vehicle, by compensating for the effect of such disability, or
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) the aggregate price of the parts and accessories (and
 their installation) described in paragraph (1) with respect to the vehicle
 does not exceed $200 (or such other amount or amounts as the Secretary may
 by regulation prescribe). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) INSTALLERS SECONDARILY LIABLE FOR TAX- The owners
 of the trade or business installing the parts or accessories shall be
 secondarily liable for the tax imposed by this subsection. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) IMPOSITION OF TAX ON SALES, ETC., WITHIN 2 YEARS OF
 VEHICLES PURCHASED TAX-FREE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) no tax was imposed under this subchapter on the
 1st retail sale of any passenger vehicle by reason of its exempt use, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) within 2 years after the date of such 1st retail sale,
 such vehicle is resold by the purchaser or such purchaser makes a substantial
 nonexempt use of such vehicle, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] then such sale or use of such vehicle by such purchaser shall
 be treated as the 1st retail sale of such vehicle for a price equal to its
 fair market value at the time of such sale or use. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) EXEMPT USE- For purposes of this subsection, the term
 `exempt use' means any use of a vehicle if the 1st retail sale of such vehicle
 is not taxable under this subchapter by reason of such use. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) PARTS AND ACCESSORIES SOLD WITH TAXABLE ARTICLE-
 Parts and accessories sold on, in connection with, or with the sale of any
 passenger vehicle shall be treated as part of the vehicle. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) PARTIAL PAYMENTS, ETC- In the case of a contract, sale,
 or arrangement described in paragraph (2), (3), or (4) of section 4216(c),
 rules similar to the rules of section 4217(e)(2) shall apply for purposes
 of this subchapter.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) TECHNICAL AMENDMENTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1)  Subsection (c) of section 4221 is amended by striking
 `4002(b), 4003(c), 4004(a)' and inserting `4001(d)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) Subsection (d) of section 4222 is amended by striking
 `4002(b), 4003(c), 4004(a)' and inserting `4001(d)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (3) The table of subchapters for chapter 31 is amended
 by striking the item relating to subchapter A and inserting the following:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subchapter A. Luxury passenger vehicles.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall take effect on February 1, 1992. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 2502. TAX ON DIESEL FUEL USED IN NONCOMMERCIAL
 MOTORBOATS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) Paragraph (2) of section 4092(a) (defining diesel
 fuel) is amended by striking `or a diesel-powered train' and inserting `,
 a diesel-powered train, or a diesel-powered motorboat'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) Paragraph (1) of section 4041(a) is amended--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) by striking `diesel-powered highway vehicle' each place
 it appears and inserting `diesel-powered highway vehicle or diesel-powered
 motorboat', and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) by striking `such vehicle' and inserting `such vehicle
 or motorboat'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (3) Subparagraph (B) of section 4092(b)(1) is amended by
 striking `commercial and noncommercial vessels' each place it appears and
 inserting `vessels for use in an off-highway business use (as defined in
 section 6421(e)(2)(B))'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) EXEMPTION FOR USE IN FISHERIES OR COMMERCIAL NAVIGATION-
 Subparagraph (B) of section 6421(e)(2) is amended to read as follows:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) USES IN MOTORBOATS- The term `off-highway business
 use' does not include any use in a motorboat; except that such term shall
 include any use in-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) a vessel employed in the fisheries or in the whaling
 business, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) a motorboat in the active conduct of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) a trade or business of commercial fishing or
 transporting persons or property for compensation or hire, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) any other trade or business unless the motorboat is
 used predominantly in any activity which is of a type generally considered
 to constitute entertainment, amusement or recreation.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) Retention of Taxes in General Fund-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) TAXES IMPOSED AT HIGHWAY TRUST FUND FINANCING RATE-
 Paragraph (4) of section 9503(b) (relating to transfers to Highway Trust
 Fund) is amended-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) by striking `and' at the end of subparagraph (A),
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) by striking the period at the end of subparagraph (B)
 and inserting `, and', and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (C) by adding at the end thereof the following new
 subparagraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) there shall not be taken into account the taxes
 imposed by sections 4041 and 4091 on diesel fuel sold for use or used as
 fuel in a diesel-powered motorboat.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) TAXES IMPOSED AT LEAKING UNDERGROUND STORAGE TANK TRUST
 FUND FINANCING RATE- Subsection (b) of section 9508 (relating to transfers
 to Leaking Underground Storage Tank Trust Fund) is amended by adding at the

 there shall not be taken into account the taxes imposed by sections 4041
 and 4091 on diesel fuel sold for use or used as fuel in a diesel-powered
 motorboat.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (d) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall take effect on July 1, 1992. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] Subtitle G--Urban Tax Enterprise Zones and Rural Development
 Investment Zones [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 2601. STATEMENT OF PURPOSE. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   It is the purpose of this subtitle to establish a
 demonstration program of providing incentives for the creation of tax
 enterprise zones in order-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) to revitalize economically and physically distressed
 areas, primarily by encouraging the formation of new businesses and the
 retention and expansion of existing businesses, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) to promote meaningful employment for tax enterprise
 zone residents, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (3) to encourage individuals to reside in the tax enterprise
 zones in which they are employed. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] PART I--DESIGNATION AND TAX INCENTIVES [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 2602. DESIGNATION AND TREATMENT OF URBAN TAX ENTERPRISE
 ZONES AND RURAL DEVELOPMENT INVESTMENT ZONES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Chapter 1 (relating to normal taxes and
 surtaxes) is amended by inserting after subchapter T the following new
 subchapter: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subchapter U--Designation and Treatment of Tax Enterprise
 Zones [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Part I. Designation of tax enterprise zones. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Part II. Incentives for tax enterprise zones. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `PART I--DESIGNATION OF TAX ENTERPRISE ZONES [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1391. Designation procedure. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1392. Eligibility and selection criteria. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1393. Definitions and special rules. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1391. DESIGNATION PROCEDURE. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this title, the term `tax
 enterprise zone' means any area which is, under this part-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) nominated by 1 or more local governments and the
 State in which it is located for designation as a tax enterprise zone, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) designated by-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the Secretary of Housing and Urban Development in
 the case of an urban tax enterprise zone, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the Secretary of Agriculture, in consultation with
 the Secretary of Commerce, in the case of a rural development investment
 zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) NUMBER OF DESIGNATIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) AGGREGATE LIMIT- The appropriate Secretaries may
 designate in the aggregate 35 nominated areas as tax enterprise zones under
 this section, subject to the availability of eligible nominated areas. Not
 more than 10 urban tax enterprise zones may be designated and not more than
 25 rural development investment zones may be designated. Such designations may
 be made only during the calendar years 1993, 1994, and 1995. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) ANNUAL LIMITS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) URBAN TAX ENTERPRISE ZONES- The number of urban tax
 enterprise zones designated under paragraph (1)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) in calendar year 1993 shall not exceed 5, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) in calendar year 1994 shall not exceed the sum of
 3 plus the carryover amount for such year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) in calendar year 1995 shall not exceed the sum of
 2 plus the carryover amount for such year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) RURAL DEVELOPMENT INVESTMENT ZONES- The number of rural
 development investment zones designated under paragraph (1)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) in calendar year 1993 shall not exceed 12, [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) in calendar year 1994 shall not exceed the sum of
 7 plus the carryover amount for such year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) in calendar year 1995 shall not exceed the sum of
 6 plus the carryover amount for such year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) CARRYOVER AMOUNT- For purposes of subparagraphs (A)
 and (B), the carryover amount for any calendar year shall be equal to the
 amount by which-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the limitation under such subparagraph for the
 preceding calendar year, exceeds [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the number of designations made under paragraph (1)
 for the type of tax enterprise zone to which such subparagraph relates in
 such preceding calendar year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) ADVANCE DESIGNATIONS PERMITTED- For purposes of this
 subchapter, a designation during any calendar year shall be treated as made
 on January 1 of the following calendar year if the appropriate Secretary,
 in making such designation, specifies that such designation is effective
 as of such January 1. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) LIMITATIONS ON DESIGNATIONS- The appropriate Secretary
 may not make any designation under subsection (a) unless-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) the local governments and the State in which the
 nominated area is located have the authority-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) to nominate the area for designation as a tax enterprise
 zone, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) to provide assurances satisfactory to the appropriate
 Secretary that the commitments under section 1392(c) will be fulfilled,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the local governments and the State in which the
 nominated area is located-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) have designated a governmental official with
 responsibility for making allocations under section 1397A (relating to
 overall limitation on zone incentives), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) have established procedures to ensure that allocations
 under section 1397A are made in a manner designed primarily to increase
 economic activity in the tax enterprise zone over that which would otherwise
 have occurred, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) a nomination of the area is submitted in a reasonable
 time before the calendar year for which designation as a tax enterprise
 zone is sought, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) the appropriate Secretary determines that any
 information furnished is reasonably accurate, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) the State and local governments certify that no
 portion of the area nominated is already included in a tax enterprise zone
 or in an area otherwise nominated to be a tax enterprise zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) PERIOD FOR WHICH DESIGNATION IS IN EFFECT-  [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Any designation of an area as a tax
 enterprise zone shall remain in effect during the period beginning on the
 date of the designation and ending on the earliest of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) December 31 of the 15th calendar year following the
 calendar year in which such date occurs, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the termination date designated by the State and
 local governments as provided for in their nomination, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) the date the appropriate Secretary revokes the
 designation under paragraph (2). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) REVOCATION OF DESIGNATION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The appropriate Secretary shall revoke the
 designation of an area as a tax enterprise zone if such Secretary determines
 that the local government or the State in which it is located-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) has significantly modified the boundaries of the area,
 or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) is not complying substantially with the State and
 local commitments pursuant to section 1392(c). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) APPLICABLE PROCEDURES- A designation may be revoked
 by the appropriate Secretary under subparagraph (A) only after a hearing
 on the record involving officials of the State or local government
 involved. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1392. ELIGIBILITY AND SELECTION CRITERIA. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) IN GENERAL- The appropriate Secretary may make a
 designation of any nominated area under section 1391 only on the basis of the
 eligibility and selection criteria set forth in this section. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) URBAN TAX ENTERPRISE ZONES- A nominated area which
 is not a rural area shall be eligible for designation under section 1391
 only if it meets the following criteria: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) POPULATION- The nominated area has a population
 (as determined by the most recent census data available) of not less than
 4,000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) DISTRESS- The nominated area is one of pervasive
 poverty, unemployment, and general distress. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SIZE- The nominated area-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) does not exceed 12 square miles, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) has a boundary which is continuous, or consists of
 not more than 3 noncontiguous parcels, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) is located entirely within 1 State. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) UNEMPLOYMENT RATE- The unemployment rate (as determined
 by the appropriate available data) is not less than 1.5 times the national
 unemployment rate. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) POVERTY RATE- The poverty rate (as determined
 by the most recent census data available) for not less than 90 percent
 of the population census tracts (or where not tracted, the equivalent
 county divisions as defined by the Bureau of the Census for the purposes
 of defining poverty areas) within the nominated area is not less than 20
 percent. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(F) COURSE OF ACTION- There has been adopted for the
 nominated area a course of action which meets the requirements of subsection
 (c). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) RURAL DEVELOPMENT INVESTMENT ZONES- A nominated area
 which is a rural area shall be eligible for designation under section 1391
 only if it meets the following criteria: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) POPULATION- The nominated area has a population
 (as determined by the most recent census data available) of not less than
 1,000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) DISTRESS- The nominated area is one of general
 distress. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SIZE- The nominated area-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) does not exceed 10,000 square miles, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) consists of areas within not more than 4 contiguous
 counties, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) has a boundary which is continuous, or consists of
 not more than 3 noncontiguous parcels, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) except in the case of nominated areas located in 1 or
 more Indian reservations, is located entirely within 1 State. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) ADDITIONAL CRITERIA- Not less than 2 of the following
 criteria: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) UNEMPLOYMENT RATE- The criterion set forth in paragraph
 (1)(D). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) POVERTY RATE- The criterion set forth in paragraph
 (1)(E). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) JOB LOSS- The amount of wages attributable to
 employment in the area, and subject to tax under section 3301 during the
 preceding calendar year, is not more than 95 percent of such wages during
 the 5th preceding calendar year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) OUT-MIGRATION- The population of the area decreased
 (as determined by the most recent census data available) by 10 percent or
 more between 1980 and 1990. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) COURSE OF ACTION- There has been adopted for the
 nominated area a course of action which meets the requirements of subsection
 (c). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) REQUIRED STATE AND LOCAL COURSE OF ACTION-  [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- No nominated area may be designated as a
 tax enterprise zone unless the local government and the State in which it
 is located agree in writing that, during any period during which the area
 is a tax enterprise zone, the governments will follow a specified course
 of action designed to reduce the various burdens borne by employers or
 employees in the area. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) COURSE OF ACTION- The course of action under paragraph
 (1) may be implemented by both governments and private nongovernmental
 entities, may not be funded from proceeds of any Federal program, and may
 include-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) a reduction of tax rates or fees applying within the
 tax enterprise zone, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) an increase in the level, or efficiency of delivery,
 of local public services within the tax enterprise zone, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) actions to reduce, remove, simplify, or streamline
 government paperwork requirements applicable within the tax enterprise zone,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) the involvement in the program by public authorities
 or private entities, organizations, neighborhood associations, and community
 groups, particularly those within the nominated area, including a written
 commitment to provide jobs and job training for, and technical, financial,
 or other assistance to, employers, employees, and residents of the nominated
 area, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) the giving of special preference to contractors owned
 and operated by members of any minority, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(F) the gift (or sale at below fair market value) of
 surplus land in the tax enterprise zone to neighborhood organizations
 agreeing to operate a business on the land, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(G) the establishment of a program under which employers
 within the tax enterprise zone may purchase health insurance for their
 employees on a pooled basis, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(H) the establishment of a program to encourage local
 financial institutions to satisfy their obligations under the Community
 Reinvestment Act of 1977 (12 U.S.C. 2901 et seq.) by making loans
 to tax enterprise zone businesses, with emphasis on startup and other
 small-business concerns (as defined in section 3(a) of the Small Business
 Act (15 U.S.C. 632(a)), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) the giving of special preference to qualified low-income
 housing projects located in tax enterprise zones, in the allocation of the
 State housing credit ceiling applicable under section 42, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(J) the giving of special preference to facilities located
 in tax enterprise zones, in the allocation of the State ceiling on private
 activity bonds applicable under section 146. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) RECOGNITION OF PAST EFFORTS- In evaluating courses of
 action agreed to by any State or local government, the appropriate Secretary
 shall take into account the past efforts of the State or local government
 in reducing the various burdens borne by employers and employees in the
 area involved. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) PROHIBITION OF ASSISTANCE FOR BUSINESS RELOCATIONS-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The course of action implemented under
 paragraph (1) may not include any action to assist any establishment in
 relocating from 1 area to another area. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) EXCEPTION- The limitation established in subparagraph
 (A) shall not be construed to prohibit assistance for the expansion of
 an existing business entity through the establishment of a new branch,
 affiliate, or subsidiary if the appropriate Secretary-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) finds that the establishment of the new branch,
 affiliate, or subsidiary will not result in an increase in unemployment
 in the area of original location or in any other area where the existing
 business entity conducts business operations, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) has no reason to believe that the new branch,
 affiliate, or subsidiary is being established with the intention of closing
 down the operations of the existing business entity in the area of its
 original location or in any other area where the existing business entity
 conducts business operations. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) SELECTION CRITERIA- From among the nominated areas
 eligible for designation under subsection (b) by the appropriate Secretary,
 such appropriate Secretary shall make designations of tax enterprise zones
 on the basis of the following factors (each of which is to be given equal
 weight): [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) STATE AND LOCAL CONTRIBUTIONS- The strength and
 quality of the contributions which have been promised as part of the course
 of action relative to the fiscal ability of the nominating State and local
 governments. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) IMPLEMENTATION OF COURSE OF ACTION- The effectiveness
 and enforceability of the guarantees that the course of action will actually
 be carried out. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) PRIVATE COMMITMENTS- The level of commitments by
 private entities of additional resources and contributions to the economy
 of the nominated area, including the creation of new or expanded business
 activities. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) AVERAGE RANKINGS- The average ranking with respect to--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the criteria set forth in subparagraphs (D) and (E)
 of subsection (b)(1), in the case of an area which is not a rural area, or
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the 2 criteria set forth in subsection (b)(2)(D)
 that give the area a higher average ranking, in the case of a rural
 area. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) REVITALIZATION POTENTIAL- The potential for the
 revitalization of the nominated area as a result of zone designation,
 taking into account particularly the number of jobs to be created and
 retained. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1393. DEFINITIONS AND SPECIAL RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `For purposes of this subchapter-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) URBAN TAX ENTERPRISE ZONE- The term `urban tax
 enterprise zone' means a tax enterprise zone which meets the requirements
 of section 1392(b)(1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) RURAL DEVELOPMENT INVESTMENT ZONE- The term `rural
 development investment zone' means a tax enterprise zone which meets the
 requirements of section 1392(b)(2). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) GOVERNMENTS- If more than 1 local government seeks to
 nominate an area as a tax enterprise zone, any reference to, or requirement
 of, this subchapter shall apply to all such governments. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) LOCAL GOVERNMENT- The term `local government' means--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any county, city, town, township, parish, village,
 or other general purpose political subdivision of a State, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any combination of political subdivisions described
 in subparagraph (A) recognized by the appropriate Secretary. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) NOMINATED AREA-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The term `nominated area' means an
 area which is nominated by 1 or more local governments and the State in
 which it is located for designation as a tax enterprise zone under this
 subchapter. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) INDIAN RESERVATIONS- In the case of a nominated area
 on an Indian reservation, the reservation governing body (as determined
 by the Secretary of the Interior) shall be deemed to be both the State and
 local governments with respect to the area. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(6) RURAL AREA- The term `rural area' means any area
 which is-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) outside of a metropolitan statistical area (within
 the meaning of section 143(k)(2)(B)), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) determined by the Secretary of Agriculture, after
 consultation with the Secretary of Commerce, to be a rural area. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(7) APPROPRIATE SECRETARY- The term `appropriate Secretary'
 means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the Secretary of Housing and Urban Development in
 the case of urban tax enterprise zones, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the Secretary of Agriculture in the case of rural
 development investment zones. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(8) STATE-CHARTERED DEVELOPMENT CORPORATIONS- An area shall
 be treated as nominated by a State and a local government if it is nominated
 by an economic development corporation chartered by the State. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `PART II--INCENTIVES FOR TAX ENTERPRISE ZONES [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SUBPART A. Enterprise zone employment credit. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SUBPART B. Investment incentives. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SUBPART C. General provisions. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart A--Enterprise Zone Employment Credit [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1394. Enterprise zone employment credit. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1395. Other definitions and special rules. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1394. ENTERPRISE ZONE EMPLOYMENT CREDIT. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) AMOUNT OF CREDIT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of section 38, the amount of
 the enterprise zone employment credit determined under this section with
 respect to any small employer for any taxable year is 7.5 percent of the
 qualified zone wages paid or incurred during such taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) LIMITATION- The amount of the enterprise zone employment
 credit of any small employer for any taxable year with respect to any tax
 enterprise zone shall not exceed the employment credit amount allocated
 to such employer for such taxable year under section 1397A with respect to
 such zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) QUALIFIED ZONE WAGES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this section, the term
 `qualified zone wages' means any wages paid or incurred by a small employer
 for services performed by an employee while such employee is a qualified
 zone employee. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) COORDINATION WITH TARGETED JOBS CREDIT- The term
 `qualified wages' shall not include wages attributable to service rendered
 during the 1-year period beginning with the day the individual begins
 work for the employer if any portion of such wages are qualified wages
 (as defined in section 51(b)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) QUALIFIED ZONE EMPLOYEE- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 subsection, the term `qualified zone employee' means, with respect to any
 period, any employee of a small employer if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) substantially all of the services performed during
 such period by such employee for such employer are performed within a tax
 enterprise zone in a trade or business of the employer, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the principal place of abode of such employee while
 performing such services is within such tax enterprise zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CREDIT ALLOWED ONLY FOR FIRST 5 YEARS- An employee
 shall not be treated as a qualified zone employee for any period after the
 date 5 years after the day on which such employee first began work for the
 employer (whether or not in a tax enterprise zone). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) INDIVIDUALS RECEIVING WAGES IN EXCESS OF $30,000 NOT
 ELIGIBLE- An employee shall not be treated as a qualified zone employee for
 any taxable year of the employer if the total amount of the wages paid or
 incurred by such employer to such employee during such taxable year (whether
 or not for services in a tax enterprise zone) exceeds the amount determined
 at an annual rate of $30,000. The Secretary shall adjust the $30,000 amount
 contained in the preceding sentence for years beginning after 1992 at the
 same time and in the same manner as under section 415(d). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) CERTAIN INDIVIDUALS NOT ELIGIBLE- The term `qualified
 zone employee' shall not include-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any individual described in subparagraph (A), (B),
 or (C) of section 51(i)(1), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any 5-percent owner (as defined in section
 416(i)(1)(B)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) SMALL EMPLOYER- For purposes of this section, the term
 `small employer' means, with respect to any taxable year, any employer if
 the average number of individuals employed full-time (within the meaning
 of the last sentence of section 44(b)) during such taxable year by such
 employer does not exceed 100. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) EARLY TERMINATION OF EMPLOYMENT BY EMPLOYER-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If the employment of any employee is
 terminated by the taxpayer before the day 1 year after the day on which
 such employee began work for the employer-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) no wages with respect to such employee shall be
 taken into account under subsection (a) for the taxable year in which such
 employment is terminated, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the tax under this chapter for the taxable year in which
 such employment is terminated shall be increased by the aggregate credits
 (if any) allowed under section 38(a) for prior taxable years by reason of
 wages taken into account with respect to such employee. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CARRYBACKS AND CARRYOVERS ADJUSTED- In the case of
 any termination of employment to which paragraph (1) applies, the carrybacks
 and carryovers under section 39 shall be properly adjusted. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) SUBSECTION NOT TO APPLY IN CERTAIN CASES-  [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- Paragraph (1) shall not apply to--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) a termination of employment of an employee who
 voluntarily leaves the employment of the taxpayer, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) a termination of employment of an individual who
 before the close of the period referred to in paragraph (1) becomes disabled
 to perform the services of such employment unless such disability is removed
 before the close of such period and the taxpayer fails to offer reemployment
 to such individual, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) a termination of employment of an individual if it
 is determined under the applicable State unemployment compensation law that
 the termination was due to the misconduct of such individual. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) CHANGES IN FORM OF BUSINESS- For purposes of paragraph
 (1), the employment relationship between the taxpayer and an employee shall
 not be treated as terminated-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) by a transaction to which section 381(a) applies
 if the employee continues to be employed by the acquiring corporation, or
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) by reason of a mere change in the form of conducting
 the trade or business of the taxpayer if the employee continues to be
 employed in such trade or business and the taxpayer retains a substantial
 interest in such trade or business. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) SPECIAL RULE- Any increase in tax under paragraph
 (1) shall not be treated as a tax imposed by this chapter for purposes of--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) determining the amount of any credit allowable under
 this chapter, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) determining the amount of the tax imposed by section
 55. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1395. OTHER DEFINITIONS AND SPECIAL RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) WAGES- For purposes of this subpart, the term `wages'
 has the same meaning as when used in section 51 except that paragraph (4)
 of section 51(c) shall not apply. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) CONTROLLED GROUPS- For purposes of this subpart--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) all employers treated as a single employer under
 subsection (a) or (b) of section 52 shall be treated as a single employer
 for purposes of this subpart, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the credit (if any) determined under section 1394
 with respect to each such employer shall be its proportionate share of the
 wages giving rise to such credit. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) CERTAIN OTHER RULES MADE APPLICABLE- For purposes of
 this subpart, rules similar to the rules of section 51(k) and subsections
 (c), (d), and (e) of section 52 shall apply. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart B--Investment Incentives [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1396. Enterprise zone stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1397. Additional first-year depreciation
 allowance. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1396. ENTERPRISE ZONE STOCK. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) GENERAL RULE- In the case of an individual, there
 shall be allowed as a deduction an amount equal to the aggregate amount
 paid in cash by the taxpayer during the taxable year for the purchase of
 enterprise zone stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) LIMITATIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) CEILING-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The maximum amount allowed as a deduction
 under subsection (a) to a taxpayer shall not exceed whichever of the
 following is the least for the taxable year: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) $25,000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) The enterprise zone stock amount allocated under
 section 1397A to the taxpayer for such taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) The excess of $250,000 over the amount allowed
 as a deduction under this section to the taxpayer for all prior taxable
 years. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) EXCESS AMOUNTS- If the amount otherwise deductible by
 any person under subsection (a) exceeds the limitation under subparagraph
 (A)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the amount of such excess shall be treated as an
 amount paid to which subsection (a) applies during the next taxable year,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the deduction allowed for any taxable year shall
 be allocated among the enterprise zone stock purchased by such person in
 accordance with the purchase price per share. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) AGGREGATION WITH FAMILY MEMBERS- The taxpayer and
 members of the taxpayer's family (as defined in section 267(c)(4)) shall be
 treated as one person for purposes of clauses (i) and (iii) of paragraph
 (1)(A), and the limitations contained in such clauses shall be allocated
 among the taxpayer and such members in accordance with their respective
 purchases of enterprise zone stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) DISPOSITIONS OF STOCK-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) GAIN TREATED AS ORDINARY INCOME- Except as otherwise
 provided in regulations, if a taxpayer disposes of any enterprise zone
 stock with respect to which a deduction was allowed under subsection (a),
 the amount realized on such disposition-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) shall be recognized notwithstanding any other provision
 of this subtitle, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) to the extent such amount does not exceed the amount
 allowed as a deduction under subsection (a) with respect to such stock,
 shall be treated as ordinary income. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) INTEREST CHARGED IF DISPOSITION WITHIN 5 YEARS OF
 PURCHASE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If a taxpayer disposes of any enterprise
 zone stock with respect to which a deduction was allowed under subsection
 (a) before the end of the 5-year period beginning on the date such stock
 was purchased by the taxpayer, the tax imposed by this chapter for the
 taxable year in which such disposition occurs shall be increased by the
 amount determined under subparagraph (B). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) ADDITIONAL AMOUNT- For purposes of subparagraph (A), the
 additional amount shall be equal to the amount of interest (determined at the
 rate applicable under section 6621(a)(2)) that would accrue-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) during the period beginning on the date the stock was
 purchased by the taxpayer and ending on the date such stock was disposed
 of by the taxpayer, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) on an amount equal to the aggregate decrease in tax
 of the taxpayer resulting from the deduction allowed under this subsection
 (a) with respect to the stock so disposed of. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SPECIAL RULE- Any increase in tax under subparagraph
 (A) shall not be treated as a tax imposed by this chapter for purposes of--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) determining the amount of any credit allowable under
 this chapter, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) determining the amount of the tax imposed by section
 55. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) EXCEPTION FOR TRANSFERS AT DEATH- This subsection
 shall not apply to a transfer at death. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) DISQUALIFICATION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) ISSUER OR STOCK CEASES TO QUALIFY- If, during the
 10-year period beginning on the date enterprise zone stock was purchased
 by the taxpayer-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the issuer of such stock ceases to be a qualified
 issuer (determined without regard to subsection (f)(1)(C)), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the proceeds from the issuance of such stock fail or
 otherwise cease to be invested by the issuer in qualified enterprise zone
 property, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] then, notwithstanding any provision of this subtitle other
 than paragraph (2), the taxpayer shall be treated for purposes of subsection
 (c) as disposing of such stock during the taxable year during which such
 cessation or failure occurs at its fair market value as of 1st day of such
 taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CESSATION OF ENTERPRISE ZONE STATUS NOT TO CAUSE
 RECAPTURE- A corporation shall not fail to be treated as a qualified
 issuer for purposes of paragraph (1) solely by reason of the termination
 or revocation of a tax enterprise zone designation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) ENTERPRISE ZONE STOCK- For purposes of this section,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The term `enterprise zone stock' means
 stock of a corporation if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such stock was acquired on original issue from the
 corporation, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such corporation was, at the time of issue, a qualified
 issuer. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) PROCEEDS MUST BE INVESTED IN QUALIFIED ENTERPRISE
 ZONE PROPERTY- Such term shall include such stock only to the extent that
 the amount of proceeds of such issuance are used by such issuer during
 the 12-month period beginning on the date of issuance to acquire qualified
 enterprise zone property. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) $5,000,000 LIMIT- Not more than $5,000,000 of
 stock of such corporation and all related persons may be enterprise zone
 stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) QUALIFIED ISSUER- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The term `qualified issuer' means any
 domestic C corporation if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such corporation does not have more than one class
 of stock, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such corporation meets the enterprise zone business
 requirements of paragraph (2), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) the sum of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the money, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the aggregate unadjusted bases of property owned by
 such corporation, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) the value of property leased to the corporation
 (as determined under regulations prescribed by the Secretary), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] does not exceed $5,000,000, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) more than 20 percent of the total voting power, and
 20 percent of the total value, of the stock of such corporation is owned
 by individuals or estates or indirectly by individuals through partnerships
 or trusts. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) ENTERPRISE ZONE BUSINESS REQUIREMENTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- A corporation meets the enterprise
 zone business requirements of this paragraph for any taxable year if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) at least 80 percent of the total gross income of such
 corporation for the taxable year is derived from the active conduct of a
 trade or business within a tax enterprise zone, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) less than 10 percent of the average of the aggregate
 unadjusted bases of the property of the corporation during such taxable
 year is attributable to securities (as defined in section 165(g)(2)),
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) substantially all of the use of the tangible property
 of the corporation (whether owned or leased) is within a tax enterprise zone,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) substantially all of the services performed for the
 corporation by the employees of such corporation are performed in a tax
 enterprise zone, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(v) no more than an insubstantial portion of the property of
 the corporation constitutes collectibles (as defined in section 408(m)(2)),
 unless such collectibles constitute property held primarily for sale to
 customers in the ordinary course of such trade or business. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) Special rules-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) RENTAL REAL PROPERTY- For purposes of subparagraph
 (A), real property located within a tax enterprise zone and held for use by
 customers other than related persons shall be treated as the active conduct
 of a trade or business. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) EXCESSIVE PROPERTY OR SERVICES PROVIDED TO OR BY
 RELATED PERSONS- A corporation shall cease to meet the requirements of this
 paragraph if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) more than 50 percent (by value) of the property or
 services acquired by the corporation during the taxable year are acquired
 from related persons which do not meet the requirements of this paragraph;
 or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) more than 50 percent of the gross income of the
 corporation for the taxable year is attributable to property or services
 provided to related persons which do not meet the requirements of this
 paragraph. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) NEW CORPORATIONS- In the case of a new corporation,
 clauses (i) and (ii) of subparagraph (A) shall not apply to the 1st taxable
 year of such corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) QUALIFIED ENTERPRISE ZONE PROPERTY- The term `qualified
 enterprise zone property' means property to which section 168 applies--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the original use of which commences with the qualified
 issuer, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) substantially all of the use of which is in a tax
 enterprise zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) RELATED PERSON- A person shall be treated as related
 to another person if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the relationship of such persons is described in
 section 267(b) or 707(b)(1), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such persons are engaged in trades or businesses
 under common control (within the meaning of subsections (a) and (b) of
 section 52). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of subparagraph (A), in applying section 267(b) or
 707(b)(1), `33 percent' shall be substituted for `50 percent'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(g) BASIS ADJUSTMENT- For purposes of this subtitle,
 the taxpayer's basis (without regard to this subsection) for the enterprise
 zone stock shall be reduced by the deduction allowed under subsection (a)
 with respect to such stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1397. ADDITIONAL FIRST-YEAR DEPRECIATION
 ALLOWANCE. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) IN GENERAL- In the case of any qualified zone property--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) the depreciation deduction provided by section 167(a)
 for the taxable year in which such property is placed in service shall
 include an allowance equal to 25 percent of the adjusted basis of such
 property, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the adjusted basis of such property shall be reduced by
 the amount of such allowance before computing the amount otherwise allowable
 as a depreciation deduction under this chapter for such taxable year and
 any subsequent taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) QUALIFIED ZONE PROPERTY- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The term `qualified zone property' means
 any property to which section 168 applies-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) which is section 1245 property (as defined in section
 1245(a)(3)), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the original use of which commences with the taxpayer
 in a tax enterprise zone, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) substantially all of the use of which is in a tax
 enterprise zone and is in the active conduct of a trade or business by the
 taxpayer in such zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) EXCEPTION FOR ALTERNATIVE DEPRECIATION PROPERTY- The
 term `qualified zone property' does not include any property to which the
 alternative depreciation system under section 168(g) applies, determined--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) without regard to section 168(g)(7) (relating to
 election to use alternative depreciation system), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) after application of section 280F(b) (relating to
 listed property with limited business use). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) LIMITATION- The aggregate adjusted bases of property
 which may be taken into account under subsection (a) by any taxpayer for any
 taxable year with respect to any tax enterprise zone shall not exceed the
 additional first-year depreciation amount allocated to such taxpayer for such
 taxable year under section 1397A with respect to such zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) SPECIAL RULES FOR SALE-LEASEBACKS- For purposes of
 subsection (b)(1)(B), if property is sold and leased back by the taxpayer
 within 3 months after the date such property was originally placed in service,
 such property shall be treated as originally placed in service not earlier
 than the date on which such property is used under the leaseback. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 280F-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) AUTOMOBILES- In the case of a passenger automobile
 (within the meaning of section 280F(d)(5)) which is qualified zone property,
 the Secretary shall increase the limitation under section 280F(a)(1)(A)(i),
 and decrease each other limitation under subparagraphs (A) and (B) of
 section 280F(a)(1), to appropriately reflect the amount of the allowance
 under subsection (a). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) LISTED PROPERTY- The allowance under subsection (a)
 shall be taken into account in computing any recapture amount under section
 280F(b)(2). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 169(j)- In the case of
 property for which a deduction would (but for this subsection) be allowable
 under section 168(j) and this section, section 168(j) shall not apply and
 this section shall be applied by substituting `40 percent' for `25 percent'
 in subsection (a). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart C--General Provisions [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1397A. Overall limitation on zone incentives. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1397B. Regulations. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1397A. OVERALL LIMITATION ON ZONE INCENTIVES. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) GENERAL RULE- The allocating official of each tax
 enterprise zone shall make allocations of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) employment credit amounts, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) enterprise zone stock amounts, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) additional first-year depreciation amounts. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) LIMITATION ON AGGREGATE AMOUNTS ALLOCATED-  [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) LIMITATION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- No amount may be allocated under subsection
 (a) by the allocating official of any tax enterprise zone if such allocation
 would result in the zone limit for the calendar year of the allocation
 (or any succeeding calendar year) being reduced below zero. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) COORDINATION WITH INCREASE- For purposes of applying
 subparagraph (A) to an allocation during any calendar year, it shall be
 assumed that no increase in the zone limit will be made under paragraph
 (2)(B) for any succeeding calendar year unless-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the allocating official provides assurances satisfactory
 to the Secretary that the zone will be entitled to such an increase for
 such succeeding calendar year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the allocating official agrees to such recapture
 provisions as the Secretary may require in cases where the zone is not
 entitled to such increase. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) ZONE LIMIT- For purposes of this section-- [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) BASIC AMOUNT- Except as otherwise provided in this
 paragraph, the zone limit for any tax enterprise zone for any calendar year
 is-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) $13,000,000 in the case of an urban tax enterprise
 zone, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) $5,000,000 in the case of a rural development
 investment zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) INCREASE IN LIMIT FOR CERTAIN STATE OR LOCAL
 EXPENDITURES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- The amount of the zone limit for any tax
 enterprise zone for any calendar year shall be increased by the lesser of--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) 10 percent of the limit determined under subparagraph
 (A), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the amount determined under clause (ii) with respect
 to such zone for such calendar year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) AMOUNT OF INCREASE- For purposes of clause (i),
 the amount determined under this clause with respect to any tax enterprise
 zone for any calendar year is the sum of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) the State and local business incentives with respect
 to such zone for the preceding calendar year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the qualified State and local governmental expenditures
 with respect to such zone for the preceding calendar year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) CARRYOVER OF UNUSED AMOUNTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- Before the end of any calendar year,
 the allocating official of any tax enterprise zone may elect-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) to reduce the zone limit applicable to such zone for
 such year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) to increase the zone limit applicable to such zone for
 the succeeding calendar year by an amount equal to such reduction. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) LIMITATION- The increase in a zone limit under clause
 (i)(II) for any calendar year shall not exceed 70 percent of the zone limit
 otherwise applicable to the tax enterprise zone for such year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) DEFINITIONS- For purposes of this subsection--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) STATE AND LOCAL BUSINESS INCENTIVES- The State and
 local business incentives with respect to any tax enterprise zone for any
 calendar year is the sum of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the aggregate of property tax or sales tax abatements
 provided during State or local fiscal years ending in such calendar year with
 respect to otherwise taxable property or sales in such tax enterprise zone,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the aggregate grants made by any State or local
 government during such fiscal years to startup and other small business
 concerns in such tax enterprise zone, plus [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) 5 percent of the total outstanding balance (as
 of the close of such fiscal years) of loans made by any State or local
 government to startup and other small business concerns in such tax enterprise
 zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] No amount shall be taken into account under the preceding
 sentence if such amount consists of assistance which would be prohibited
 under section 1392(c)(4) (relating to prohibition of assistance for business
 relocations). No loan shall be taken into account under clause (iii) unless
 the State or local government bears the risk of any default with respect
 to such loan. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) QUALIFIED STATE AND LOCAL GOVERNMENTAL EXPENDITURES-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- The qualified State and local governmental
 expenditures with respect to any tax enterprise zone for any calendar year
 shall be the excess (if any) of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) the specified expenditures during State or local
 fiscal years ending in such calendar year with respect to such zone, over
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the adjusted base period expenditures for such
 zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) SPECIFIED EXPENDITURES- For purposes of this
 subparagraph, the term `specified expenditures' means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) any expenditures by any State or local government for
 the acquisition, construction, repair, or maintenance of public improvements
 or facilities in the tax enterprise zone, plus [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) any expenditures by any State or local government
 for police or fire protection to the extent allocable to the tax enterprise
 zone. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) ADJUSTED BASE PERIOD EXPENDITURES- For purposes
 of this subparagraph, the term `adjusted base period expenditures' means,
 with respect to any calendar year-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) the aggregate specified expenditures during State
 or local fiscal years ending in calendar year 1991 with respect to the tax
 enterprise zone, increased by [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the cost-of-living adjustment for the calendar year
 for which the increase is being determined (as determined under section
 1(f)(3) by substituting `calendar year 1990' for `calendar year 1991'
 in subparagraph (B) of such section). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) ADJUSTMENT FOR CERTAIN CAPITAL EXPENDITURES- For
 purposes of clause (iii)(I), the appropriate Secretary may disregard any
 expenditures if such Secretary determines that such expenditures were
 unusual and not recurring and that inclusion of such expenditures would
 not be consistent with the purposes of this section. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) DETERMINATIONS BY APPROPRIATE SECRETARY- The amount
 of the State and local business incentives and qualified State or local
 governmental expenditures with respect to any tax enterprise zone for
 any calendar year shall be determined by the appropriate Secretary with
 respect to such zone and certified to the Secretary of the Treasury or his
 delegate. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) SMALL BUSINESS CONCERN- The term `small business
 concern' has the meaning given such term by section 3(a) of the Small
 Business Act (15 U.S.C. 632(a)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) ALLOCATION PREFERENCE FOR SMALL BUSINESS CONCERNS-
 In making allocations under subsection (a), the allocating official of
 each tax enterprise zone shall give preference to small business concerns
 (as defined in subsection (b)(3)(D)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) OPERATING RULES- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) EMPLOYMENT CREDIT AMOUNT- Any allocation of an
 employment credit amount-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) shall specify the employer and taxable year to which
 such allocation applies, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) shall reduce the zone limit for the calendar year in
 which such taxable year begins by 67 cents for each dollar of the amount
 so allocated. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) ENTERPRISE ZONE STOCK AMOUNT- Any allocation of an
 enterprise zone stock amount-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) shall specify the stock purchases to which the
 allocation relates, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) shall reduce the zone limit for the calendar year in
 which such taxable year begins by 35 cents for each dollar of the amount
 so allocated. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) ADDITIONAL FIRST-YEAR DEPRECIATION AMOUNT- Any
 allocation of an additional first-year depreciation amount-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) shall specify the adjusted basis of the property to
 which such allocation applies, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) shall reduce the zone limit for the calendar year
 in which the property is placed in service by 1.5 cents for each dollar so
 allocated. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) RETROACTIVE ALLOCATIONS NOT EFFECTIVE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- No retroactive allocation under subsection
 (a) shall be effective. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) RETROACTIVE ALLOCATION- For purposes of subsection (a),
 the term `retroactive allocation' means any allocation of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) an employment credit amount after the beginning of
 the taxable year to which such allocation applies, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) an enterprise zone stock amount after the stock
 involved is acquired, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) an additional first-year depreciation amount after
 the property involved is placed in service. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) ALLOCATING OFFICIAL- For purposes of this section,
 the term `allocating official' means the official designated as provided
 in section 1391(c)(2) as the official responsible for making allocations
 under this section. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1397B. REGULATIONS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `The Secretary shall prescribe such regulations as may be
 necessary or appropriate to carry out the purposes of this part, including--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) regulations limiting the benefit of this part in
 circumstances where such benefits, in combination with benefits provided
 under other Federal programs, would result in an activity being 100 percent
 or more subsidized by the Federal Government, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) regulations preventing avoidance of the provisions
 of this part.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CLERICAL AMENDMENT- The table of subchapters for
 chapter 1 is amended by inserting after the item relating to subchapter T
 the following new item: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subchapter U. Designation and treatment of tax enterprise
 zones.' [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->]   (2) not later than July 1, 2001, a final report setting
 forth the findings as a result of such studies. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] SEC. 3003. SURTAX ON INDIVIDUALS WITH INCOMES OVER
 $1,000,000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Subchapter A of chapter 1 (relating to
 determination of tax liability) is amended by adding at the end thereof
 the following new part: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `PART VIII--SURTAX ON INDIVIDUALS WITH INCOMES OVER $1,000,000
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 59B. Surtax on section 1 tax. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 59C. Surtax on minimum tax. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 59D. Special rules. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 59B. SURTAX ON SECTION 1 TAX. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `In the case of an individual who has taxable income for
 the taxable year in excess of $1,000,000, the amount of the tax imposed
 under section 1 for such taxable year shall be increased by 10 percent of
 the amount which bears the same ratio to the tax imposed under section 1
 (determined without regard to this section) as-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) the amount by which the taxable income of such
 individual for such taxable year exceeds $1,000,000, bears to [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the total amount of such individual's taxable income
 for such taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 59C. SURTAX ON MINIMUM TAX. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `In the case of an individual who has alternative minimum
 taxable income for the taxable year in excess of $1,000,000, the amount of
 the tentative minimum tax determined under section 55 for such taxable year
 shall be increased by 2.5 percent of the amount by which the alternative
 minimum taxable income of such taxpayer for the taxable year exceeds
 $1,000,000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 59D. SPECIAL RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) SURTAX TO APPLY TO ESTATES AND TRUSTS- For purposes
 of this part, the term `individual' includes any estate or trust taxable
 under section 1. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) TREATMENT OF MARRIED INDIVIDUALS FILING SEPARATE
 RETURNS- In the case of a married individual (within the meaning of section
 7703) filing a separate return for the taxable year, sections 59B and 59C
 shall be applied by substituting `$500,000' for `$1,000,000'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) COORDINATION WITH OTHER PROVISIONS- The provisions
 of this part-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) shall be applied after the application of section 1(h),
 but [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) before the application of any other provision of
 this title which refers to the amount of tax imposed by section 1 or 55,
 as the case may be.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CLERICAL AMENDMENT- The table of parts for subchapter
 A of chapter 1 is amended by adding at the end the following new item:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Part VIII. Surtax on individuals with incomes over
 $1,000,000.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to taxable years beginning after December 31, 1991. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- For purposes of chapter 1 of the Internal
 Revenue Code of 1986-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) any FSLIC assistance with respect to any loss of

 taken into account for purposes of section 166, 585, or 593 of such Code in

 is worthless) and in determining the amount of any addition to a reserve
 for bad debts arising from the worthlessness or partial worthlessness of
 such debts. [<-Struck out]

 term `FSLIC assistance' means any assistance (or right to assistance) with

 not credited before March 4, 1991. [<-Struck out]

 1991, is with respect to a loss sustained or charge-off in a taxable year
 ending before March 4, 1991, for purposes of determining the amount of any
 net operating loss carryover to a taxable year ending after on or after
 March 4, 1991, the provisions of this section shall apply to such assistance
 for purposes of determining the amount of the net operating loss for the
 taxable year in which such loss was sustained or debt written off. Except
