 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Clause (i) of section 6231(a)(1)(B)
 (relating to exception for small partnerships) is amended to read as follows:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- The term `partnership' shall not include
 any partnership having 10 or fewer partners each of whom is an individual
 (other than a nonresident alien), a C corporation, or an estate of a deceased
 partner. For purposes of the preceding sentence, a husband and wife (and
 their estates) shall be treated as 1 partner.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendment made by this section
 shall apply to partnership taxable years ending after the date of the
 enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4315. EXCLUSION OF PARTIAL SETTLEMENTS FROM 1 YEAR
 LIMITATION ON ASSESSMENT. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Subsection (f) of section 6229 (relating
 to items becoming nonpartnership items) is amended-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) by striking `(f) ITEMS BECOMING NONPARTNERSHIP ITEMS-
 If' and inserting the following: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) SPECIAL RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) ITEMS BECOMING NONPARTNERSHIP ITEMS- If', [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) by moving the text of such subsection 2 ems to the
 right, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (3) by adding at the end thereof the following new paragraph:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULE FOR PARTIAL SETTLEMENT AGREEMENTS-
 If a partner enters into a settlement agreement with the Secretary with
 respect to the treatment of some of the partnership items in dispute for a
 partnership taxable year but other partnership items for such year remain
 in dispute, the period of limitations for assessing any tax attributable
 to the settled items shall be determined as if such agreement had not been
 entered into.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendment made by this section
 shall apply to partnership taxable years ending after the date of the
 enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4316. EXTENSION OF TIME FOR FILING A REQUEST FOR
 ADMINISTRATIVE ADJUSTMENT. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Section 6227 (relating to administrative
 adjustment requests) is amended by redesignating subsections (b) and (c)
 as subsections (c) and (d), respectively, and by inserting after subsection
 (a) the following new subsection: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) SPECIAL RULE IN CASE OF EXTENSION OF PERIOD OF
 LIMITATIONS UNDER SECTION 6229- The period prescribed by subsection (a)(1)
 for filing of a request for an administrative adjustment shall be extended--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) for the period within which an assessment may be made
 pursuant to an agreement (or any extension thereof) under section 6229(b),
 and [<-Struck out]

 shall take effect as if included in the amendments made by section 402 of
 the Tax Equity and Fiscal Responsibility Act of 1982. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4317. AVAILABILITY OF INNOCENT SPOUSE RELIEF IN CONTEXT
 OF PARTNERSHIP PROCEEDINGS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Subsection (a) of section 6230 is amended
 by adding at the end thereof the following new paragraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) SPECIAL RULE IN CASE OF ASSERTION BY PARTNER'S SPOUSE
 OF INNOCENT SPOUSE RELIEF-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) Notwithstanding section 6404(b), if the spouse of a
 partner asserts that section 6013(e) applies with respect to a liability that
 is attributable to any adjustment to a partnership item, then such spouse
 may file with the Secretary within 60 days after the notice and demand
 (or notice of computational adjustment) is mailed to the spouse a request
 for abatement of the assessment specified in such notice. Upon receipt of
 such request, the Secretary shall abate the assessment. Any reassessment of
 the tax with respect to which an abatement is made under this subparagraph
 shall be subject to the deficiency procedures prescribed by subchapter
 B. The period for making any such reassessment shall not expire before the
 expiration of 60 days after the date of such abatement. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) If the spouse files a petition with the Tax Court
 pursuant to section 6213 with respect to the request for abatement described
 in subparagraph (A), the Tax Court shall only have jurisdiction pursuant
 to this section to determine whether the requirements of section 6013(e)
 have been satisfied. For purposes of such determination, the treatment of
 partnership items under the settlement, the final partnership administrative
 adjustment, or the decision of the court (whichever is appropriate) that
 gave rise to the liability in question shall be conclusive. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) Rules similar to the rules contained in subparagraphs
 (B) and (C) of paragraph (2) shall apply for purposes of this
 paragraph.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CLAIMS FOR REFUND- Subsection (c) of section 6230
 is amended by adding at the end thereof the following new paragraph:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) RULES FOR SEEKING INNOCENT SPOUSE RELIEF-  [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The spouse of a partner may file a claim
 for refund on the ground that the Secretary failed to relieve the spouse
 under section 6013(e) from a liability that is attributable to an adjustment
 to a partnership item. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) TIME FOR FILING CLAIM- Any claim under subparagraph
 (A) shall be filed within 6 months after the day on which the Secretary mails
 to the spouse the notice and demand (or notice of computational adjustment)
 referred to in subsection (a)(3)(A). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SUIT IF CLAIM NOT ALLOWED- If the claim under
 subparagraph (B) is not allowed, the spouse may bring suit with respect to
 the claim within the period specified in paragraph (3). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) PRIOR DETERMINATIONS ARE BINDING- For purposes of
 any claim or suit under this paragraph, the treatment of partnership items
 under the settlement, the final partnership administrative adjustment,
 or the decision of the court (whichever is appropriate) that gave rise to
 the liability in question shall be conclusive.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) TECHNICAL AMENDMENTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) Paragraph (1) of section 6230(a) is amended by striking
 `paragraph (2)' and inserting `paragraph (2) or (3)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) Subsection (a) of section 6503 is amended by striking
 `section 6230(a)(2)(A)' and inserting `paragraph (2)(A) or (3) of section
 6230(a)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (d) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall take effect as if included in the amendments made by section 402 of
 the Tax Equity and Fiscal Responsibility Act of 1982. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4318. DETERMINATION OF PENALTIES AT PARTNERSHIP
 LEVEL. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Section 6221 (relating to tax treatment
 determined at partnership level) is amended by striking `item' and inserting
 `item (and the applicability of any penalty, addition to tax, or additional
 amount which relates to an adjustment to a partnership item)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CONFORMING AMENDMENTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) Subsection (f) of section 6226 is amended-- [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) by striking `relates and' and inserting `relates,',
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) by inserting before the period `, and the applicability
 of any penalty, addition to tax, or additional amount which relates to an
 adjustment to a partnership item'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) Clause (i) of section 6230(a)(2)(A) is amended to read
 as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) affected items which require partner level
 determinations (other than penalties, additions to tax, and additional
 amounts that relate to adjustments to partnership items), or'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (3)(A) Subparagraph (A) of section 6230(a)(3), as added
 by section 3317, is amended by inserting `(including any liability for any
 penalty, addition to tax, or additional amount relating to such adjustment)'
 after `partnership item'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) Subparagraph (B) of such section is amended by inserting
 `(and the applicability of any penalties, additions to tax, or additional
 amounts)' after `partnership items'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (C) Subparagraph (A) of section 6230(c)(5), as added
 by section 3317, is amended by inserting before the period  `(including
 any liability for any penalties, additions to tax, or additional amounts
 relating to such adjustment)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (D) Subparagraph (D) of section 6230(c)(5), as added
 by section 3317, is amended by inserting `(and the applicability of any
 penalties, additions to tax, or additional amounts)' after `partnership
 items'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (4) Paragraph (1) of section 6230(c) is amended by striking
 `or' at the end of subparagraph (A), by striking the period at the end of
 subparagraph (B) and inserting `, or', and by adding at the end thereof
 the following new subparagraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) the Secretary erroneously imposed any penalty,
 addition to tax, or additional amount which relates to an adjustment to a
 partnership item.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (5) So much of subparagraph (A) of section 6230(c)(2)
 as precedes `shall be filed' is amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) UNDER PARAGRAPH (1)(A) or (C)- Any claim under
 subparagraph (A) or (C) of paragraph (1)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (6) Paragraph (4) of section 6230(c) is amended by adding
 at the end thereof the following: `In addition, the determination under
 the final partnership administrative adjustment or under the decision
 of the court (whichever is appropriate) concerning the applicability of
 any penalty, addition to tax, or additional amount which relates to an
 adjustment to a partnership item shall also be conclusive. Notwithstanding
 the preceding sentence, the partner shall be allowed to assert any partner
 level defenses that may apply or to challenge the amount of the computational
 adjustment.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to partnership taxable years ending after the date of the
 enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4319. PROVISIONS RELATING TO COURT JURISDICTION,
 ETC. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) TAX COURT JURISDICTION TO ENJOIN PREMATURE ASSESSMENTS
 OF DEFICIENCIES ATTRIBUTABLE TO PARTNERSHIP ITEMS- Subsection (b) of section
 6225 is amended by striking `the proper court.' and inserting `the proper
 court, including the Tax Court. The Tax Court shall have no jurisdiction
 to enjoin any action or proceeding under this subsection unless a timely
 petition for a readjustment of the partnership items for the taxable year
 has been filed and then only in respect of the adjustments that are the
 subject of such petition.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) JURISDICTION TO CONSIDER STATUTE OF LIMITATIONS WITH
 RESPECT TO PARTNERS- Paragraph (1) of section 6226(d) is amended by adding
 at the end thereof the following new sentence: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Notwithstanding subparagraph (B), any person treated under
 subsection (c) as a party to an action shall be permitted to participate in
 such action (or file a readjustment petition under subsection (b) or paragraph
 (2) of this subsection) solely for the purpose of asserting that the period
 of limitations for assessing any tax attributable to partnership items has
 expired with respect to such person, and the court having jurisdiction of such
 action shall have jurisdiction to consider such assertion.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) TAX COURT JURISDICTION TO DETERMINE OVERPAYMENTS
 ATTRIBUTABLE TO AFFECTED ITEMS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) Paragraph (6) of section 6230(d) is amended by striking
 `(or an affected item)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) Paragraph (3) of section 6512(b) is amended by adding
 at the end thereof the following new sentence: [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] SEC. 4402. REPLACEMENT FOR PASSIVE FOREIGN INVESTMENT COMPANY
 RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Part VI of subchapter P of chapter 1
 (relating to treatment of certain passive foreign investment companies)
 is amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `PART VI--TREATMENT OF PASSIVE FOREIGN CORPORATIONS
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart A. Current taxation rules. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart B. Interest on holdings to which subpart A does
 not apply. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart C. General provisions. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart A--Current Taxation Rules [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1291. Stock in certain passive foreign corporations
 marked to market. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1292. Inclusion of income of certain passive foreign
 corporations. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1291. STOCK IN CERTAIN PASSIVE FOREIGN CORPORATIONS
 MARKED TO MARKET. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) GENERAL RULE- In the case of marketable stock in a
 passive foreign corporation which is owned (or treated under subsection
 (g) as owned) by a United States person at the close of any taxable year
 of such person-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) If the fair market value of such stock as of the close
 of such taxable year exceeds its adjusted basis, such United States person
 shall include in gross income for such taxable year an amount equal to the
 amount of such excess. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) If the adjusted basis of such stock exceeds the fair
 market value of such stock as of the close of such taxable year, such United
 States person shall be allowed a deduction for such taxable year equal to
 the lesser of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the amount of such excess, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the unreversed inclusions with respect to such
 stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) BASIS ADJUSTMENTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The adjusted basis of stock in a passive
 foreign corporation-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) shall be increased by the amount included in the gross
 income of the United States person under subsection (a)(1) with respect to
 such stock, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) shall be decreased by the amount allowed as a deduction
 to the United States person under subsection (a)(2) with respect to such
 stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULE FOR STOCK CONSTRUCTIVELY OWNED- In the
 case of stock in a passive foreign corporation which the United States
 person is treated as owning under subsection (g)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the adjustments under paragraph (1) shall apply to
 such stock in the hands of the person actually holding such stock but only
 for purposes of determining the subsequent treatment under this chapter of
 the United States person with respect to such stock, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) similar adjustments shall be made to the adjusted basis
 of the property by reason of which the United States person is treated as
 owning such stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) CHARACTER AND SOURCE RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) ORDINARY TREATMENT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) GAIN- Any amount included in gross income under
 subsection (a)(1), and any gain on the sale or other disposition of
 marketable stock in a passive foreign corporation, shall be treated as
 ordinary income. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) LOSS- Any-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) amount allowed as a deduction under subsection (a)(2),
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) loss on the sale or other disposition of marketable
 stock in a passive foreign corporation to the extent that the amount of such
 loss does not exceed the unreversed inclusions with respect to such stock,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] shall be treated as an ordinary loss. The amount so treated
 shall be treated as a deduction allowable in computing adjusted gross
 income. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SOURCE- The source of any amount included in gross
 income under subsection (a)(1) (or allowed as a deduction under subsection
 (a)(2)) shall be determined in the same manner as if such amount were gain
 or loss (as the case may be) from the sale of stock in the passive foreign
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) UNREVERSED INCLUSIONS- For purposes of this section,
 the term `unreversed inclusions' means, with respect to any stock in a
 passive foreign corporation, the excess (if any) of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) the amount included in gross income of the taxpayer
 under subsection (a)(1) with respect to such stock for prior taxable years,
 over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the amount allowed as a deduction under subsection
 (a)(2) with respect to such stock for prior taxable years. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] The amount referred to in paragraph (1) shall include any
 amount which would have been included in gross income under subsection
 (a)(1) with respect to such stock for any prior taxable year but for section
 1293. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 1292- This section shall
 not apply with respect to any stock in a passive foreign corporation--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) which is U.S. controlled, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) which is a qualified electing fund with respect to
 the United States person for the taxable year, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) in which the United States person is a 25-percent
 shareholder. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) TREATMENT OF CONTROLLED FOREIGN CORPORATIONS WHICH
 ARE SHAREHOLDERS IN PASSIVE FOREIGN CORPORATIONS- In the case of a foreign
 corporation which is a controlled foreign corporation (or is treated
 as a controlled foreign corporation under section 1292) and which owns
 (or is treated under subsection (g) as owning) stock in a passive foreign
 corporation-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) this section (other than subsection (c)(2) thereof)
 shall apply to such foreign corporation in the same manner as if such
 corporation were a United States person, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) for purposes of subpart F of part III of subchapter N--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any amount included in gross income under subsection
 (a)(1) shall be treated as foreign personal holding company income described
 in section 954(c)(1)(A), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any amount allowed as a deduction under subsection
 (a)(2) shall be treated as a deduction allocable to foreign personal holding
 company income so described. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(g) STOCK OWNED THROUGH CERTAIN FOREIGN ENTITIES- Except
 as provided in regulations-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this section, stock owned,
 directly or indirectly, by or for a foreign partnership or foreign trust
 or foreign estate shall be considered as being owned proportionately by its
 partners or beneficiaries. Stock considered to be owned by a person by reason
 of the application of the preceding sentence shall, for purposes of applying
 such sentence, be treated as actually owned by such person. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN DISPOSITIONS- In any case in
 which a United States person is treated as owning stock in a passive foreign
 corporation by reason of paragraph (1)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any disposition by the United States person or by
 any other person which results in the United States person being treated
 as no longer owning such stock, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any disposition by the person owning such stock,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] shall be treated as a disposition by the United States person
 of the stock in the passive foreign corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(h) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 851(b)- For purposes of
 paragraphs (2) and (3) of section 851(b), any amount included in gross
 income under subsection (a) shall be treated as a dividend. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) TRANSITION RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) INDIVIDUALS BECOMING SUBJECT TO U.S. TAX- If any
 individual becomes a United States person in a taxable year beginning after
 December 31, 1992, solely for purposes of this section, the adjusted basis
 (before adjustments under subsection (b)) of any marketable stock in a
 passive foreign corporation owned (or treated as owned under subsection
 (g)) by such individual on the first day of such taxable year shall be
 treated as being the greater of its fair market value on such first day or
 its adjusted basis on such first day. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) MARKETABLE STOCK HELD BEFORE EFFECTIVE DATE-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If any marketable stock in a passive
 foreign corporation is owned (or treated under subsection (g) as owned)
 by a United States person on the first day of such person's first taxable
 year, beginning after December 31, 1992-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) paragraph (2) of section 1294(a) shall apply to such
 stock as if it became marketable during such first taxable year; except that--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) section 1293 shall not apply to the amount included in
 gross income under subsection (a) to the extent such amount is attributable
 to increases in fair market value during such first taxable year, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the taxpayer's holding period shall be treated as
 having ended on the last day of the preceding taxable year for purposes of
 allocating amounts under section 1293(a)(1)(A), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) such person may elect to extend the time for
 the payment of the applicable section 1293 deferred tax as provided in
 subparagraph (B). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) ELECTION TO EXTEND TIME FOR PAYMENT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- At the election of the taxpayer, the
 time for the payment of the applicable section 1293 deferred tax shall
 be extended to the extent and subject to the limitations provided in this
 subparagraph. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) TERMINATION OF EXTENSION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) DISTRIBUTIONS- If any distribution is received with
 respect to any stock to which an extension under clause (i) relates and such
 distribution would be an excess distribution within the meaning of section
 1293 if such section applied to such stock, then the extension under clause
 (i) for the appropriate portion (as determined under regulations) of the
 applicable section 1293 deferred tax shall expire on the last day prescribed
 by law (determined without regard to extensions) for filing the return of
 tax for the taxable year in which the distribution is received. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) REVERSAL OF INCLUSION- If an amount is allowable as
 a deduction under subsection (a)(2) with respect to any stock to which an
 extension under clause (i) relates and the amount so allowable is allocable
 to the amount which gave rise to the applicable section 1293 deferred
 tax, then the extension under clause (i) for the appropriate portion (as
 determined under regulations) of the applicable section 1293 deferred tax
 shall expire on the last day prescribed by law (determined without regard
 to extensions) for filing the return of the tax for the taxable year for
 which such deduction is allowed. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(III) DISPOSITIONS, ETC- If stock in a passive foreign
 corporation is disposed of during the taxable year, all extensions
 under clause (i) for payment of the applicable section 1293 deferred tax
 attributable to such stock which have not expired before the date of such
 disposition shall expire on the last date prescribed by law (determined
 without regard to extensions) for filing the return of tax for the taxable
 year in which such disposition occurs. To the extent provided in regulations,
 the preceding sentence shall not apply in the case of a disposition in
 a transaction with respect to which gain or loss is not recognized (in
 whole or in part), and the person acquiring such stock in such transaction
 shall succeed to the treatment under this section of the person making such
 disposition. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) OTHER RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) ELECTION- The election under clause (i) shall be
 made not later than the time prescribed by law (including extensions) for
 filing the return of tax imposed by this chapter for the first taxable year
 referred to in subparagraph (A). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) TREATMENT OF LOANS TO SHAREHOLDER- For purposes
 of this subparagraph, any loan by a passive foreign corporation (directly
 or indirectly) to a shareholder of such corporation shall be treated as a
 distribution to such shareholder. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) CROSS REFERENCE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]  `For provisions providing for interest for the period of
 the extension under this paragraph, see section 6601. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) APPLICABLE SECTION 1293 DEFERRED TAX- For purposes
 of this paragraph, the term `applicable section 1293 deferred tax' means
 the deferred tax amount determined under section 1293 with respect to the
 amount which, but for section 1293, would have been included in gross income
 for the first taxable year referred to in subparagraph (A). Such term also
 includes the tax imposed by this chapter for such first taxable year to the
 extent attributable to the amounts allocated under section 1293(a)(1)(A)
 to a period described in section 1293(a)(1)(B)(ii). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) SPECIAL RULES FOR REGULATED INVESTMENT COMPANIES-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If any marketable stock in a passive
 foreign corporation is owned (or treated under subsection (g) as owned)
 by a regulated investment company on the first day of such company's first
 taxable year beginning after December 31, 1992-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) section 1293 shall not apply to such stock with respect
 to any distribution or disposition during, or amount included in gross
 income under this section for, such first taxable year, but [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) such company's tax under this chapter for such first
 taxable year shall be increased by the aggregate amount of interest which
 would have been determined under section 1293(c)(3) if section 1293 were
 applied without regard to this subparagraph. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) DISALLOWANCE OF DEDUCTION- No deduction shall be
 allowed to any regulated investment company for the increase in tax under
 subparagraph (A)(ii). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1292. CURRENT INCLUSION OF INCOME OF CERTAIN PASSIVE
 FOREIGN CORPORATIONS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) PASSIVE FOREIGN CORPORATIONS WHICH ARE U.S. CONTROLLED-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) TREATMENT UNDER SUBPART F-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If a passive foreign corporation is United
 States controlled, then for purposes of subpart F of part III of subchapter
 N-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) such corporation, if not otherwise a controlled
 foreign corporation, shall be treated as a controlled foreign corporation,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the term `United States shareholder' means, with
 respect to such corporation, any United States person who owns (within the
 meaning of section 958(a)) any stock in such corporation, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) the entire gross income of such corporation shall,
 after being reduced under the principles of paragraph (5) of section 954(b),
 be treated as foreign base company income, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) sections 970 and 971 shall not apply. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] Except as provided in regulations, the preceding sentence
 shall also apply for purposes of section 904(d). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) SPECIAL RULES- If any taxpayer is treated as being
 a United States shareholder in a controlled foreign corporation solely by
 reason of this section-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) section 954(b)(4) (relating to exception for certain
 income subject to high foreign taxes) shall not apply for purposes of
 determining the amount included in the gross income of such taxpayer under
 section 951 by reason of being so treated with respect to such corporation,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the amount so included in the gross income of such
 taxpayer under section 951 with respect to such corporation shall be treated
 as long-term capital gain to the extent attributable to the net capital
 gain of such corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) U.S. CONTROLLED- For purposes of this subpart,
 a passive foreign corporation is United States controlled if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such corporation is a controlled foreign corporation
 determined without regard to this subsection, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) at any time during the taxable year more than 50
 percent of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the total combined voting power of all classes of
 stock of such corporation entitled to vote, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the total value of the stock of such corporation,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] is owned directly or indirectly by 5 or fewer United States
 persons. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) CONSTRUCTIVE OWNERSHIP RULES FOR PURPOSES OF PARAGRAPH
 (2)(B)- For purposes of paragraph (2)(B), the attribution rules provided
 in section 544 shall apply, determined as if any reference to a personal
 holding company were a reference to a corporation described in paragraph
 (2)(B) (and any reference to the stock ownership requirement provided in
 section 542(a)(2) were a reference to the requirement of paragraph (2)(B));
 except that-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) subsection (a)(4) of such section shall be applied by
 substituting `Paragraphs (1), (2), and (3)' for `Paragraphs (2) and (3)',
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) stock owned by a nonresident alien individual shall
 not be considered by reason of attribution through family membership as
 owned by a citizen or resident alien individual who is not the spouse of the
 nonresident alien individual and who does not otherwise own stock in the
 foreign corporation (determined after the application of such attribution
 rules other than attribution through family membership), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) stock of a corporation owned by any foreign person
 shall not be considered by reason of attribution through partners as owned
 by a citizen or resident of the United States who does not otherwise own
 stock in the foreign corporation (determined after the application of such
 attribution rules and subparagraph (A), other than attribution through
 partners). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) TAXPAYERS ELECTING CURRENT INCLUSION AND 25-PERCENT
 SHAREHOLDERS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If a passive foreign corporation which is
 not United States controlled is a qualified electing fund with respect to
 any taxpayer or the taxpayer is a 25-percent shareholder in such corporation,
 then for purposes of subpart F of part III of subchapter N-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such passive foreign corporation shall be treated as
 a controlled foreign corporation with respect to such taxpayer, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such taxpayer shall be treated as a United States
 shareholder in such corporation, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) the modifications of clauses (iii) and (iv) of
 subsection (a)(1)(A) and of subparagraph (B) of subsection (a)(1) shall apply
 in determining the amount included under such subpart F in the gross income
 of such taxpayer (and the character of the amount so included). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of section 904(d), any amount included in the
 gross income of the taxpayer under the preceding sentence shall be treated
 as a dividend from a foreign corporation which is not a controlled foreign
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) QUALIFIED ELECTING FUND- For purposes of this subpart,
 the term `qualified electing fund' means any passive foreign corporation if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) an election by the taxpayer under paragraph (3) applies
 to such corporation for the taxable year of the taxpayer, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such corporation complies with such requirements as
 the Secretary may prescribe for purposes of carrying out the purposes of
 this subpart. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) ELECTION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- A taxpayer may make an election under
 this paragraph with respect to any passive foreign corporation for any
 taxable year of the taxpayer. Such an election, once made with respect
 to any corporation, shall apply to all subsequent taxable years of the
 taxpayer with respect to such corporation unless revoked by the taxpayer
 with the consent of the Secretary. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) WHEN MADE- An election under this subsection may be
 made for any taxable year of the taxpayer at any time on or before the due
 date (determined with regard to extensions) for filing the return of the
 tax imposed by this chapter for such taxable year. To the extent provided
 in regulations, such an election may be made later than as required in
 the preceding sentence where the taxpayer fails to make a timely election
 because the taxpayer reasonably believes that the corporation was not a
 passive foreign corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) 25-PERCENT SHAREHOLDER- For purposes of this subpart,
 the term `25-percent shareholder' means, with respect to any passive
 foreign corporation, any United States person who owns (within the meaning
 of section 958(a)), or is considered as owning by applying the rules of
 section 958(b), 25 percent or more (by vote or value) of the stock of such
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart B--Interest on Holdings To Which Subpart A Does
 Not Apply [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1293. Interest on tax deferral. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1294. Definitions and special rules. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1293. INTEREST ON TAX DEFERRAL. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) TREATMENT OF DISTRIBUTIONS AND STOCK DISPOSITIONS-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) DISTRIBUTIONS- If a United States person receives an
 excess distribution in respect of stock to which this section applies, then--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the amount of the excess distribution shall be
 allocated ratably to each day in the taxpayer's holding period for the stock,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) with respect to such excess distribution, the taxpayer's
 gross income for the current year shall include (as ordinary income) only
 the amounts allocated under subparagraph (A) to-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the current year, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) any period in the taxpayer's holding period before the
 first day of the first taxable year of the corporation which begins after
 December 31, 1986, and for which it was a passive foreign corporation, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) the tax imposed by this chapter for the current year
 shall be increased by the deferred tax amount (determined under subsection
 (c)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) DISPOSITIONS- If the taxpayer disposes of stock to
 which this section applies, then the rules of paragraph (1) shall apply to
 any gain recognized on such disposition in the same manner as if such gain
 were an excess distribution. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) DEFINITIONS- For purposes of this subpart--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) HOLDING PERIOD- The taxpayer's holding period shall
 be determined under section 1223; except that-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) for purposes of applying this section to an excess
 distribution, such holding period shall be treated as ending on the date
 of such distribution, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) if section 1291 applied to such stock with respect
 to the taxpayer for any prior taxable year, such holding period shall be
 treated as beginning on the first day of the first taxable year beginning
 after the last taxable year for which section 1291 so applied. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) CURRENT YEAR- The term `current year' means the taxable
 year in which the excess distribution or disposition occurs. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) EXCESS DISTRIBUTION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this section, the term
 `excess distribution' means any distribution in respect of stock received
 during any taxable year to the extent such distribution does not exceed its
 ratable portion of the total excess distribution (if any) for such taxable
 year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TOTAL EXCESS DISTRIBUTION- For purposes of this
 subsection-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The term `total excess distribution'
 means the excess (if any) of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the amount of the distributions in respect of the
 stock received by the taxpayer during the taxable year, over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) 125 percent of the average amount received in respect
 of such stock by the taxpayer during the 3 preceding taxable years (or,
 if shorter, the portion of the taxpayer's holding period before the taxable
 year). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of clause (ii), any excess distribution received
 during such 3-year period shall be taken into account only to the extent
 it was included in gross income under subsection (a)(1)(B). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) NO EXCESS FOR FIRST YEAR- The total excess distributions
 with respect to any stock shall be zero for the taxable year in which the
 taxpayer's holding period in such stock begins. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) ADJUSTMENTS- Under regulations prescribed by the
 Secretary-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) determinations under this subsection shall be made
 on a share-by-share basis, except that shares with the same holding period
 may be aggregated, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) proper adjustments shall be made for stock splits
 and stock dividends, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) if the taxpayer does not hold the stock during the
 entire taxable year, distributions received during such year shall be
 annualized, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) if the taxpayer's holding period includes periods during
 which the stock was held by another person, distributions received by such
 other person shall be taken into account as if received by the taxpayer,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) if the distributions are received in a foreign currency,
 determinations under this subsection shall be made in such currency and
 the amount of any excess distribution determined in such currency shall be
 translated into dollars, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(F) proper adjustment shall be made for amounts not
 includible in gross income by reason of section 959(a) or for which a
 deduction is allowable under section 245(c), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(G) if a charitable deduction was allowable under
 section 642(c) to a trust for any distribution of its income, proper
 adjustments shall be made for the deduction so allowable to the extent
 allocable to distributions or gain in respect of stock in a passive foreign
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of subparagraph (F), any amount not includible in
 gross income by reason of section 551(d) (as in effect on January 1, 1992)
 or 1293(c) (as so in effect) shall be treated as an amount not includible
 in gross income by reason of section 959(a). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) DEFERRED TAX AMOUNT- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The term `deferred tax amount' means,
 with respect to any distribution or disposition to which subsection (a)
 applies, an amount equal to the sum of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the aggregate increases in taxes described in paragraph
 (2), plus [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the aggregate amount of interest (determined in the
 manner provided under paragraph (3)) on such increases in tax. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] Any increase in the tax imposed by this chapter for the
 current year under subsection (a) to the extent attributable to the amount
 referred to in subparagraph (B) shall be treated as interest paid under
 section 6601 on the due date for the current year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) AGGREGATE INCREASES IN TAXES- For purposes of paragraph
 (1)(A), the aggregate increases in taxes shall be determined by multiplying
 each amount allocated under subsection (a)(1)(A) to any taxable year (other
 than the current year) by the highest rate of tax in effect for such taxable
 year under section 1 or 11, whichever applies. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) COMPUTATION OF INTEREST-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The amount of interest referred to in
 paragraph (1)(B) on any increase determined under paragraph (2) for any
 taxable year shall be determined for the period-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) beginning on the due date for such taxable year, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) ending on the due date for the taxable year with or
 within which the distribution or disposition occurs, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] by using the rates and method applicable under section 6621
 for underpayments of tax for such period. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) DUE DATE- For purposes of this subsection, the term
 `due date' means the date prescribed by law (determined without regard to
 extensions) for filing the return of the tax imposed by this chapter for
 the taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SPECIAL RULE- For purposes of determining the amount
 of interest referred to in paragraph (1)(B), the amount of any increase
 in tax determined under paragraph (2) shall be determined without regard
 to any reduction under section 1294(d) for a tax described in paragraph
 (2)(A)(ii) thereof. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1294. DEFINITIONS AND SPECIAL RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) STOCK TO WHICH SECTION 1293 APPLIES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 paragraph, section 1293 shall apply to any stock in a passive foreign
 corporation unless-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such stock is marketable stock as of the time of the
 distribution or disposition involved, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B)(i) with respect to each of such corporation's taxable
 years which begin after December 31, 1992, and include any portion of the
 taxpayer's holding period in such stock-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) such corporation was U.S. controlled (within the
 meaning of section 1292(a)(2)), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) such corporation was treated as a controlled
 foreign corporation under section 1292(b) with respect to the taxpayer,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) with respect to each of such corporation's taxable
 years which begin after December 31, 1986, and before January 1, 1993,
 and include any portion of the taxpayer's holding period in such stock,
 such corporation was treated as a qualified electing fund under this part
 (as in effect on January 1, 1992) with respect to the taxpayer. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TREATMENT WHERE STOCK BECOMES MARKETABLE- If any stock
 in a passive foreign corporation becomes marketable stock after the beginning
 of the taxpayer's holding period in such stock, section 1293 shall apply to--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any distributions with respect to, or disposition
 of, such stock in the taxable year of the taxpayer in which it becomes so
 marketable, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any amount which, but for section 1293, would have
 been included in gross income under section 1291(a) with respect to such
 stock for such taxable year in the same manner as if such amount were gain
 on the disposition of such stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) ELECTION TO RECOGNIZE GAIN WHERE COMPANY BECOMES
 SUBJECT TO CURRENT INCLUSIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) a passive foreign corporation first meets the
 requirements of clause (i) of paragraph (1)(B) with respect to the taxpayer
 for a taxable year of such taxpayer which begins after December 31, 1992,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the taxpayer holds stock in such company on the
 first day of such taxable year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) the taxpayer establishes to the satisfaction
 of the Secretary the fair market value of such stock on such first day,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] the taxpayer may elect to recognize gain as if he sold such
 stock on such first day for such fair market value. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) ADDITIONAL ELECTION FOR SHAREHOLDER OF CONTROLLED
 FOREIGN CORPORATIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- If-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) a passive foreign corporation first meets the
 requirements of subclause (I) of paragraph (1)(B)(i) with respect to the
 taxpayer for a taxable year of such taxpayer which begins after December 31,
 1992, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the taxpayer holds stock in such corporation on the
 first day of such taxable year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(III) such corporation is a controlled foreign corporation
 without regard to this part, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] the taxpayer may elect to be treated as receiving a dividend
 on such first day in an amount equal to the portion of the post-1986 earnings
 and profits of such corporation attributable (under regulations prescribed by
 the Secretary) to the stock in such corporation held by the taxpayer on such
 first day. The amount treated as a dividend under the preceding sentence
 shall be treated as an excess distribution and shall be allocated under
 section 1293(a)(1)(A) only two days during periods taken into account in
 determining the post-1986 earnings and profits so attributable. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) POST-1986 EARNINGS AND PROFITS- For purposes of
 clause (i), the term `post-1986 earnings and profits' means earnings
 and profits which were accumulated in taxable years of the corporation
 beginning after December 31, 1986, and during the period or periods the
 stock was held by the taxpayer while the corporation was a passive foreign
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 959(e)- For purposes of
 section 959(e), any amount treated as a dividend under this subparagraph shall
 be treated as included in gross income under section 1248(a). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) ADJUSTMENTS- In the case of any stock to which
 subparagraph (A) or (B) applies-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the adjusted basis of such stock shall be increased
 by the gain recognized under subparagraph (A) or the amount treated as a
 dividend under subparagraph (B), as the case may be, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the taxpayer's holding period in such stock
 shall be treated as beginning on the first day referred to in such
 subparagraph. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) RULES RELATING TO STOCK ACQUIRED FROM A DECEDENT-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) BASIS- In the case of stock of a passive foreign
 corporation acquired by bequest, devise, or inheritance (or by the decedent's
 estate), notwithstanding section 1014, the basis of such stock in the hands
 of the person so acquiring it shall be the adjusted basis of such stock
 in the hands of the decedent immediately before his death (or, if lesser,
 the basis which would have been determined under section 1014 without regard
 to this paragraph). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) DEDUCTION FOR ESTATE TAX- If stock in a passive
 foreign corporation is acquired from a decedent, the taxpayer shall,
 under regulations prescribed by the Secretary, be allowed (for the taxable
 year of the sale or exchange) a deduction from gross income equal to that
 portion of the decedent's estate tax deemed paid which is attributable to
 the excess of (A) the value at which such stock was taken into account for
 purposes of determining the value of the decedent's gross estate, over (B)
 the basis determined under paragraph (1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) EXCEPTIONS- This subsection shall not apply to any
 stock in a passive foreign corporation if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) section 1293 would not have applied to a disposition
 of such stock by the decedent immediately before his death, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the decedent was a nonresident alien at all times
 during his holding period in such stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) RECOGNITION OF GAIN- Except as otherwise provided
 in regulations, in the case of any transfer of stock in a passive foreign
 company to which section 1293 applies, where (but for this subsection)
 there is not full recognition of gain, the excess (if any) of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) the fair market value of such stock, over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) its adjusted basis, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] shall be treated as gain from the sale or exchange of such
 stock and shall be recognized notwithstanding any provision of law. Proper
 adjustment shall be made to the basis of property for gain recognized under
 the preceding sentence. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) COORDINATION WITH FOREIGN TAX CREDIT RULES-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If there are creditable foreign taxes
 with respect to any distribution in respect of stock in a passive foreign
 corporation-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the amount of such distribution shall be determined
 for purposes of section 1293 with regard to section 78, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the excess distribution taxes shall be allocated ratably
 to each day in the taxpayer's holding period for the stock, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) to the extent-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) that such excess distribution taxes are allocated to
 a taxable year referred to in section 1293(a)(1)(B), such taxes shall be
 taken into account under section 901 for the current year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) that such excess distribution taxes are allocated to
 any other taxable year, such taxes shall reduce (subject to the principles of
 section 904 and not below zero) the increase in tax determined under section
 1293(c)(2) for such taxable year by reason of such distribution (but such
 taxes shall not be taken into account under section 901). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) DEFINITIONS- For purposes of this subsection--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) CREDITABLE FOREIGN TAXES- The term `creditable foreign
 taxes' means, with respect to any distribution-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) any foreign taxes deemed paid under section 902 with
 respect to such distribution, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) any withholding tax imposed with respect to such
 distribution, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] but only if the taxpayer chooses the benefits of section 901
 and such taxes are creditable under section 901 (determined without regard
 to paragraph (1)(C)(ii)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) EXCESS DISTRIBUTION TAXES- The term `excess distribution
 taxes' means, with respect to any distribution, the portion of the creditable
 foreign taxes with respect to such distribution which is attributable (on
 a pro rata basis) to the portion of such distribution which is an excess
 distribution. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) SECTION 1248 GAIN- The rules of this subsection also
 shall apply in the case of any gain which but for this section would be
 includible in gross income as a dividend under section 1248. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) ATTRIBUTION OF OWNERSHIP- For purposes of this subpart--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) ATTRIBUTION TO UNITED STATES PERSONS- This subsection--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) shall apply to the extent that the effect is to treat
 stock of a passive foreign corporation as owned by a United States person,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) except as provided in paragraph (3) or in
 regulations, shall not apply to treat stock owned (or treated as owned
 under this subsection) by a United States person as owned by any other
 person. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CORPORATIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If 50 percent or more in value of the
 stock of a corporation (other than an S corporation) is owned, directly or
 indirectly, by or for any person, such person shall be considered as owning
 the stock owned directly or indirectly by or for such corporation in that
 proportion which the value of the stock which such person so owns bears to
 the value of all stock in the corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) 50-PERCENT LIMITATION NOT TO APPLY IN CERTAIN CASES-
 For purposes of determining whether a shareholder of a passive foreign
 corporation (or whether a United States shareholder of a controlled foreign
 corporation which is not a passive foreign corporation) is treated as owning
 stock owned directly or indirectly by or for such corporation, subparagraph
 (A) shall be applied without regard to the 50-percent limitation contained
 therein. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) FAMILY AND PARTNER ATTRIBUTION FOR 50-PERCENT
 LIMITATION- For purposes of determining whether the 50-percent limitation of
 subparagraph (A) is met, the constructive ownership rules of section 544(a)(2)
 shall apply in addition to the other rules of this subsection. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) PARTNERSHIPS, ETC- Except as provided in regulations,
 stock owned, directly or indirectly, by or for a partnership, S corporation,
 estate, or trust shall be considered as being owned proportionately by its
 partners, shareholders, or beneficiaries (as the case may be). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) OPTIONS- To the extent provided in regulations, if
 any person has an option to acquire stock, such stock shall be considered as
 owned by such person. For purposes of this paragraph, an option to acquire
 such an option, and each one of a series of such options, shall be considered
 as an option to acquire such stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) SUCCESSIVE APPLICATION- Stock considered to be owned by
 a person by reason of the application of paragraph (2), (3), or (4) shall,
 for purposes of applying such paragraphs, be considered as actually owned
 by such person. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) OTHER SPECIAL RULES- For purposes of this subpart--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) TIME FOR DETERMINATION- Stock held by a taxpayer
 shall be treated as stock in a passive foreign corporation if, at any time
 during the holding period of the taxpayer with respect to such stock, such
 corporation (or any predecessor) was a passive foreign corporation. The
 preceding sentence shall not apply if the taxpayer elects to recognize gain
 (as of the last day of the last taxable year for which the company was a
 passive foreign corporation) under rules similar to the rules of subsection
 (a)(3)(A). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) APPLICATION OF SUBPART WHERE STOCK HELD BY OTHER
 ENTITY- Under regulations-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- In any case in which a United States person
 is treated as owning stock in a passive foreign corporation by reason of
 subsection (e)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) any transaction which results in the United States
 person being treated as no longer owning such stock, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) any disposition of such stock by the person owning
 such stock, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) any distribution of property in respect of such
 stock to the person holding such stock, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] shall be treated as a disposition by, or distribution to,
 the United States person with respect to the stock in the passive foreign
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) AMOUNT TREATED IN SAME MANNER AS PREVIOUSLY TAXED
 INCOME- Rules similar to the rules of section 959(b) shall apply to any
 amount described in subparagraph (A) in respect of stock which the taxpayer
 is treated as owning under subsection (e). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 951- If, but for this
 subparagraph, an amount would be taken into account under section 1293 by
 reason of subparagraph (A) and such amount would also be included in the
 gross income of the taxpayer under section 951, such amount shall only be
 taken into account under section 1293. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) DISPOSITIONS- Except as provided in regulations,
 if a taxpayer uses any stock in a passive foreign corporation as security
 for a loan, the taxpayer shall be treated as having disposed of such
 stock. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Subpart C--General Provisions [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1296. Passive foreign corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1297. Special rules. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1296. PASSIVE FOREIGN CORPORATION. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this part, except as
 otherwise provided in this subpart, the term `passive foreign corporation'
 means any foreign corporation if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) 60 percent or more of the gross income of such
 corporation for the taxable year is passive income, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the average percentage of assets (by value) held by
 such corporation during the taxable year which produce passive income or
 which are held for the production of passive income is at least 50 percent,
 or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) such corporation is registered under the Investment
 Company Act of 1940, as amended (15 U.S.C. 80a-1 to 80b-2), either as a
 management company or as a unit investment trust. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] A foreign corporation may elect to have the determination
 under paragraph (2) based on the adjusted bases of its assets in lieu of
 their value. Such an election, once made, may be revoked only with the
 consent of the Secretary. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) PASSIVE INCOME- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 subsection, the term `passive income' means any income which is of a kind
 which would be foreign personal holding company income as defined in section
 954(c) without regard to paragraph (3) thereof. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) EXCEPTIONS- Except as provided in regulations, the term
 `passive income' does not include any income-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) derived in the active conduct of a banking business
 by an institution licensed to do business as a bank in the United States
 (or, to the extent provided in regulations, by any other corporation),
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) derived in the active conduct of an insurance business
 by a corporation which is predominantly engaged in an insurance business
 and which would be subject to tax under subchapter L if it were a domestic
 corporation, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) which is interest, a dividend, or a rent or royalty,
 which is received or accrued from a related person (within the meaning of
 section 954(d)(3)) to the extent such amount is properly allocable (under
 regulations prescribed by the Secretary) to income of such related person
 which is not passive income, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) any foreign trade income of a FSC. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of subparagraph (C), the term `related person' has
 the meaning given such term by section 954(d)(3) determined by substituting
 `foreign corporation' for `controlled foreign corporation' each place it
 appears in section 954(d)(3). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) TREATMENT OF INCOME FROM CERTAIN ASSETS- To the extent
 that any asset is properly treated as not held for the production of passive
 income for purposes of subsection (a)(2), all income from such asset shall
 be treated as income which is not passive income. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) LOOK-THROUGH IN CASE OF 25-PERCENT OWNED CORPORATION-
 If a foreign corporation owns (directly or indirectly) at least 25 percent
 (by value) of the stock of another corporation, for purposes of determining
 whether such foreign corporation is a passive foreign corporation, such
 foreign corporation shall be treated as if it-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) held its proportionate share of the assets of such
 other corporation, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) received directly its proportionate share of the
 income of such other corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1297. SPECIAL RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) UNITED STATES PERSON- For purposes of this part, the
 term `United States person' has the meaning given to such term by section
 7701(a)(30). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) CONTROLLED FOREIGN CORPORATION- For purposes of this
 part, the term `controlled foreign corporation' has the meaning given such
 term by section 957(a). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) MARKETABLE STOCK- For purposes of this part--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The term `marketable stock' means--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any stock which is regularly traded on-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) a national securities exchange which is registered
 with the Securities and Exchange Commission or the national market system
 established pursuant to section 11A of the Securities and Exchange Act of
 1934, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) any exchange or other market which the Secretary
 determines has rules adequate to carry out the purposes of this part, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) to the extent provided in regulations, stock in any
 foreign corporation which is comparable to a regulated investment company
 and which offers for sale or has outstanding any stock of which it is the
 issuer and which is redeemable at its net asset value. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULE FOR REGULATED INVESTMENT COMPANIES- In
 the case of any regulated investment company which is offering for sale or
 has outstanding any stock of which it is the issuer and which is redeemable
 at its net asset value, all stock in a passive foreign corporation which
 it owns (or is treated under section 1291(g) as owning) shall be treated as
 marketable stock for purposes of this part. Except as provided in regulations,
 a similar rule shall apply in the case of any other regulated investment
 company. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) OTHER SPECIAL RULES- For purposes of this part--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) CERTAIN CORPORATIONS NOT TREATED AS PASSIVE- A
 corporation shall not be treated as a passive foreign corporation for the
 1st taxable year such corporation has gross income (hereinafter in this
 paragraph referred to as the `start-up year') if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) no predecessor of such corporation was a passive
 foreign corporation, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) it is established to the satisfaction of the Secretary
 that such corporation will not be a passive foreign corporation for either
 of the 1st 2 taxable years following the start-up year, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) such corporation is not a passive foreign corporation
 for either of the 1st 2 taxable years following the start-up year. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CERTAIN CORPORATIONS CHANGING BUSINESSES- A corporation
 shall not be treated as a passive foreign corporation for any taxable year
 if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) neither such corporation (nor any predecessor) was
 a passive foreign corporation for any prior taxable year, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) it is established to the satisfaction of the Secretary
 that-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) substantially all of the passive income of the
 corporation for the taxable year is attributable to proceeds from the
 disposition of 1 or more active trades or businesses, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) such corporation will not be a passive foreign
 corporation for either of the 1st 2 taxable years following the taxable year,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) such corporation is not a passive foreign corporation
 for either of such 2 taxable years. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of section 1296(c), any passive income referred
 to in subparagraph (B)(i) shall be treated as income which is not passive
 income and any assets which produce income so described shall be treated
 as assets producing income other than passive income. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN FOREIGN CORPORATIONS OWNING
 STOCK IN 25-PERCENT OWNED DOMESTIC CORPORATION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If a foreign corporation owns at least 25
 percent (by value) of the stock of a domestic corporation, for purposes of
 determining whether such foreign corporation is a passive foreign corporation,
 any qualified stock held by such domestic corporation shall be treated as
 an asset which does not produce passive income (and is not held for the
 production of passive income) and any amount included in gross income with
 respect to such stock shall not be treated as passive income. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) QUALIFIED STOCK- For purposes of subparagraph (A),
 the term `qualified stock' means any stock in a C corporation which is a
 domestic corporation and which is not a regulated investment company or
 real estate investment trust. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) TREATMENT OF CORPORATION WHICH WAS A PFIC- A corporation
 shall be treated as a passive foreign corporation for any taxable year
 beginning before January 1, 1993, if and only if such corporation was a
 passive foreign investment company under this part as in effect for such
 taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) SEPARATE INTERESTS TREATED AS SEPARATE CORPORATIONS-
 Under regulations prescribed by the Secretary, where necessary to carry
 out the purposes of this part, separate classes of stock (or other
 interests) in a corporation shall be treated as interests in separate
 corporations. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN LEASED PROPERTY- For purposes
 of section 1296(a)(2)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Any tangible personal property with
 respect to which the foreign corporation is the lessee under a lease with
 a term of at least 12 months shall be treated as an asset actually held by
 such corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) DETERMINATION OF VALUE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The value of any asset to which paragraph
 (1) applies shall be the lesser of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the fair market value of such property, or [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the unamortized portion (as determined under
 regulations prescribed by the Secretary) of the present value of the payments
 under the lease for the use of such property. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) PRESENT VALUE- For purposes of subparagraph (A),
 the present value of payments described in subparagraph (A)(ii) shall be
 determined in the manner provided in regulations prescribed by the Secretary--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) as of the beginning of the lease term, and [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) except as provided in such regulations, by using a
 discount rate equal to the applicable Federal rate determined under section
 1274(d)-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) by substituting the lease term for the term of the
 debt instrument, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) without regard to paragraph (2) or (3)
 thereof. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) EXCEPTIONS- This subsection shall not apply in any
 case where-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the lessor is a related person (as defined in the last
 sentence of section 1296(b)(2)) with respect to the foreign corporation,
 or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) a principal purpose of leasing the property was to
 avoid the provisions of this part. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) ELECTION BY CERTAIN PASSIVE FOREIGN CORPORATIONS TO
 BE TREATED AS A DOMESTIC CORPORATION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of this title, if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) a passive foreign corporation would qualify as a
 regulated investment company under part I of subchapter M if such passive
 foreign corporation were a domestic corporation, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such passive foreign corporation meets such requirements
 as the Secretary shall prescribe to ensure that the taxes imposed by this
 title on such passive foreign corporation are paid, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) such passive foreign corporation makes an election to
 have this paragraph apply and waives all benefits which are granted by the
 United States under any treaty and to which such corporation would otherwise
 be entitled by reason of being a resident of another country, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] such corporation shall be treated as a domestic
 corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CERTAIN RULES MADE APPLICABLE- Rules similar to
 the rules of paragraphs (2), (3), (4)(A), and (5) of section 953(d) shall
 apply with respect to any corporation making an election under paragraph
 (1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(g) SPECIAL RULES FOR CERTAIN TAXPAYERS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) TAX-EXEMPT ORGANIZATIONS- In the case of any
 organization exempt from tax under section 501-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) this part shall apply to any stock in a passive
 foreign corporation owned (or treated as owned under section 1294(e)) by
 such organization only to the extent that a dividend on such stock would
 be taken into account in determining the unrelated business taxable income
 of such organization, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) to the extent that this part applies to any such stock,
 this part shall be applied in the same manner as if such organization were
 not exempt from tax under section 501(a). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TREATMENT OF STOCK HELD BY POOLED INCOME FUND- If
 stock in a passive foreign corporation is owned (or treated as owned under
 section 1294(e)) by a pooled income fund (as defined in section 642(c)(5))
 and no portion of any gain from a disposition of such stock may be allocated
 to income under the terms of the governing instrument of such fund--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) section 1293 shall not apply to any gain on a
 disposition of such stock by such fund if (without regard to section 1293)
 a deduction would be allowable with respect to such gain under section
 642(c)(3), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) subpart A shall not apply with respect to such stock,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) in determining whether section 1293 applies to any
 distribution in respect of such stock, such stock shall be treated as
 failing to qualify for the exceptions under section 1294(a)(1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(h) INFORMATION FROM SHAREHOLDERS- Every United States
 person who owns stock in any passive foreign corporation shall furnish
 with respect to such corporation such information as the Secretary may
 prescribe. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) REGULATIONS- The Secretary shall prescribe such
 regulations as may be necessary or appropriate to carry out the purposes
 of this part, including regulations-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) providing that gross income shall be determined
 without regard to section 1293 for such purposes as may be specified in
 such regulations, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) to prevent avoidance of the provisions of this part
 through changes in citizenship or residence status.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) INSTALLMENT SALES TREATMENT NOT AVAILABLE- Paragraph
 (2) of section 453(k) is amended by striking `or' at the end of subparagraph
 (A), by inserting `or' at the end of subparagraph (B), and by adding at
 the end thereof the following new subparagraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) stock in a passive foreign corporation (as defined
 in section 1296) if section 1293 applies to such sale,'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) TREATMENT OF MARK-TO-MARKET GAIN UNDER SECTION 4982-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) Subsection (e) of section 4982 is amended by adding

 [Struck out->]   `(6) TREATMENT OF GAIN RECOGNIZED UNDER SECTION 1291- For
 purposes of determining a regulated investment company's ordinary income--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) notwithstanding paragraph (1)(C), section 1291 shall
 be applied as if such company's taxable year ended on October 31, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any ordinary gain or loss from an actual disposition of

 [Struck out->] In the case of a company making an election under paragraph
 (4), the preceding sentence shall be applied by substituting the last day
 of the company's taxable year for October 31.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) Subsection (b) of section 852 is amended by adding at

 FOREIGN CORPORATIONS- To the extent provided in regulations, the taxable

 [Struck out->]   (3) Subsection (c) of section 852 is amended by inserting

 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Except as otherwise provided in this

 December 31, 1992, and [<-Struck out]

 1992. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] PART II--TREATMENT OF CONTROLLED FOREIGN CORPORATIONS
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4411. GAIN ON CERTAIN STOCK SALES BY CONTROLLED FOREIGN
 CORPORATIONS TREATED AS DIVIDENDS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Section 964 (relating to miscellaneous
 provisions) is amended by adding at the end thereof the following new
 subsection: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) GAIN ON CERTAIN STOCK SALES BY CONTROLLED FOREIGN
 CORPORATIONS TREATED AS DIVIDENDS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If a controlled foreign corporation sells
 or exchanges stock in any other foreign corporation, gain recognized on such
 sale or exchange shall be included in the gross income of such controlled
 foreign corporation as a dividend to the same extent that it would have been
 so included under section 1248(a) if such controlled foreign corporation
 were a United States person. For purposes of determining the amount which
 would have been so includible, the determination of whether such other
 foreign corporation was a controlled foreign corporation shall be made
 without regard to the preceding sentence. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SAME COUNTRY EXCEPTION NOT APPLICABLE- Clause (i)
 of section 954(c)(3)(A) shall not apply to any amount treated as a dividend
 by reason of paragraph (1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) CLARIFICATION OF DEEMED SALES- For purposes of this
 subsection, a controlled foreign corporation shall be treated as having
 sold or exchanged any stock if, under any provision of this subtitle, such
 controlled foreign corporation is treated as having gain from the sale or
 exchange of such stock.'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) AMENDMENT OF SECTION 904(d)- Clause (i) of section
 904(d)(2)(E) is amended by striking `and except as provided in regulations,
 the taxpayer was a United States shareholder in such corporation'. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) The amendment made by subsection (a) shall apply to
 gain recognized on transactions occurring after the date of the enactment
 of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) The amendment made by subsection (b) shall apply to
 distributions after the date of the enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] SEC. 4413. MISCELLANEOUS MODIFICATIONS TO SUBPART F. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) SECTION 1248 GAIN TAKEN INTO ACCOUNT IN DETERMINING
 PRO RATA SHARE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Paragraph (2) of section 951(a) (defining
 pro rata share of subpart F income) is amended by adding at the end thereof
 the following new sentence: `For purposes of subparagraph (B), any gain
 included in the gross income of any person as a dividend under section 1248

 [Struck out->] SEC. 4414. INDIRECT FOREIGN TAX CREDIT ALLOWED FOR CERTAIN
 LOWER TIER COMPANIES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) SECTION 902 CREDIT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Subsection (b) of section 902 (relating
