 corporations) is amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) DEEMED TAXES INCREASED IN CASE OF CERTAIN LOWER TIER
 CORPORATIONS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) any foreign corporation is a member of a qualified
 group, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such foreign corporation owns 10 percent or more of
 the voting stock of another member of such group from which it receives
 dividends in any taxable year, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] such foreign corporation shall be deemed to have paid the
 same proportion of such other member's post-1986 foreign income taxes as
 would be determined under subsection (a) if such foreign corporation were
 a domestic corporation. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) QUALIFIED GROUP- For purposes of paragraph (1),
 the term `qualified group' means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the foreign corporation described in subsection (a),
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any other foreign corporation if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the domestic corporation owns at least 5 percent
 of the voting stock of such other foreign corporation indirectly through
 a chain of foreign corporations connected through stock ownership of at
 least 10 percent of their voting stock, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the foreign corporation described in subsection (a)
 is the first tier corporation in such chain, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) such other corporation is not below the sixth tier
 in such chain, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] The term `qualified group' shall not include any foreign
 corporation below the third tier in the chain referred to in clause (i) unless
 such foreign corporation is a controlled foreign corporation (as defined in
 section 957) and the domestic corporation is a United States shareholder
 (as defined in section 951(b)) in such foreign corporation. Paragraph (1)
 shall apply to those taxes paid by a member of the qualified group below
 the third tier only with respect to periods during which it was a controlled
 foreign corporation.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) CONFORMING AMENDMENTS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) Subparagraph (B) of section 902(c)(3) is amended by

 [Struck out->] PART III--OTHER PROVISIONS [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4421. EXCHANGE RATE USED IN TRANSLATING FOREIGN
 TAXES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) ACCRUED TAXES TRANSLATED BY USING AVERAGE RATE FOR
 YEAR TO WHICH TAXES RELATE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Subsection (a) of section 986 (relating
 to translation of foreign taxes) is amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) FOREIGN INCOME TAXES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) TRANSLATION OF ACCRUED TAXES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- For purposes of determining the amount of
 the foreign tax credit, in the case of a taxpayer who takes foreign income
 taxes into account when accrued, the amount of any foreign income taxes (and
 any adjustment thereto) shall be translated into dollars by using the average
 exchange rate for the taxable year to which such taxes relate. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) EXCEPTION FOR TAXES NOT PAID WITHIN FOLLOWING 2 YEARS-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) Subparagraph (A) shall not apply to any foreign income
 taxes paid after the date 2 years after the close of the taxable year to
 which such taxes relate. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) Subparagraph (A) shall not apply to taxes paid before
 the beginning of the taxable year to which such taxes relate. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) EXCEPTION FOR INFLATIONARY CURRENCIES- To the extent
 provided in regulations, subparagraph (A) shall not apply to any foreign
 income taxes the liability for which is denominated in any currency determined
 to be an inflationary currency under such regulations. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) CROSS REFERENCE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]  `For adjustments where tax is not paid within 2 years,
 see section 905(c). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TRANSLATION OF TAXES TO WHICH PARAGRAPH (1) DOES NOT
 APPLY- For purposes of determining the amount of the foreign tax credit, in
 the case of any foreign income taxes to which subparagraph (A) of paragraph
 (1) does not apply-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) such taxes shall be translated into dollars using the
 exchange rates as of the time such taxes were paid to the foreign country
 or possession of the United States, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) any adjustment to the amount of such taxes shall be
 translated into dollars using-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) except as provided in clause (ii), the exchange rate as
 of the time when such adjustment is paid to the foreign country or possession,
 or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) in the case of any refund or credit of foreign income
 taxes, using the exchange rate as of the time of the original payment of
 such foreign income taxes. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) FOREIGN INCOME TAXES- For purposes of this subsection,
 the term `foreign income taxes' means any income, war profits, or excess
 profits taxes paid or accrued to any foreign country or to any possession
 of the United States.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) ADJUSTMENT WHEN NOT PAID WITHIN 2 YEARS AFTER YEAR
 TO WHICH TAXES RELATE- Subsection (c) of section 905 is amended to read as
 follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) ADJUSTMENTS TO ACCRUED TAXES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) accrued taxes when paid differ from the amounts
 claimed as credits by the taxpayer, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) accrued taxes are not paid before the date 2 years after
 the close of the taxable year to which such taxes relate, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) any tax paid is refunded in whole or in part,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] the taxpayer shall notify the Secretary, who shall redetermine
 the amount of the tax for the year or years affected. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULE FOR TAXES NOT PAID WITHIN 2 YEARS- In
 making the redetermination under paragraph (1), no credit shall be allowed
 for accrued taxes not paid before the date referred to in subparagraph (B)
 of paragraph (1). Any such taxes if subsequently paid shall be taken into
 account for the taxable year in which paid and no redetermination under
 this section shall be made on account of such payment. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) ADJUSTMENTS- The amount of tax due on any
 redetermination under paragraph (1) (if any) shall be paid by the taxpayer on
 notice and demand by the Secretary, and the amount of tax overpaid (if any)
 shall be credited or refunded to the taxpayer in accordance with subchapter
 B of chapter 66 (section 6511 et seq.). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) BOND REQUIREMENTS- In the case of any tax accrued but
 not paid, the Secretary, as a condition precedent to the allowance of the
 credit provided in this subpart, may require the taxpayer to give a bond,
 with sureties satisfactory to and approved by the Secretary, in such sum
 as the Secretary may require, conditioned on the payment by the taxpayer of
 any amount of tax found due on any such redetermination. Any such bond shall
 contain such further conditions as the Secretary may require. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) OTHER SPECIAL RULES- In any redetermination under
 paragraph (1) by the Secretary of the amount of tax due from the taxpayer for
 the year or years affected by a refund, the amount of the taxes refunded
 for which credit has been allowed under this section shall be reduced
 by the amount of any tax described in section 901 imposed by the foreign
 country or possession of the United States with respect to such refund;
 but no credit under this subpart, or deduction under section 164, shall be
 allowed for any taxable year with respect to any such tax imposed on the
 refund. No interest shall be assessed or collected on any amount of tax
 due on any redetermination by the Secretary, resulting from a refund to
 the taxpayer, for any period before the receipt of such refund, except to
 the extent interest was paid by the foreign country or possession of the
 United States on such refund for such period.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) AUTHORITY TO USE AVERAGE RATES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Subsection (a) of section 986 (relating
 to foreign taxes) is amended by adding at the end thereof the following
 new paragraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) AUTHORITY TO PERMIT USE OF AVERAGE RATES- To the extent
 prescribed in regulations, the average exchange rate for the period (specified
 in such regulations) during which the taxes or adjustment is paid may be used
 instead of the exchange rate as of the time of such payment.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) DETERMINATION OF AVERAGE RATES- Subsection (c) of

 [Struck out->]   (3) CONFORMING AMENDMENTS- Subsection (b) of section 989
 is amended by striking `weighted' each place it appears. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section shall
 apply to taxes paid or accrued in taxable years beginning after December 31,
 1991. [<-Struck out]

 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1491. Recognition of gain. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `Sec. 1492. Exceptions. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 1491. RECOGNITION OF GAIN. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `In the case of any transfer of property by a United States
 person to a foreign corporation as paid-in surplus or as a contribution
 to capital, to a foreign estate or trust, or to a foreign partnership,
 for purposes of this subtitle, such transfer shall be treated as a sale
 or exchange for an amount equal to the fair market value of the property
 transferred, and the transferor shall recognize as gain the excess of--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) the fair market value of the property so transferred,
 over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the adjusted basis (for purposes of determining gain)
 of such property in the hands of the transferor.' [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] Subtitle E--Treatment of Intangibles [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4501. AMORTIZATION OF GOODWILL AND CERTAIN OTHER
 INTANGIBLES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Part VI of subchapter B of chapter 1
 (relating to itemized deductions for individuals and corporations) is
 amended by adding at the end thereof the following new section: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 197. AMORTIZATION OF GOODWILL AND CERTAIN OTHER
 INTANGIBLES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) GENERAL RULE- A taxpayer shall be entitled to
 an amortization deduction with respect to any amortizable section 197
 intangible. The amount of such deduction shall be determined by amortizing
 the adjusted basis (for purposes of determining gain) of such intangible
 ratably over the 14-year period beginning with the month in which such
 intangible was acquired. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) NO OTHER DEPRECIATION OR AMORTIZATION DEDUCTION
 ALLOWABLE- Except as provided in subsection (a), no depreciation or
 amortization deduction shall be allowable with respect to any amortizable
 section 197 intangible. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) AMORTIZABLE SECTION 197 INTANGIBLE- For purposes of
 this section-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 section, the term `amortizable section 197 intangible' means any section
 197 intangible-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) which is acquired by the taxpayer after the date of
 the enactment of this section, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) which is held in connection with the conduct of a
 trade or business or an activity described in section 212. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) EXCLUSION OF SELF-CREATED INTANGIBLES, ETC- The term
 `amortizable section 197 intangible' shall not include any section 197
 intangible-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) which is not described in subparagraph (D), (E), or
 (F) of subsection (d)(1), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) which is created by the taxpayer. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] This paragraph shall not apply if the intangible is created in
 connection with a transaction (or series of related transactions) involving
 the acquisition of assets constituting a trade or business or substantial
 portion thereof. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) ANTI-CHURNING RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]  `For exclusion of intangibles acquired in certain
 transactions, see subsection (f)(9). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) SECTION 197 INTANGIBLE- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 section, the term `section 197 intangible' means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) goodwill, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) going concern value, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) any of the following intangible items: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) workforce in place including its composition and terms
 and conditions (contractual or otherwise) of its employment, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) business books and records, operating systems,
 or any other information base (including lists or other information with
 respect to current or prospective customers), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) any patent, copyright, formula, process, design,
 pattern, knowhow, format, or other similar item, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iv) any customer-based intangible, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(v) any supplier-based intangible, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(vi) any other similar item, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) any license, permit, or other right granted by a
 governmental unit or an agency or instrumentality thereof, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) any covenant not to compete (or other arrangement to
 the extent such arrangement has substantially the same effect as a covenant
 not to compete) entered into in connection with an acquisition (directly
 or indirectly) of an interest in a trade or business or substantial portion
 thereof, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(F) any franchise, trademark, or trade name. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CUSTOMER-BASED INTANGIBLE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The term `customer-based intangible'
 means-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) composition of market, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) market share, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) any other value resulting from future provision
 of goods or services pursuant to relationships (contractual or otherwise)
 in the ordinary course of business with customers. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) SPECIAL RULE FOR FINANCIAL INSTITUTIONS- In the case
 of a financial institution, the term `customer-based intangible' includes
 deposit base and similar items. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) SUPPLIER-BASED INTANGIBLE- The term `supplier-based
 intangible' means any value resulting from future acquisitions of goods
 or services pursuant to relationships (contractual or otherwise) in the
 ordinary course of business with suppliers of goods or services to be used
 or sold by the taxpayer. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) EXCEPTIONS- For purposes of this section, the
 term `section 197 intangible' shall not include any of the following:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) FINANCIAL INTERESTS- Any interest-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) in a corporation, partnership, trust, or estate, or
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) under an existing futures contract, foreign currency
 contract, notional principal contract, interest rate swap, or other similar
 financial contract. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) LAND- Any interest in land. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) COMPUTER SOFTWARE- Any-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) computer software which is readily available for
 purchase  by the general public, is subject to a nonexclusive license,
 and has not been substantially modified, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) other computer software which is not acquired in a
 transaction (or series of related transactions) involving the acquisition
 of assets constituting a trade or business or substantial portion
 thereof. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of the preceding sentence, the term `computer
 software' means any program designed to cause a computer to perform a desired
 function; except that such term shall not include any data base or similar
 item. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) CERTAIN INTERESTS OR RIGHTS ACQUIRED SEPARATELY-
 Any of the following not acquired in a transaction (or series of related
 transactions) referred to in paragraph (3)(B): [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) Any interest in a film, sound recording, video tape,
 book, or similar property. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) Any right to receive tangible property or services under
 a contract or granted by a governmental unit or agency or instrumentality
 thereof. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) Any interest in a patent or copyright. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) INTERESTS UNDER LEASES AND DEBT INSTRUMENTS- Any
 interest under-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) an existing lease of tangible property, or [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) except as provided in subsection (d)(2)(B), any
 existing indebtedness. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(6) TREATMENT OF SPORTS FRANCHISES- A franchise to engage
 in professional football, basketball, baseball, or other professional sport,
 and any item acquired in connection with such a franchise. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) SPECIAL RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN DISPOSITIONS, ETC- If there
 is a disposition of any amortizable section 197 intangible acquired in
 a transaction or series of related transactions (or any such intangible
 becomes worthless) and one or more other amortizable section 197 intangibles
 acquired in such transaction or series of related transactions are retained--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) no loss shall be recognized by reason of such
 disposition (or such worthlessness), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) appropriate adjustments to the adjusted bases of
 such retained intangibles shall be made for any loss not recognized under
 subparagraph (A). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] All persons treated as a single taxpayer under section 41(f)
 shall be so treated for purposes of the preceding sentence. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN TRANSFERS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- In the case of any section 197 intangible
 transferred in a transaction described in subparagraph (B), the transferee
 shall be treated as the transferor for purposes of applying this section with
 respect to so much of the adjusted basis in the hands of the transferee as
 does not exceed the adjusted basis in the hands of the transferor. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) TRANSACTIONS COVERED- The transactions described in
 this subparagraph are-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) any transaction described in section 332, 351, 361,
 721, 731, 1031, or 1033, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) any transaction between members of the same affiliated
 group during any taxable year for which a consolidated return is made by
 such group. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) TREATMENT OF AMOUNTS PAID PURSUANT TO COVENANTS NOT
 TO COMPETE, ETC- Any amount paid or incurred pursuant to a covenant or
 arrangement referred to in subsection (d)(1)(E) shall be treated as an
 amount chargeable to capital account. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) TREATMENT OF FRANCHISES, ETC-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) FRANCHISE- The term `franchise' has the meaning given
 to such term by section 1253(b)(1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) TREATMENT OF RENEWALS- Any renewal of a franchise,
 trademark, or trade name (or of a license, a permit, or other right referred
 to in subsection (d)(1)(D)) shall be treated as an acquisition. The preceding
 sentence shall only apply with respect to costs incurred in connection with
 such renewal. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) CERTAIN AMOUNTS NOT TAKEN INTO ACCOUNT- Any amount
 to which section 1253(d)(1) applies shall not be taken into account under
 this section. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN REINSURANCE TRANSACTIONS- In the
 case of any amortizable section 197 intangible resulting from an assumption
 reinsurance transaction, the amount taken into account as the adjusted basis
 of such intangible under this section shall be the excess of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the amount paid or incurred by the acquirer under
 the assumption reinsurance transaction, over [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the amount required to be capitalized under section
 848 in connection with such transaction. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] Subsection (b) shall not apply to any amount required to be
 capitalized under section 848. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(6) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN SUBLEASES- For purposes of this
 section, a sublease shall be treated in the same manner as a lease of the
 underlying property involved. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(7) TREATMENT AS DEPRECIABLE- For purposes of this chapter,
 any amortizable section 197 intangible shall be treated as property which
 is of a character subject to the allowance for depreciation provided in
 section 167. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(8) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN INCREMENTS IN VALUE- This section
 shall not apply to any increment in value if, without regard to this section,
 such increment is properly taken into account in determining the cost of
 property which is not a section 197 intangible. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(9) ANTI-CHURNING RULES- For purposes of this section--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The term `amortizable section 197
 intangible' shall not include any section 197 intangible which is described
 in subparagraph (A) or (B) of subsection (d)(1) (or for which depreciation
 or amortization would not have been allowable but for this section) and
 which is acquired by the taxpayer after the date of the enactment of this
 section, if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the intangible was held or used at any time on or after
 July 25, 1991, and on or before such date of enactment by the taxpayer or
 a related person, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) the intangible was acquired from a person who held
 such intangible at any time on or after July 25, 1991, and on or before
 such date of enactment, and, as part of the transaction, the user of such
 intangible does not change, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) the taxpayer grants the right to use such intangible
 to a person (or a person related to such person) who held or used such
 intangible at any time on or after July 25, 1991, and on or before such
 date of enactment. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of this subparagraph, the determination of whether
 the user of property changes as part of a transaction shall be determined
 in accordance with regulations prescribed by the Secretary. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) RELATED PERSON DEFINED- For purposes of this paragraph--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) RELATED PERSON- A person (hereinafter in this
 paragraph referred to as the `related person') is related to any person if--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) the related person bears a relationship to such person
 specified in section 267(b) or section 707(b)(1), or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the related person and such person are engaged in
 trades or businesses under common control (within the meaning of subparagraphs
 (A) and (B) of section 41(f)(1)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of subclause (I), in applying section 267(b) or
 707(b)(1), `20 percent' shall be substituted for `50 percent'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) TIME FOR MAKING DETERMINATION- A person shall
 be treated as related to another person if such relationship exists
 immediately before or immediately after the acquisition of the intangible
 involved. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) ACQUISITIONS BY REASON OF DEATH- Subparagraph (A)
 shall not apply to the acquisition of any property by the taxpayer if the
 basis of the property in the hands of the taxpayer is determined under
 section 1014(a). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) SPECIAL RULE FOR PARTNERSHIPS- With respect to any
 increase in the basis of partnership property under section 732, 734, or
 743, determinations under this paragraph shall be made at the partner level
 and each partner shall be treated as having owned and used such partner's
 proportionate share of the partnership assets. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(E) ANTI-ABUSE RULES- The term `amortizable section
 197 intangible' does not include any section 197 intangible acquired in
 a transaction, one of the principal purposes of which is to avoid the
 requirement of subsection (c)(1) that the intangible be acquired after
 the date of the enactment of this section or to avoid the provisions of
 subparagraph (A). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(g) REGULATIONS- The Secretary shall prescribe such
 regulations as may be appropriate to carry out the purposes of this section,
 including such regulations as may be appropriate to prevent avoidance of the
 purposes of this section through related persons or otherwise.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) MODIFICATIONS TO DEPRECIATION RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN PROPERTY EXCLUDED FROM SECTION
 197- Section 167 (relating to depreciation deduction) is amended
 by redesignating subsection (f) as subsection (g) and by inserting
 after subsection (e) the following new subsection: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN PROPERTY EXCLUDED FROM SECTION 197-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) COMPUTER SOFTWARE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- If a depreciation deduction is allowable
 under subsection (a) with respect to any computer software, such deduction
 shall be computed by using the straight line method and a useful life of
 36 months. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) COMPUTER SOFTWARE- For purposes of this section,
 the term `computer software' has the meaning given to such term by the last
 sentence of section 197(e)(3); except that such term shall not include any
 such software which is an amortizable section 197 intangible. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) CERTAIN INTERESTS OR RIGHTS ACQUIRED SEPARATELY-
 If a depreciation deduction is allowable under subsection (a) with respect
 to any property described in subparagraph (B) or (C) of section 197(e)(4),
 such deduction shall be computed in accordance with regulations prescribed
 by the Secretary.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) ALLOCATION OF BASIS IN CASE OF LEASED PROPERTY-
 Subsection (c) of section 167 is amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) BASIS FOR DEPRECIATION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- The basis on which exhaustion, wear and
 tear, and obsolescence are to be allowed in respect of any property shall be
 the adjusted basis provided in section 1011, for the purpose of determining
 the gain on the sale or other disposition of such property. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) SPECIAL RULE FOR PROPERTY SUBJECT TO LEASE- If any
 property is acquired subject to a lease-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) no portion of the adjusted basis shall be allocated
 to the leasehold interest, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the entire adjusted basis shall be taken into account
 in determining the depreciation deduction (if any) with respect to the
 property subject to the lease.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) AMENDMENTS TO SECTION 1253- Subsection (d) of section
 1253 is amended by striking paragraphs (2), (3), (4), and (5) and inserting
 the following: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) OTHER PAYMENTS- Any amount paid or incurred on account
 of a transfer, sale, or other disposition of a franchise, trademark, or
 trade name to which paragraph (1) does not apply shall be treated as an
 amount chargeable to capital account. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) RENEWALS, ETC- For purposes of determining the term of
 a transfer agreement under this section, there shall be taken into account
 all renewal options (and any other period for which the parties reasonably
 expect the agreement to be renewed).' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (d) AMENDMENT TO SECTION 848- Subsection (g) of section
 848 is amended by striking `this section' and inserting `this section or
 section 197'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (e) AMENDMENTS TO SECTION 1060-  [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->]   (g) EFFECTIVE DATE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this
 subsection, the amendments made by this section shall apply with respect to
 property acquired after the date of the enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) ELECTION TO HAVE AMENDMENTS APPLY TO PROPERTY ACQUIRED
 AFTER JULY 25, 1991-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) IN GENERAL- If an election under this paragraph applies
 to the taxpayer-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (i) the amendments made by this section shall apply to
 property acquired by the taxpayer after July 25, 1991, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) subsection (c)(1)(A) of section 197 of the Internal
 Revenue Code of 1986 (as added by this section) (and so much of subsection
 (f)(9)(A) of such section 197 as precedes clause (i) thereof) shall be
 applied with respect to the taxpayer by treating July 25, 1991, as the date
 of the enactment of such section, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (iii) in applying subsection (f)(9) of such section,
 with respect to any property acquired by the taxpayer on or before the
 date of the enactment of this Act, only holding or use on July 25, 1991,
 shall be taken into account. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) ELECTION- An election under this paragraph shall be
 made at such time and in such manner as the Secretary of the Treasury or
 his delegate may prescribe. Such an election by any taxpayer, once made--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (i) may be revoked only with the consent of the Secretary,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) shall apply to the taxpayer making such election
 and any other taxpayer under common control with the taxpayer (within the
 meaning of subparagraphs (A) and (B) of section 41(f)(1) of such Code)
 at any time after November 22, 1991, and on or before the date on which
 such election is made. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (3) ELECTION TO HAVE AMENDMENTS APPLY TO PROPERTY ACQUIRED
 IN ALL OPEN YEARS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) IN GENERAL- If an election under this paragraph applies
 to the taxpayer-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (i) the amendments made by this section shall apply to
 property acquired by the taxpayer after the date referred to in subparagraph
 (B), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) subsection (c)(1)(A) of section 197 of the Internal
 Revenue Code of 1986 (as added by this section) shall be applied with
 respect to the taxpayer by treating the date referred to in subparagraph
 (B) as the date of the enactment of such section, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (iii) subsection (f)(9) of such section 197 shall not apply
 with respect to any property acquired by the taxpayer on or before July 25,
 1991, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (iv) in applying subsection (f)(9) of such section 197
 with respect to property acquired by the taxpayer after July 25, 1991,
 and on or before the date of the enactment of this Act, the modifications
 to such subsection contained in clauses (ii) and (iii) of paragraph (2)(A)
 shall apply. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) DATE- For purposes of subparagraph (A), the date
 referred to in this subparagraph is the first day of the first taxable year
 in a series of consecutive taxable years all of which are open years. For
 purposes of the preceding sentence, a taxable year is an open year if the
 period prescribed by section 6501 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 for
 the assessment of any tax for such taxable year had not expired before July
 25, 1991 (determined without regard to subparagraph (C)(iii)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (C) EFFECT OF ELECTION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (i) 17-YEAR AMORTIZATION PERIOD- If an election under this
 paragraph applies to the taxpayer, section 197(a) of the Internal Revenue
 Code of 1986 shall be applied with respect to all property to which the
 amendments made by this section apply and which are acquired by the taxpayer
 on or before the date of the enactment of this Act by substituting `17-year
 period' for `14-year period'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) NO INTEREST ALLOWED ON REFUNDS- No interest shall
 be payable on any refund of tax resulting from the provisions of this
 paragraph. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (iii) EXTENSION OF STATUTE- If the assessment of any
 deficiency of tax attributable to an election under this paragraph is
 barred on the date of the enactment of this Act or at any time within the
 2-year period beginning on the date on which such election is made by any
 law or rule of law, such deficiency may, nevertheless, be assessed if such
 assessment is made within such 2-year period. If credit or refund of any tax
 attributable to an election under this paragraph is barred on the date of
 the enactment of this Act or at any time within the 2-year period beginning
 on the date on which such election is made by any law or rule of law, such
 credit or refund may, nevertheless, be allowed or made if claim therefore
 is made within such 2-year period. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (D) ELECTION- An election under this paragraph shall be
 made at such time and in such manner as the Secretary of the Treasury or
 his delegate may prescribe. Such an election by any taxpayer, once made--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (i) may be revoked only with the consent of the Secretary,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) shall apply to the taxpayer making such election
 and any other taxpayer under common control with the taxpayer (within the
 meaning of subparagraphs (A) and (B) of section 41(f)(1) of such Code)
 at any time after November 22, 1991, and on or before the date on which
 such election is made. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (E) SPECIAL RULE FOR CERTAIN ACQUISITIONS IN CLOSED YEARS-
 If-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (i) an election under this paragraph applies to the taxpayer,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) there was an agreement between the taxpayer and
 the Internal Revenue Service with respect to the amortization of any
 intangibles which were acquired by the taxpayer before the date referred
 to in subparagraph (B), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (iii) as of February 14, 1992, there was an active dispute
 between the taxpayer and the Internal Revenue Service by reason of the
 Internal Revenue Service taking a position inconsistent with such agreement,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] the amortization of such intangibles in open years shall be
 made in accordance with the agreement referred to in clause (ii). [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   (4) ELECTIVE BINDING CONTRACT EXCEPTION-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) IN GENERAL- The amendments made by this section shall
 not apply to any acquisition of property by the taxpayer if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (i) such acquisition is pursuant to a written binding
 contract in effect on February 14, 1992, and at all times thereafter before
 such acquisition, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) an election under paragraph (2) or (3) does not apply
 to the taxpayer, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (iii) the taxpayer makes an election under this paragraph
 with respect to such contract. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) ELECTION- An election under this paragraph shall be
 made at such time and in such manner as the Secretary of the Treasury or
 his delegate shall prescribe. Such an election, once made-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (i) may be revoked only with the consent of the Secretary,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) shall apply to all property acquired pursuant to the
 contract with respect to which such election was made. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] Subtitle F--Other Income Tax Provisions [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] PART I--PROVISIONS RELATING TO SUBCHAPTER S CORPORATIONS
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4601. DETERMINATION OF WHETHER CORPORATION HAS 1 CLASS
 OF STOCK. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Paragraph (4) of section 1361(c) is
 amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) DETERMINATION OF WHETHER CORPORATION HAS 1 CLASS
 OF STOCK- For purposes of subsection (b)(1)(D), a corporation shall be
 treated as having 1 class of stock if all outstanding shares of stock of
 the corporation confer identical rights to distributions and liquidation
 proceeds. The preceding sentence shall apply whether or not there are
 differences in voting rights among such shares.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendment made by subsection (a)
 shall apply to taxable years beginning after December 31, 1982. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4602. AUTHORITY TO VALIDATE CERTAIN INVALID
 ELECTIONS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Subsection (f) of section 1362 (relating
 to inadvertent terminations) is amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) INADVERTENT INVALID ELECTIONS OR TERMINATIONS- If--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) an election under subsection (a) by any corporation--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) was not effective for the taxable year for which made
 (determined without regard to subsection (b)(2)) by reason of a failure to
 meet the requirements of section 1361(b) or to obtain shareholder consents,
 or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) was terminated under paragraph (2) or (3) of subsection
 (d), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the Secretary determines that the circumstances
 resulting in such ineffectiveness or termination were inadvertent,
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) no later than a reasonable period of time after
 discovery of the circumstances resulting in such ineffectiveness or
 termination, steps were taken-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) so that the corporation is a small business corporation,
 or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) to acquire the required shareholder consents, and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) the corporation, and each person who was a shareholder
 in the corporation at any time during the period specified pursuant to this
 subsection, agrees to make such adjustments (consistent with the treatment
 of the corporation as an S corporation) as may be required by the Secretary
 with respect to such period, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] then, notwithstanding the circumstances resulting in such
 ineffectiveness or termination, such corporation shall be treated as an S
 corporation during the period specified by the Secretary.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) LATE ELECTIONS- Subsection (b) of section 1362 is amended
 by adding at the end thereof the following new paragraph: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) AUTHORITY TO TREAT LATE ELECTIONS AS TIMELY- If--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) an election under subsection (a) is made for any
 taxable year (determined without regard to paragraph (3)) after the date
 prescribed by this subsection for making such election for such taxable year,
 and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the Secretary determines that there was reasonable
 cause for the failure to timely make such election, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] the Secretary may treat such election as timely made for
 such taxable year (and paragraph (3) shall not apply).' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply with respect to elections for taxable years beginning after

 [Struck out->] PART II--ACCOUNTING PROVISIONS [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4611. MODIFICATIONS TO LOOK-BACK METHOD FOR LONG-TERM
 CONTRACTS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) LOOK-BACK METHOD NOT TO APPLY IN CERTAIN CASES-
 Subsection (b) of section 460 (relating to percentage of completion method)
 is amended by adding at the end thereof the following new paragraph:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(6) ELECTION TO HAVE LOOK-BACK METHOD NOT APPLY IN DE
 MINIMIS CASES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) AMOUNTS TAKEN INTO ACCOUNT AFTER COMPLETION OF CONTRACT-
 Paragraph (1)(B) shall not apply with respect to any taxable year (beginning
 after the taxable year in which the contract is completed) if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the cumulative taxable income (or loss) under the
 contract as of the close of such taxable year, is within [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) 10 percent of the cumulative look-back taxable income
 (or loss) under the contract as of the close of the most recent taxable year
 to which paragraph (1)(B) applied (or would have applied but for subparagraph
 (B)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) DE MINIMIS DISCREPANCIES- Paragraph (1)(B) shall not
 apply in any case to which it would otherwise apply if-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) the cumulative taxable income (or loss) under the
 contract as of the close of each prior contract year, is within [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) 10 percent of the cumulative look-back income (or loss)
 under the contract as of the close of such prior contract year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) DEFINITIONS- For purposes of this paragraph--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) CONTRACT YEAR- The term `contract year' means
 any taxable year for which income is taken into account under the
 contract. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) LOOK-BACK INCOME OR LOSS- The look-back income (or
 loss) is the amount which would be the taxable income (or loss) under the
 contract if the allocation method set forth in paragraph (2)(A) were used
 in determining taxable income. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) DISCOUNTING NOT APPLICABLE- The amounts taken
 into account after the completion of the contract shall be determined
 without regard to any discounting under the 2nd sentence of paragraph
 (2). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) CONTRACTS TO WHICH PARAGRAPH APPLIES- This
 paragraph shall only apply if the taxpayer makes an election under this
 subparagraph. Unless revoked with the consent of the Secretary, such an
 election shall apply to all long-term contracts completed during the
 taxable year for which such election is made or during any subsequent
 taxable year.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) MODIFICATION OF INTEREST RATE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Subparagraph (C) of section 460(b)(2)
 is amended by striking `the overpayment rate established by section 6621'
 and inserting `the adjusted overpayment rate (as defined in paragraph
 (7))'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) ADJUSTED OVERPAYMENT RATE- Subsection (b) of section
 460 is amended by adding at the end thereof the following new paragraph:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(7) ADJUSTED OVERPAYMENT RATE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The adjusted overpayment rate for any
 interest accrual period is the overpayment rate in effect under section
 6621 for the calendar quarter in which such interest accrual period
 begins. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) INTEREST ACCRUAL PERIOD- For purposes of subparagraph
 (A), the term `interest accrual period' means the period-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) beginning on the day after the return due date for
 any taxable year of the taxpayer, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) ending on the return due date for the following
 taxable year. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] For purposes of the preceding sentence, the term `return due
 date' means the date prescribed for filing the return of the tax imposed
 by this chapter (determined without regard to extensions).' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to contracts completed in taxable years ending after the date
 of the enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4612. SIMPLIFIED METHOD FOR CAPITALIZING CERTAIN INDIRECT
 COSTS. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Subsection (i) of section 263A (relating
 to regulations) is amended by striking `and' at the end of paragraph (1),

 [Struck out->] SEC. 4622. BASIS RULES FOR SHARES IN OPEN-END REGULATED
 INVESTMENT COMPANIES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) ADDITIONAL REPORTING REQUIREMENT- Section 6045 (relating
 to returns of brokers) is amended by adding at the end thereof the following
 new subsection: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(f) ADDITIONAL INFORMATION REQUIRED WITH RESPECT TO
 OPEN-END REGULATED INVESTMENT COMPANIES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If any person is required under subsection
 (a) to make a return regarding the gross proceeds from any disposition
 of stock in an open-end regulated investment company, such return shall
 include for each such disposition-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the basis of the stock disposed of (determined by
 reference to the average basis of all of the stock in the account from
 which the disposition was made immediately before the disposition), and
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the portion of such gross proceeds attributable to stock
 held for more than 1 year and the portion not so attributable. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] Determinations under subparagraph (B) shall be made on a
 first-in, first-out, basis and determinations of basis and holding period
 shall be made in such manner as the Secretary may prescribe. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) OPEN-END REGULATED INVESTMENT COMPANY- For purposes of
 this subsection, the term `open-end regulated investment company' means any
 regulated investment company which is offering for sale or has outstanding
 any redeemable security (as defined in section 2(a)(32) of the Investment
 Company Act of 1940) of which it is the issuer. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) INFORMATION TRANSFERS- To the extent provided in
 regulations, there shall be such exchanges of information between brokers
 as such regulations may require for purposes of enabling brokers to meet
 the requirements of this subsection. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) APPLICATION OF SUBSECTION- This subsection shall not
 apply with respect to stock in any account-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) which was established before January 1, 1994, or
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) which includes any stock not acquired by
 purchase.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) BASIS FOR INCOME TAX PURPOSES- Section 1012 of such
 Code is amended-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) by striking `The basis' and inserting `(a) GENERAL RULE-
 The basis', and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) by adding at the end thereof the following new
 subsection: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) SPECIAL RULES FOR STOCK IN OPEN-END REGULATED INVESTMENT
 COMPANIES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- In the case of any disposition of stock
 from a covered account-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) the basis of such stock shall be determined by reference
 to the average basis of all of the stock in such account immediately before
 such disposition, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) the determination of which stock in such account is
 so disposed of shall be made on a first-in, first-out, basis. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) COVERED ACCOUNT- For purposes of this subsection--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- The term `covered account' means any
 account of stock in an open-end regulated investment company if section
 6045(f) applies to such account. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) ELECTION OUT- The term `covered account' shall not
 include any account if, on the taxpayer's return for his first taxable
 year in which a disposition from such account occurs, the taxpayer elects
 to have this subsection not apply to such account.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) TECHNICAL AMENDMENT- Section 6724 of such Code is amended

 [Struck out->] SEC. 4623. NONRECOGNITION TREATMENT FOR CERTAIN TRANSFERS
 BY COMMON TRUST FUNDS TO REGULATED INVESTMENT COMPANIES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Section 584 (relating to common trust
 funds) is amended by redesignating subsection (h) as subsection (i) and by
 inserting after subsection (g) the following  new subsection: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(h) NONRECOGNITION TREATMENT FOR CERTAIN TRANSFERS TO
 REGULATED INVESTMENT COMPANIES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- If-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) a common trust fund transfers substantially all of
 its assets to a regulated investment company in exchange solely for stock
 in such company, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) such stock is distributed by such common trust fund
 to participants in such common trust fund in exchange for their interests
 in such common trust fund, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]  no gain or loss shall be recognized by such common trust
 fund by reason of such transfer or distribution, and no gain or loss shall
 be recognized by any participant in such common trust fund by reason of
 such exchange. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) BASIS RULES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) REGULATED INVESTMENT COMPANY- The basis of any asset
 received by a regulated investment company in a transfer referred to in
 paragraph (1)(A) shall be the same as it would be in the hands of the common
 trust fund. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) PARTICIPANTS- The basis of any stock in a regulated
 investment company which is received in an exchange referred to in paragraph
 (1)(B) shall be the same as that of the property exchanged. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) COMMON TRUST FUND MUST MEET DIVERSIFICATION RULES-
 This subsection shall not apply to any common trust fund which would
 not meet the requirements of section 368(a)(2)(F)(ii) if it were a
 corporation.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendment made by subsection
 (a) shall apply to transfers after the date of the enactment of this
 Act. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] SEC. 4635. REPEAL OF DISPROPORTIONATE PRIVATE BUSINESS USE

 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Except as otherwise provided in this

 required by this section shall be assessed and collected in the same manner

 [Struck out->]   `(2) DUE DATE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) ANNUAL REQUIRED PAYMENTS- The amount of any payment
 required by this section, other than any initial payment, shall be paid
 on or before May 15 of the calendar year following the year in which the
 applicable election year begins. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) INITIAL PAYMENT- The amount of any initial payment
 required by this section shall be paid on or before September 15 of the
 calendar year in which the 1st applicable election year begins. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) INTEREST- For purposes of determining interest,
 any payment required by this section shall be treated as a tax; except

 under this section only with respect to the period from the latest date

 [Struck out->]   `(4) PENALTIES-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- In the case of any failure by any person
 to pay on the date prescribed therefor any amount required by this section,
 other than an initial payment, there shall be imposed on such person a
 penalty of 10 percent of the underpayment. For purposes of the preceding
 sentence, the term `underpayment' means the excess of the amount of the
 payment required under this section over the amount (if any) of such payment
 paid on or before the date prescribed therefor. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) INEFFECTIVE ELECTION- In the case of any failure of

 section on the date prescribed therefor, such entity shall be treated as
 having failed to make an election under section 444. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) NEGLIGENCE AND FRAUD PENALTIES MADE APPLICABLE- For
 purposes of part II of subchapter A of chapter 68, any payment required by
 this section shall be treated as a tax. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) WILLFUL FAILURE- If any partnership or S corporation
 willfully fails to comply with the requirements of this section,
 section 444 shall cease to apply with respect to such partnership or S
 corporation.' [<-Struck out]

 (f)(2).' [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] SEC. 4702. ADJUSTMENTS FOR GIFTS WITHIN 3 YEARS OF DECEDENT'S
 DEATH. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE- Section 2035 is amended to read as follows:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 2035. ADJUSTMENTS FOR CERTAIN GIFTS MADE WITHIN 3
 YEARS OF DECEDENT'S DEATH. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) INCLUSION OF CERTAIN PROPERTY IN GROSS ESTATE- If--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) the decedent made a transfer (by trust or otherwise)
 of an interest in any property, or relinquished a power with respect to
 any property, during the 3-year period ending on the date of the decedent's
 death, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) the value of such property (or an interest therein)
 would have been included in the decedent's gross estate under section 2036,
 2037, 2038, or 2042 if such transferred interest or relinquished power had
 been retained by the decedent on the date of his death, [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] the value of the gross estate shall include the value of any
 property (or interest therein) which would have been so included. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) INCLUSION OF GIFT TAX ON GIFTS MADE DURING 3 YEARS
 BEFORE DECEDENT'S DEATH- The amount of the gross estate (determined without
 regard to this subsection) shall be increased by the amount of any tax
 paid under chapter 12 by the decedent or his estate on any gift made by
 the decedent or his spouse during the 3-year period ending on the date of
 the decedent's death. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) OTHER RULES RELATING TO TRANSFERS WITHIN 3 YEARS OF
 DEATH-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- For purposes of-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) section 303(b) (relating to distributions in redemption
 of stock to pay death taxes), [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) section 2032A (relating to special valuation of
 certain farms, etc., real property), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) subchapter C of chapter 64 (relating to lien for taxes),
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] the value of the gross estate shall include the value of
 all property to the extent of any interest therein of which the decedent
 has at any time made a transfer, by trust or otherwise, during the 3-year
 period ending on the date of the decedent's death. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) COORDINATION WITH SECTION 6166- An estate shall be
 treated as meeting the 35 percent of adjusted gross estate requirement of
 section 6166(a)(1) only if the estate meets such requirement both with and
 without the application of paragraph (1). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) SMALL TRANSFERS- Paragraph (1) shall not apply to any
 transfer (other than a transfer with respect to a life insurance policy)
 made during a calendar year to any donee if the decedent was not required by
 section 6019 (other than by reason of section 6019(a)(2)) to file any gift tax
 return for such year with respect to transfers to such donee. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) EXCEPTION- Subsection (a) shall not apply to any
 bona fide sale for an adequate and full consideration in money or money's
 worth. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN REVOCABLE TRUSTS- For purposes
 of this section and section 2038, any transfer from any portion of a trust
 with respect to which the decedent was the grantor during any period when
 the decedent held the power to revest in the decedent title to such portion
 shall be treated as a transfer made directly by the decedent.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CLERICAL AMENDMENT- The table of sections for part
 III of subchapter A of chapter 11 is amended by striking `gifts' in the
 item relating to section 2035 and inserting `certain gifts'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE- The amendments made by this section
 shall apply to the estates of decedents dying after the date of the enactment
 of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4703. CLARIFICATION OF QUALIFIED TERMINABLE INTEREST
 RULES. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) GENERAL RULE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) ESTATE TAX- Subparagraph (B) of section 2056(b)(7)
 (defining qualified terminable interest property) is amended by adding at
 the end thereof the following new clause: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(v)(i) TREATMENT OF CERTAIN INCOME DISTRIBUTIONS- An income
 interest shall not fail to qualify as a qualified income interest for life
 solely because income for the period after the last distribution date and
 on or before the date of the surviving spouse's death is not required to
 be distributed to the surviving spouse or to the estate of the surviving
 spouse.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) GIFT TAX- Paragraph (3) of section 2523(f) is amended
 by striking `and (iv)' and inserting `, (iv), and (vi)'. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CLARIFICATION OF SUBSEQUENT INCLUSIONS- Section 2044
 is amended by adding at the end thereof the following new subsection:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) CLARIFICATION OF INCLUSION OF CERTAIN INCOME- The
 amount included in the gross estate under subsection (a) shall include
 the amount of any income from the property to which this section applies
 for the period after the last distribution date and on or before the date
 of the decedent's death if such income is not otherwise included in the
 decedent's gross estate.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (c) EFFECTIVE DATE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- The amendments made by this section shall
 apply with respect to the estates of decedents dying, and gifts made,
 after the date of the enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) APPLICATION OF SECTION 2044 TO TRANSFERS BEFORE DATE
 OF ENACTMENT- In the case of the estate of any decedent dying after the
 date of the enactment of this Act, if there was a transfer of property on
 or before such date-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (A) such property shall not be included in the gross estate
 of the decedent under section 2044 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 if
 no prior marital deduction was allowed with respect to such a transfer of
 such property to the decedent, but [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) such property shall be so included if such a deduction
 was allowed. [<-Struck out]

 dying after the date of the enactment of this Act. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (B) EXCEPTION- The amendment made by subsection (a) shall

 [Struck out->]   (i) the decedent dies on or before the date 3 years after
 such date of enactment, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (ii) the decedent was, on such date of enactment, under

 regain his competence to dispose of such property before the date of his
 death. [<-Struck out]

 [Struck out->] Subtitle H--Excise Tax Simplification [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] PART I--FUEL TAX PROVISIONS [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] SEC. 4801. REPEAL OF CERTAIN RETAIL AND USE TAXES. [<-Struck
 out]
 [Struck out->]   (a) IN GENERAL- Section 4041 is amended to read as follows:
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 4041. SPECIAL MOTOR FUELS AND NONCOMMERCIAL AVIATION
 GASOLINE. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(a) SPECIAL MOTOR FUELS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- There is hereby imposed a tax on benzol,
 benzene, naphtha, liquefied petroleum gas, casing head and natural gasoline,
 or any other liquid-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) sold by any person to an owner, lessee, or other
 operator of a motor vehicle or a motorboat for use as a fuel in such motor
 vehicle or motorboat, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) used by any person as a fuel in a motor vehicle or
 motorboat unless there was a taxable sale of such liquid under subparagraph
 (A). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) RATE OF TAX- The rate of the tax imposed by this
 subsection shall be the aggregate rate of tax in effect under section 4081
 at the time of such sale or use. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) CERTAIN FUELS EXEMPT FROM TAX- The tax imposed by
 this subsection shall not apply to gasoline (as defined in section 4082),
 diesel fuel (as defined in section 4092), kerosene, gas oil, or fuel
 oil. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) REDUCED RATES OF TAX ON CERTAIN FUELS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) QUALIFIED METHANOL AND ETHANOL FUEL-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- In the case of any qualified methanol or
 ethanol fuel-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) the Highway Trust Fund financing rate applicable
 under paragraph (2) shall be 5.4 cents per gallon less than the otherwise
 applicable rate (6 cents per gallon less in the case of a mixture none of
 the alcohol in which consists of ethanol), and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the Leaking Underground Storage Tank Trust Fund
 financing rate applicable under paragraph (2) shall be 0.05 cent per
 gallon. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) QUALIFIED METHANOL OR ETHANOL FUEL- The term
 `qualified methanol or ethanol fuel' means any liquid at least 85 percent
 of which consists of methanol, ethanol, or other alcohol produced from a
 substance other than petroleum or natural gas. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) TERMINATION- Clause (i) shall not apply to any sale
 or use after September 30, 2000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) NATURAL GAS-DERIVED METHANOL OR ETHANOL FUEL-
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- In the case of natural gas-derived methanol
 or ethanol fuel-- [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(I) the Highway Trust Fund financing rate applicable
 under paragraph (2) shall be 5.75 cents per gallon, and [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(II) the deficit reduction rate applicable under paragraph
 (2) shall be 1.25 cents per gallon. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) NATURAL GAS-DERIVED METHANOL OR ETHANOL FUEL- The
 term `natural-gas derived methanol or ethanol fuel' means any liquid at
 least 85 percent of which consists of methanol, ethanol, or other alcohol
 produced from natural gas. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) OTHER FUELS CONTAINING ALCOHOL-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(i) IN GENERAL- Under regulations prescribed by the
 Secretary, in the case of any liquid at least 10 percent of which consists of
 alcohol (as defined in section 4081(c)(3)), the Highway Trust Fund financing
 rate applicable under paragraph (2) shall be the comparable  rate under
 section 4081. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(ii) LATER SEPARATION- If any person separates the liquid
 fuel from a mixture of the liquid fuel and alcohol to which clause (i)
 applies, such separation shall be treated as a sale of the liquid fuel. Any
 tax imposed on such sale shall be reduced by the amount (if any) of the
 tax imposed on the sale of such mixture. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(iii) TERMINATION- Clause (i) shall not apply to any sale
 or use after September 30, 2000. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) LIQUEFIED PETROLEUM GAS- The rate of tax applicable
 under paragraph (2) to liquefied petroleum gas shall be determined without
 regard to the Leaking Underground Storage Tank Trust Fund financing rate
 under section 4081. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) EXEMPTION FOR OFF-HIGHWAY BUSINESS USE- No tax shall
 be imposed by paragraph (1) on liquids sold for use or used in an off-highway
 business use (within the meaning of section 6420(f)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(b) NONCOMMERCIAL AVIATION GASOLINE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- There is hereby imposed a tax on gasoline--
 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) sold by any person to an owner, lessee, or other
 operator of an aircraft for use as a fuel in such aircraft in noncommercial
 aviation, or [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(B) used by any person as a fuel in an aircraft in
 noncommercial aviation unless there was a taxable sale of such gasoline
 under subparagraph (A). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] The tax imposed by this paragraph shall be in addition to
 any tax imposed by section 4081. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) RATE OF TAX- The rate of the tax imposed by paragraph
 (1) on any gasoline is the excess of 15 cents a gallon over the sum of the
 Highway Trust Fund financing rate plus the deficit reduction rate at which
 tax was imposed on such gasoline under section 4081. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(3) NONCOMMERCIAL AVIATION- For purposes of this subsection,
 the term `noncommercial aviation' means any use of an aircraft other than
 use in a business of transporting persons or property for compensation
 or hire by air. Such term includes any use of an aircraft, in a business
 described in the preceding sentence, which is properly allocable to any
 transportation exempt from the taxes imposed by sections 4261 and 4271 by
 reason of section 4281 or 4282. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(4) EXEMPTION FOR FUELS CONTAINING ALCOHOL- No tax shall
 be imposed by this subsection on any liquid at least 10 percent of which
 consists of alcohol (as defined in section 4081(c)(3)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(5) EXEMPTION FOR CERTAIN HELICOPTER USES- No tax
 shall be imposed by this subsection on gasoline sold for use or used in a
 helicopter for purposes of providing transportation with respect to which the
 requirements of subsection (e) or (f) of section 4261 are met. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(6) REGISTRATION- Except as provided in regulations
 prescribed by the Secretary, if any gasoline is sold by any person for
 use as a fuel in an aircraft, it shall be presumed for purposes of this
 subsection that a tax imposed by this subsection applies to the sale of such
 gasoline unless the purchaser is registered in such manner (and furnished
 such information in respect of the use of the gasoline) as the Secretary
 shall by regulations provide. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(7) GASOLINE- For purposes of this subsection, the term
 `gasoline' has the meaning given such term by section 4082. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(8) TERMINATION- Paragraph (1) shall not apply to any
 sale or use after December 31, 1995. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(c) EXEMPTION FOR FARM USE-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Under regulations prescribed by the
 Secretary, no tax shall be imposed under this section on any liquid sold
 for use or used on a farm for farming purposes (determined in accordance
 with paragraphs (1), (2), and (3) of section 6420(e)). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TERMINATION- Except with respect to so much of the
 tax imposed by subsection (a) as is determined by reference to the Leaking
 Underground Storage Tank Trust Fund financing rate under section 4081,
 paragraph (1) shall not apply after September 30, 1999. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(d) EXEMPTIONS FOR STATE AND LOCAL GOVERNMENTS, SCHOOLS,
 EXPORTATION, AND SUPPLIES FOR VESSELS AND AIRCRAFT-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(1) IN GENERAL- Under regulations prescribed by the
 Secretary, no tax shall be imposed under this section on any liquid sold
 for use, or used, in an exempt use described in paragraph (4), (5), (6),
 or (7) of section 6420(b). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(2) TERMINATION- Except with respect to so much of the
 tax imposed by subsection (a) as is determined by reference to the Leaking
 Underground Storage Tank Trust Fund financing rate under section 4081,
 after September 30, 1999, paragraph (1) shall not apply to exempt uses
 described in paragraph (4) and (5) of section 6420(b). [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(e) EXEMPTION FOR USE BY CERTAIN AIRCRAFT MUSEUMS- Under
 regulations prescribed by the Secretary, no tax shall be imposed under this
 section on any liquid sold for use or used in an exempt use described in
 section 6420(b)(11).' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (b) CERTAIN ADDITIONAL PURCHASERS OF FUEL TREATED AS
 PRODUCERS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (1) IN GENERAL- Subparagraph (C) of section 4092(b)(1)
 is amended to read as follows: [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(C) REDUCED-TAX PURCHASERS TREATED AS PRODUCERS- Any
 person to whom any fuel is sold in a sale on which the amount of tax
 otherwise required to be paid under section 4091 is reduced under section
 4093 shall be treated as the producer of such fuel. The amount of tax imposed
 by section 4091 on any sale of such fuel by such person shall be reduced by
 the amount of tax imposed under section 4091 (and not credited or refunded)
 on any prior sale of such fuel.' [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   (2) CONFORMING AMENDMENT- Subsection (b) of section 4093
 is amended by inserting `(as defined in section 4092(b) without regard to
 paragraph (1)(C) thereof)' after `producer'. [<-Struck out]

 [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->] `SEC. 6420. CERTAIN TAXES ON FUELS USED FOR EXEMPT
 PURPOSES. [<-Struck out]

 section, if any fuel on which tax was imposed under section 4041, 4081, or

 [Struck out->]   `(1) NO REFUND OF LEAKING UNDERGROUND STORAGE TANK TRUST

 [Struck out->] but only if such bus is a qualified local bus. [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(D) QUALIFIED LOCAL BUS- For purposes of this paragraph,

 [Struck out->]   `(4) ALCOHOL FUELS-  [<-Struck out]
 [Struck out->]   `(A) IN GENERAL- In the case of a fuel used as described

 the rate of tax taken into account under subsection (a) with respect to
 the fuel so used shall equal the excess of the regular tax rate over the
